117: - `holy_vow`: +armor, +frost resistance, immediate heal
118: - `void_oath`: +weapon damage, +crit chance, -armor tradeoff
119: - Blessings are mutually exclusive: selecting a new blessing replaces the previous one
120:

122: - Some event choices add a timed chapter effect for next 2-3 rooms

Job A：配置与资源检查（Python）\n  - Job B：Godot `--import`、headless 启动、GUT 单测。\n- `README.md` 增加 CI 说明。\n\n三、切入下一高价值任务：敌人对象池化（本范围末的活动实现）\n1) 目标与接入点确认\n- 读取并确认现状：\n  - `ObjectPool` 已服务 projectile/pickup。\n  - `EnemySpawner` 仍 `instantiate()` 直生。\n  - `Enemy` 死亡仍 `queue_free()`。\n  - `GameWorld._clear_active_enemies()` 仍直接销毁。\n- 形成方案：Spawner/Enemy/GameWorld 全链路接池，补充复位与回归测试。\n\n2) 已落代码改动（对象池化主线）\n- `scripts/game/enemy.gd`：\n  - 新增池化状态与模板快照字段：`_pool_active`、`_template_*`。\n  - `_ready()` 改为捕获模板并重置到可复用基线，信号连接去重。\n  - 死亡 `_on_health_died(...)` 改为优先 `ObjectPool.release(\"enemy_basic\", self)`，无池回退 `queue_free()`。\n  - 新增生命周期钩子：`on_pool_acquired()` / `on_pool_released()` / `is_pool_active()`。\n  - 新增重置函数：`_capture_template_state()`、`_reset_for_spawn()`、`_reset_for_pool()`、`_set_pool_active(...)`。\n  - 复用时恢复基础属性/HP/运行态，清理 knockback/dash/ranged cooldown 等残留。\n- `scripts/systems/enemy_spawner.gd`：\n  - 新增 `_ready()` 注册敌人池：`ObjectPool.register_scene(\"enemy_basic\", enemy_scene, ...)`。\n  - 新增 `_acquire_enemy_instance()`：优先池获取，失败回退 instantiate。\n  - `_spawn_enemy()` 与 `_spawn_boss()` 改为通过 `_acquire_enemy_instance()` 生成。\n  - `get_alive_count()` 改为过滤池内/非激活敌人（避免把已回收对象计入活体）。\n- `scripts/game/game_world.gd`：\n  - `_clear_active_enemies()` 改为优先 `ObjectPool.release(\"enemy_basic\", node)`，回退 `queue_free()`。\n\n3) 回归测试与资源清单\n- 新增测试：`test/unit/test_enemy_pooling.gd`\n  - `test_enemy_pool_lifecycle_resets_runtime_state()`：验证 release/acquire 后属性、HP、group、active 状态正确重置。\n  - `test_enemy_died_releases_to_object_pool()`：验证死亡后进入 `ObjectPool` 且 inactive。\n- `scripts/check_resources.py`：新增 required file `test/unit/test_enemy_pooling.gd`。\n\n4) 任务状态更新\n- todo 已更新为：\n  - 对象池接入：completed\n  - Enemy 生命周期与重置：completed\n  - 测试与 check_resources：completed\n  - README 与全量验证：in_progress\n\n四、未完成项（当前活动切片）\n- 仍待完成：\n  - 在 `README.md` 增加“敌人对象池化”与新测试说明；\n  - 执行并回报本轮全量验证（Python/Godot/GUT）是否全绿。\n\n用户意图保持：继续按文档推进开发，且全程中文输出。"

15: - Shop economy assist system (chapter-aware pricing profile, catch-up discount, high-gold markup, escalating restock, chapter-weighted quality/category bias)
16: - Boss progression now follows generated run-plan chapter metadata (default still 15-room MVP pacing)
17: - Boss phase behavior (dash + pulse) driven by HP thresholds
18: - Chapter-based environment hazards (water/spore/lava/ice/void) with status gauges
19: - Hazard visual feedback (chapter tint + damage flash) and boss-room hazard amplification
20: - Meta progression save with run summary rewards
21: - Route-based victory ending unlock and achievement tracking
22: - Run result panel with ending/achievement unlock summary
23: - Main menu meta-upgrade shop (permanent run-start bonuses)
24: - Chapter transition narrative panel after boss rooms (route choice impacts alignment)
25: - Data-driven narrative content config (`data/balance/narrative_content.json`)
26: - Chapter intro panel now follows run-plan intro markers (default 1/5/9/13)
27: - Narrative event rooms (chapter event choices with resource/route consequences)
28: - Narrative choices can attach lasting chapter effects (2-3 rooms of buffs/curses)
29: - Event branch selection now uses weighted routing (alignment + unlocked endings)
30: - Memory fragments unlocked from chapter bosses and tracked in meta save
31: - Safe-camp Memory Altar panel supports in-run fragment review
32: - Blessing system now safely swaps (no unintended stacking from repeated choices)
33: - Run result panel includes a narrative-choice timeline summary
34: - Ending unlock now includes epilogue text (first unlock vs repeat cycle variants)
35: - Main menu memory archive can cycle unlocked fragment full text
36: - Main menu character selection (Knight/Mage/Rogue) with persisted last pick

39: - Character weapon profile is data-driven (single/spread, projectile count, spread angle, random jitter, pierce hits, visual style)
40: - Weapon evolution option now appears in level-up panel when recipe conditions are met (weapon + passive level)
41: - Main menu Codex overlay tracks all categories with catalog progress (locked + unlocked + unlock hints)

57: ```
58: 
59: ## CI (GitHub Actions)
60: 
61: Workflow file: `.github/workflows/ci.yml`
62: 
63: CI jobs:
64: - `validate-config-and-resources`: run `scripts/validate_configs.py` and `scripts/check_resources.py`
65: - `godot-headless-and-gut`: run `godot --import`, headless startup check, and GUT unit tests
66: 
67: Trigger:
68: - push (all branches)
69: - pull_request
70: 
71: Controls:
72: - `WASD` / Arrows: Move
73: - `Shift`: Sprint
74: - `E`: Next room (non-combat rooms / cleared combat rooms)
75: - Shop room: `1/2/3/4` buy slot, `R` restock
76: - Shop room: `T` exchange ore -> gold (limited trades per shop visit)
77: - Shop economy now shifts by chapter (`chapter_1`~`chapter_4`) with per-chapter price/restock/exchange tuning, quality-rate multipliers, and category bias
78: - Elite rooms are generated by run-plan metadata; they use elite-only combat waves and higher pressure
79: - Treasure rooms auto-deploy loot pickups on entry; collect and press `E` to continue
80: - Route branching: after cleared rooms with multiple exits, use `1/2` to select route then `E` to confirm next room
81: - Route style now locks per chapter on first branch choice (`vanguard` / `raider`) and biases event weights, shop economy, hazard intensity, gold/ore drop tendency, route-tint visual feedback, and boss parameter profile (HP/Damage/Speed/Scale/Color)
82: - Level-up panel may show `Evolution: ...` option; selecting it upgrades current weapon profile according to `data/balance/evolutions.json`
83: - Safe camp: `F` damage forge (3 ore), `G` speed forge (5 ore)
84: - Safe camp: `T` open Memory Altar (in-run fragment archive)
85: - Safe camp route: `Q` holy route, `V` void route
86: - Chapter transition panel: `1/2` choose route, `E` confirm continue
87: - Narrative event panel: `1/2` choose event branch, `E` / `Esc` continue
88: - Chapter intro panel: `E` / `Esc` begin chapter
89: - Boss rooms: defeat 1 boss target to unlock doors and progress chapter
90: - Accessory drops: auto-equip up to 2 slots on pickup (extra converts to gold)
91: - Environment gauges: Frostbite/Void Corruption shown on HUD (builds in hazard rooms, decays in shop/camp)
92: - HUD Chapter Effects row: shows active timed effects with icon and remaining rooms (`[+]` boon / `[-]` curse / `[~]` mixed)
93: - HUD Route Style row: shows current style, per-chapter style comparison (`CH1~CH4`), and latest style-lock event
94: - HUD toast notifications for key milestones (achievement, ending, memory fragment, accessory, codex unlock)
95: - HUD minimap now prefers run-plan graph coordinates (`map_x/map_y` + `map_bounds`) for branch-aware layout, with index-grid fallback when coordinates are unavailable; unexplored rooms use `??`
96: - Accessories now include environment resistance bonuses (frost/void mitigation)
97: - `Esc`: Open/close Pause Panel during run
98: - Pause panel: `1` Resume, `2` Retreat (settle run), `3` Main Menu
99: - Pause panel settings subpage: `4` open settings, sliders apply instantly and persist
100: - Settings include Master/BGM/SFX/Ambience volume, Screen Shake strength, UI scale (0.8x-1.5x)
101: - Settings panel supports `Reset Defaults`, and changed values are highlighted in gold
102: - Settings panel includes audio bus meters (Master/BGM/SFX/Ambience) and `Play Test SFX` button
103: - Settings panel now supports input remap (keyboard + gamepad): click `Key`/`Pad` to listen, press target input to bind, `Esc` cancels capture
104: - Input remap has independent `Reset Input Defaults`; while listening, pause/menu close hotkeys are suppressed to prevent accidental panel close
105: - Run result panel: `E` / `Esc` to return menu
106: - Main menu memory archive: click `Review Next Memory Fragment` to cycle unlocked fragments
107: - Main menu ending archive: click `Review Next Ending` to cycle unlocked endings (story + first/repeat epilogue), with faction theme colors (Redeem/Fall/Balance)
108: - Run result panel now includes chapter-effect timeline replay for this run (room, chapter, effect icon, duration) with filter cycling (`ALL/BOON/CURSE/MIXED`, click or key `1`), mode tinting, in-session filter memory, view switch (`FLAT/GROUPED`, click or key `2`), grouped chapter-anchor navigation (`Q/E` or Anchor button), and grouped scope toggle (`ALL CHAPTERS` vs `ANCHOR ONLY`, click or key `3`)
109: - Run result panel now includes route-style evolution summary (chapter comparison + lock trajectory by room/chapter)
110: - Main menu now has a Settings overlay using the same runtime settings data as pause panel
111: - Main menu character switch: `Prev/Next` buttons, selection applies to next run and is saved
112: - Character trait is shown on selection panel and applied at run start before meta upgrades
113: - Main menu Codex: open with `Codex` button; use `Prev/Next` (or keys `1/2`) to browse categories, `Entry Prev/Next` (or keys `3/4`) to inspect entries, `Source/Chapter` filter buttons (or keys `5/6`) to filter statistics, `E/Esc` to close; detail pane shows status/hint/source/time/run index
114: - Codex statistics panel shows per-category completion bars, chapter completion bars (Chapter 1~4 + Global), global completion bar, and most recent 5 unlock records filtered by source/chapter (chapter comes from real unlock context metadata; filters persist across sessions)
115: 
116: Chapter transition blessing effects:
117: - `holy_vow`: +armor, +frost resistance, immediate heal
118: - `void_oath`: +weapon damage, +crit chance, -armor tradeoff
119: - Blessings are mutually exclusive: selecting a new blessing replaces the previous one
120: 
121: Chapter event lasting effects:
122: - Some event choices add a timed chapter effect for next 2-3 rooms
123: - Effects can modify enemy spawn rate/HP/damage, hazard intensity, move speed, damage bonus, and temporary armor delta
124: - Effects are shown in both room status and HUD Chapter Effects row, with remaining room count (`(nR)`)
125: 
126: Meta progression:
127: - Run ends on death / victory / retreat, shows result panel, then returns to menu
128: - Main menu shows meta currency, run stats, and last run reward
129: - Main menu also shows achievement/ending unlock progress and meta upgrades
130: - Main menu now lists unlocked memory fragments

<content>1: extends CharacterBody2D
2: 
3: @export var enemy_id: String = "enemy_shadowling"
4: @export var move_speed: float = 72.0
5: @export var touch_damage: float = 8.0
6: @export var attack_interval: float = 0.7
7: @export var boss_dash_cooldown: float = 4.8
8: @export var boss_pulse_cooldown: float = 5.5
9: 
10: @onready var _health_component: Node = $HealthComponent

13: var _player: CharacterBody2D
14: var _touch_cooldown: float = 0.0
15: var _knockback_velocity: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
16: var _is_boss: bool = false
17: var _phase_thresholds: Array[float] = [1.0, 0.6, 0.3]
18: var _phase_index: int = 0
19: var _phase_speed_mult: float = 1.0
20: var _phase_damage_mult: float = 1.0
21: var _dash_cooldown_timer: float = 0.0
22: var _pulse_cooldown_timer: float = 0.0
23: var _dash_velocity: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
24: var _dash_time: float = 0.0
25: var _base_attack_interval: float = 0.7
26: var _base_scale: Vector2 = Vector2.ONE
27: var _tier: String = "normal"
28: var _archetype: String = "normal"

32: var _ranged_attack_interval: float = 1.2
33: var _ranged_damage_mult: float = 0.82

35: var _base_color: Color = Color(0.83, 0.37, 0.37, 1.0)
36: var _pool_active: bool = true

45: func _ready() -> void:
46:     _capture_template_state()
47:     _set_pool_active(true)
48:     _reset_for_spawn()
49: 
50:     if _health_component != null and _health_component.has_signal("died"):
51:         var callback: Callable = Callable(self, "_on_health_died")
52:         if not _health_component.died.is_connected(callback):
53:             _health_component.died.connect(callback)
54: 
55: 
56: func _physics_process(delta: float) -> void:
57:     if GameManager.current_state != GameManager.GameState.PLAYING:
58:         velocity = Vector2.ZERO
59:         return
60: 
61:     if _touch_cooldown > 0.0:
62:         _touch_cooldown = maxf(0.0, _touch_cooldown - delta)
63:     if _ranged_cooldown > 0.0:
64:         _ranged_cooldown = maxf(0.0, _ranged_cooldown - delta)
65: 
66:     if _player == null or not is_instance_valid(_player):
67:         _player = get_tree().get_first_node_in_group("player") as CharacterBody2D
68: 
69:     if _player == null:
70:         velocity = Vector2.ZERO
71:         return
72: 
73:     var to_player: Vector2 = _player.global_position - global_position
74:     var distance_to_player: float = to_player.length()
75:     var direction: Vector2 = to_player.normalized()
76:     if _is_boss:
77:         _update_phase_by_hp()
78:         _process_boss_skills(delta, direction)
79:     elif _is_ranged:
80:         direction = _get_ranged_direction(direction, distance_to_player)
81:         _process_ranged_attack(distance_to_player)
82: 
83:     velocity = direction * (move_speed * _phase_speed_mult) + _knockback_velocity + _dash_velocity
84:     _knockback_velocity = _knockback_velocity.move_toward(Vector2.ZERO, 780.0 * delta)
85:     _dash_velocity = _dash_velocity.move_toward(Vector2.ZERO, 1200.0 * delta)
86:     _dash_time = maxf(0.0, _dash_time - delta)
87:     move_and_slide()
88: 
89:     var hit_range: float = 22.0
90:     if _is_boss:
91:         hit_range = 34.0
92: 
93:     if _touch_cooldown <= 0.0 and global_position.distance_to(_player.global_position) <= hit_range:
94:         _touch_cooldown = attack_interval
95:         if _player.has_method("apply_damage"):
96:             var impact_damage: float = touch_damage * _phase_damage_mult
97:             if _dash_time > 0.0:
98:                 impact_damage *= 1.35
99:             _player.apply_damage(impact_damage)
100:             if _player.has_method("apply_knockback"):
101:                 var push: Vector2 = (_player.global_position - global_position).normalized()
102:                 _player.apply_knockback(push * (90.0 + 24.0 * _phase_index))
103: 
104: 
105: func apply_damage(
106:     amount: float,
107:     _source: Node = null,
108:     _damage_type: int = 0,
109:     is_crit: bool = false,
110:     knockback: Vector2 = Vector2.ZERO
111: ) -> void:
112:     if _health_component != null and _health_component.has_method("take_damage"):
113:         _health_component.take_damage(amount)
114:     if knockback != Vector2.ZERO:
115:         var knockback_scale: float = 1.0
116:         if _is_boss:
117:             knockback_scale = 0.45
118:         _knockback_velocity += knockback * knockback_scale
119:     _play_hit_feedback(is_crit)
120: 
121: 
122: func _on_health_died(owner_node: Node) -> void:
123:     if owner_node != self:
124:         return
125:     EventBus.enemy_killed.emit(enemy_id, global_position)
126:     if ObjectPool != null:
127:         ObjectPool.release("enemy_basic", self)
128:     else:
129:         queue_free()
130: 
131: 
132: func on_pool_acquired() -> void:
133:     _set_pool_active(true)
134:     _reset_for_spawn()
135: 
136: 
137: func on_pool_released() -> void:
138:     _set_pool_active(false)
139:     _reset_for_pool()
140: 
141: 
142: func is_pool_active() -> bool:
143:     return _pool_active
144: 
145: 
146: func _play_hit_feedback(is_crit: bool) -> void:
147:     if _visual == null:
148:         return
149: 
150:     var flash_color: Color = Color(1.0, 0.46, 0.46, 1.0)
151:     var target_scale: Vector2 = _base_scale * 1.08
152:     if is_crit:
153:         flash_color = Color(1.0, 0.88, 0.36, 1.0)
154:         target_scale = _base_scale * 1.22
155: 
156:     _visual.color = flash_color
157:     scale = target_scale
158: 
159:     var tween: Tween = create_tween()
160:     tween.tween_property(_visual, "color", _base_color, 0.12)
161:     tween.parallel().tween_property(self, "scale", _base_scale, 0.12)
162: 
163: 
164: func set_visual_scale_base(new_scale: Vector2) -> void:
165:     _base_scale = new_scale
166: 
167: 
168: func apply_spawn_profile(profile: Dictionary) -> void:
169:     var new_tier: String = str(profile.get("tier", "normal"))
170:     var new_archetype: String = str(profile.get("archetype", "normal"))
171:     var new_enemy_id: String = str(profile.get("enemy_id", enemy_id))
172: 
173:     if new_enemy_id != "":
174:         enemy_id = new_enemy_id
175: 
176:     _tier = new_tier
177:     _archetype = new_archetype
178:     _is_boss = _tier == "boss" or enemy_id.begins_with("boss_")
179:     _is_ranged = bool(profile.get("ranged", _archetype == "ranged"))
180:     _preferred_range = maxf(80.0, float(profile.get("preferred_range", 170.0)))
181:     _ranged_attack_range = maxf(_preferred_range + 20.0, float(profile.get("ranged_attack_range", 255.0)))
182:     _ranged_attack_interval = clampf(float(profile.get("ranged_attack_interval", 1.2)), 0.35, 4.0)
183:     _ranged_damage_mult = clampf(float(profile.get("ranged_damage_mult", 0.82)), 0.2, 3.0)
184:     _ranged_cooldown = randf_range(0.1, _ranged_attack_interval)
185: 
186:     var base_color_var: Variant = profile.get("base_color", _resolve_default_color())
187:     if base_color_var is Color:
188:         _base_color = base_color_var
189:     else:
190:         _base_color = _resolve_default_color()
191: 
192:     var scale_var: Variant = profile.get("scale", _base_scale)
193:     if scale_var is Vector2:
194:         _base_scale = scale_var
195: 
196:     scale = _base_scale
197:     _base_attack_interval = attack_interval
198:     _apply_visual_defaults()
199: 
200:     if _is_boss:
201:         _load_boss_phase_thresholds()
202:         _phase_index = 0
203:         _apply_phase_stats()
204: 
205: 
206: func _update_phase_by_hp() -> void:
207:     if _health_component == null or _health_component.get("max_hp") == null:
208:         return
209: 
210:     var max_hp_value: float = float(_health_component.max_hp)
211:     if max_hp_value <= 0.0:
212:         return
213: 
214:     var hp_ratio: float = clampf(float(_health_component.current_hp) / max_hp_value, 0.0, 1.0)
215:     var new_phase: int = 0
216:     for i in range(1, _phase_thresholds.size()):
217:         if hp_ratio <= _phase_thresholds[i]:
218:             new_phase = i
219: 
220:     if new_phase == _phase_index:
221:         return
222: 
223:     _phase_index = new_phase
224:     _apply_phase_stats()
225: 
226: 
227: func _apply_phase_stats() -> void:
228:     _phase_speed_mult = 1.0 + 0.12 * _phase_index
229:     _phase_damage_mult = 1.0 + 0.22 * _phase_index
230:     attack_interval = maxf(0.24, _base_attack_interval * (1.0 - 0.12 * _phase_index))
231: 
232: 
233: func _process_boss_skills(delta: float, direction: Vector2) -> void:
234:     _dash_cooldown_timer -= delta
235:     _pulse_cooldown_timer -= delta
236: 
237:     if _dash_cooldown_timer <= 0.0:
238:         _dash_cooldown_timer = maxf(1.5, boss_dash_cooldown - 0.55 * _phase_index)
239:         _dash_time = 0.42
240:         _dash_velocity = direction * (300.0 + 80.0 * _phase_index)
241: 
242:     if _pulse_cooldown_timer <= 0.0:
243:         _pulse_cooldown_timer = maxf(2.0, boss_pulse_cooldown - 0.45 * _phase_index)
244:         _cast_phase_pulse()
245: 
246: 
247: func _cast_phase_pulse() -> void:
248:     if _player == null:
249:         return
250: 
251:     var radius: float = 190.0 + 28.0 * _phase_index
252:     var distance: float = global_position.distance_to(_player.global_position)
253:     if distance > radius:
254:         return
255: 
256:     var pulse_damage: float = touch_damage * (0.7 + 0.4 * _phase_index)
257:     if _player.has_method("apply_damage"):
258:         _player.apply_damage(pulse_damage)
259:     if _player.has_method("apply_knockback"):
260:         var push: Vector2 = (_player.global_position - global_position).normalized()
261:         if push == Vector2.ZERO:
262:             push = Vector2.RIGHT
263:         _player.apply_knockback(push * (110.0 + 30.0 * _phase_index))
264: 
265:     if _visual != null:
266:         var pulse_tween: Tween = create_tween()
267:         pulse_tween.tween_property(_visual, "color", Color(1.0, 0.78, 0.34, 1.0), 0.08)
268:         pulse_tween.tween_property(_visual, "color", _base_color, 0.12)
269: 
270: 
271: func _load_boss_phase_thresholds() -> void:
272:     var config: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("boss_phases", {})
273:     var bosses_var: Variant = config.get("bosses", {})
274:     if not (bosses_var is Dictionary):
275:         return
276: 
277:     var bosses: Dictionary = bosses_var
278:     var phase_key: String = enemy_id
279:     if enemy_id.begins_with("boss_"):
280:         phase_key = "enemy_%s" % enemy_id.trim_prefix("boss_")
281: 
282:     var thresholds_var: Variant = bosses.get(phase_key, [])
283:     if not (thresholds_var is Array):
284:         return
285: 
286:     var parsed: Array[float] = []
287:     for value: Variant in thresholds_var:
288:         parsed.append(clampf(float(value), 0.0, 1.0))
289:     if parsed.size() >= 2:
290:         _phase_thresholds = parsed
291: 
292: 
293: func _get_ranged_direction(direction_to_player: Vector2, distance_to_player: float) -> Vector2:
294:     if distance_to_player > _preferred_range + 28.0:
295:         return direction_to_player
296:     if distance_to_player < _preferred_range - 24.0:
297:         return -direction_to_player
298: 
299:     var strafe: Vector2 = Vector2(-direction_to_player.y, direction_to_player.x)
300:     if strafe == Vector2.ZERO:
301:         strafe = Vector2.RIGHT
302:     var sign_value: float = 1.0
303:     if int(Time.get_ticks_msec() / 550) % 2 == 0:
304:         sign_value = -1.0
305:     return strafe * sign_value
306: 
307: 
308: func _process_ranged_attack(distance_to_player: float) -> void:
309:     if _player == null:
310:         return
311:     if distance_to_player > _ranged_attack_range:
312:         return
313:     if _ranged_cooldown > 0.0:
314:         return
315: 
316:     _ranged_cooldown = _ranged_attack_interval
317:     var damage: float = touch_damage * _phase_damage_mult * _ranged_damage_mult
318:     if _player.has_method("apply_damage"):
319:         _player.apply_damage(damage)
320:     if _player.has_method("apply_knockback"):
321:         var push: Vector2 = (_player.global_position - global_position).normalized()
322:         if push == Vector2.ZERO:
323:             push = Vector2.RIGHT
324:         _player.apply_knockback(push * 38.0)
325: 
326:     if _visual != null:
327:         var pulse_tween: Tween = create_tween()
328:         pulse_tween.tween_property(_visual, "color", Color(1.0, 0.9, 0.4, 1.0), 0.06)
329:         pulse_tween.tween_property(_visual, "color", _base_color, 0.1)
330: 
331: 
332: func _resolve_default_color() -> Color:
333:     if enemy_id.begins_with("boss_"):
334:         return Color(0.95, 0.45, 0.2, 1.0)
335:     if enemy_id.begins_with("elite_"):
336:         return Color(0.98, 0.84, 0.3, 1.0)
337:     if enemy_id.find("stalker") >= 0:
338:         return Color(0.78, 0.52, 0.96, 1.0)
339:     if enemy_id.find("brute") >= 0:
340:         return Color(0.55, 0.78, 0.72, 1.0)
341:     if enemy_id.find("hexcaster") >= 0:
342:         return Color(0.92, 0.62, 0.38, 1.0)
343:     return Color(0.83, 0.37, 0.37, 1.0)
344: 
345: 
346: func _apply_visual_defaults() -> void:
347:     if _visual != null:
348:         _visual.color = _base_color
349:         if _tier == "elite":
350:             _visual.color = _base_color.lightened(0.12)
351: 
352: 
353: func _capture_template_state() -> void:
354:     _template_enemy_id = enemy_id
355:     _template_move_speed = move_speed
356:     _template_touch_damage = touch_damage
357:     _template_attack_interval = attack_interval

359:     if _health_component != null and _health_component.get("max_hp") != null:
360:         _template_max_hp = float(_health_component.max_hp)
361:

335: func _get_spawn_interval() -> float:
336:     var floor_ratio: float = 1.0 + float(floor_index - 1) * 0.09
337:     var time_ratio: float = 1.0
338:     if _room_time > 120.0:
339:         time_ratio = 1.8
340:     elif _room_time > 60.0:
341:         time_ratio = 1.5
342:     elif _room_time > 30.0:
343:         time_ratio = 1.25
344: 
345:     var interval: float = 1.3 / (floor_ratio * time_ratio * _runtime_spawn_rate_mult)
346:     if _combat_mode == "elite":

348:     return clampf(interval, 0.2, 1.3)

360:     for item: Variant in brackets:

362:             continue
363:         var row: Dictionary = item

1206:     var rows: Array[String] = []
1207:     for item: Variant in _chapter_effects_this_room:
1208:         if not (item is Dictionary):
1209:             continue
1210:         var row: Dictionary = item
1211:         rows.append("%s %s(%d)" % [
1212:             str(row.get("icon", "[~]")),
1213:             str(row.get("title", "Effect")),
1214:             int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 1))
1215:         ])

1218:     return ", ".join(PackedStringArray(rows))

1222:     if _active_chapter_effects.is_empty():
1223:         return "none"

1239:         return "none"

1243: func _get_chapter_effect_icon(effects: Dictionary) -> String:
1244:     var score: float = _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(effects)
1245:     if score >= 0.25:
1246:         return "[+]"
1247:     if score <= -0.25:
1248:         return "[-]"
1249:     return "[~]"

1252: func _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(effects: Dictionary) -> float:
1253:     if effects.is_empty():
1254:         return 0.0
1255: 
1256:     var score: float = 0.0
1257:     score += float(effects.get("damage_bonus_pct", 0.0)) * 1.0
1258:     score += float(effects.get("armor_bonus", 0.0)) * 1.2
1259: 
1260:     var move_mult: float = float(effects.get("move_speed_mult", 1.0))
1261:     score += (move_mult - 1.0) * 1.4
1262: 
1263:     var spawn_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_spawn_rate_mult", 1.0))
1264:     score += (1.0 - spawn_mult) * 0.9
1265: 
1266:     var hp_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_hp_mult", 1.0))
1267:     score += (1.0 - hp_mult) * 0.9
1268: 
1269:     var dmg_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_damage_mult", 1.0))
1270:     score += (1.0 - dmg_mult) * 1.1
1271: 
1272:     var hazard_mult: float = float(effects.get("hazard_intensity_mult", 1.0))
1273:     score += (1.0 - hazard_mult) * 1.1
1274:     return score

143: func _ready() -> void:
144:     add_to_group("game_world")
145:     randomize()
146:     if pickup_scene == null:
147:         pickup_scene = load("res://scenes/game/pickup.tscn")
148:     if pickup_scene != null and ObjectPool != null:
149:         ObjectPool.register_scene("pickup_basic", pickup_scene, 32)
150: 
151:     _load_shop_economy_config()
152:     _build_run_plan()
153:     _run_kills = 0
154:     _run_rooms_cleared = 0
155:     _run_finished = false
156:     _returning_to_menu = false
157:     _chapter_intro_pending = false
158:     _narrative_event_pending = false
159:     _chapter_transition_pending = false
160:     _memory_altar_pending = false
161:     _pause_menu_pending = false
162:     _shown_chapter_intro = {}
163:     _active_blessing_id = "none"
164:     _chapter_effect_timeline.clear()
165:     _active_chapter_effects.clear()
166:     _chapter_effects_this_room.clear()
167:     _chapter_effect_applied_armor_bonus = 0.0
168:     _room_history.clear()
169:     _pending_next_rooms.clear()
170:     _selected_next_room_slot = 0
171:     _chapter_route_styles.clear()
172:     _current_route_style = "neutral"
173:     _route_event_weight_mult = 1.0
174:     _route_hazard_mult = 1.0
175:     _route_gold_drop_mult = 1.0
176:     _route_ore_drop_mult = 1.0
177:     _route_theme_tint = Color(0.18, 0.34, 0.50, 1.0)
178:     _route_theme_blend = 0.0
179:     _route_boss_style_profile = {}
180:     _route_style_timeline.clear()
181:     _load_route_style_profiles()
182:     _room_index = _get_run_start_room()
183: 
184:     GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.PLAYING)
185:     EventBus.enemy_killed.connect(_on_enemy_killed)
186:     EventBus.player_died.connect(_on_player_died)
187:     EventBus.gold_changed.emit(_gold)
188:     EventBus.ore_changed.emit(_ore)
189:     EventBus.route_changed.emit(_alignment)
190:     EventBus.frostbite_changed.emit(_frostbite)
191:     EventBus.void_corruption_changed.emit(_void_corruption)
192:     _apply_selected_character_profile()
193:     _apply_meta_upgrades()
194:     if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("reset_run_choices"):
195:         _narrative_system.reset_run_choices()
196:     if _narrative_event_panel != null and _narrative_event_panel.has_signal("event_choice_committed"):
197:         _narrative_event_panel.event_choice_committed.connect(_on_event_choice_committed)
198:     if _narrative_event_panel != null and _narrative_event_panel.has_signal("event_closed"):
199:         _narrative_event_panel.event_closed.connect(_on_event_closed)
200:     if _chapter_intro_panel != null and _chapter_intro_panel.has_signal("intro_closed"):
201:         _chapter_intro_panel.intro_closed.connect(_on_intro_closed)
202:     if _chapter_transition_panel != null and _chapter_transition_panel.has_signal("choice_committed"):
203:         _chapter_transition_panel.choice_committed.connect(_on_transition_choice_committed)
204:     if _chapter_transition_panel != null and _chapter_transition_panel.has_signal("transition_closed"):
205:         _chapter_transition_panel.transition_closed.connect(_on_transition_closed)
206:     if _memory_altar_panel != null and _memory_altar_panel.has_signal("altar_closed"):
207:         _memory_altar_panel.altar_closed.connect(_on_memory_altar_closed)
208:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_signal("resume_requested"):
209:         _pause_panel.resume_requested.connect(_on_pause_resume_requested)
210:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_signal("retreat_requested"):
211:         _pause_panel.retreat_requested.connect(_on_pause_retreat_requested)
212:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_signal("quit_to_menu_requested"):
213:         _pause_panel.quit_to_menu_requested.connect(_on_pause_quit_to_menu_requested)
214:     if _run_result_panel != null and _run_result_panel.has_signal("back_to_menu_requested"):
215:         _run_result_panel.back_to_menu_requested.connect(_on_run_result_back_to_menu)
216:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_method("close_panel"):
217:         _pause_panel.close_panel()
218:     get_tree().paused = false
219:     _start_room()
220: 
221: 
222: func _process(delta: float) -> void:
223:     if _room_active and (_current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT or _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_ELITE or _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS) and _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("get_room_time"):
224:         _room_timer_label.text = "%.1f s" % _spawner.get_room_time()
225:     elif not _room_active:
226:         _room_timer_label.text = "-"
227: 
228:     _room_kill_label.text = "%d / %d" % [_kills_in_room, _required_kills]
229:     _process_environment_hazards(delta)
230:     _update_environment_visuals(delta)
231: 
232: 
233: func _unhandled_input(event: InputEvent) -> void:
234:     if event.is_action_pressed("pause"):
235:         if _chapter_intro_pending or _narrative_event_pending or _chapter_transition_pending or _memory_altar_pending:
236:             return
237: 
238:         if _pause_menu_pending:
239:             _close_pause_panel()
240:             return
241: 
242:         if GameManager.current_state == GameManager.GameState.PLAYING and not _run_finished:
243:             _open_pause_panel()
244:         elif _run_finished:
245:             SceneManager.go_to_main_menu()
246:         return
247: 
248:     if GameManager.current_state != GameManager.GameState.PLAYING:
249:         return
250: 
251:     if _chapter_intro_pending:
252:         return
253: 
254:     if _narrative_event_pending:
255:         return
256: 
257:     if _chapter_transition_pending:
258:         return
259: 
260:     if _memory_altar_pending:
261:         return
262: 
263:     if _pause_menu_pending:
264:         return
265: 
266:     if not _room_active and _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SHOP:
267:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_buy_1"):
268:             _try_buy_shop_slot(0)
269:             return
270:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_buy_2"):
271:             _try_buy_shop_slot(1)
272:             return
273:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_buy_3"):
274:             _try_buy_shop_slot(2)
275:             return
276:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_buy_4"):
277:             _try_buy_shop_slot(3)
278:             return
279:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_restock"):
280:             _try_restock_shop()
281:             return
282:         if event.is_action_pressed("shop_exchange_ore"):
283:             _try_exchange_ore_for_gold()
284:             return
285: 
286:     if not _room_active and _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SAFE_CAMP:
287:         if event.is_action_pressed("camp_forge_damage"):
288:             _try_forge_damage()
289:             return
290:         if event.is_action_pressed("camp_forge_speed"):
291:             _try_forge_speed()
292:             return
293:         if event.is_action_pressed("camp_memory_altar"):
294:             _open_memory_altar()
295:             return
296:         if event.is_action_pressed("camp_route_holy"):
297:             _try_route_choice("holy")
298:             return
299:         if event.is_action_pressed("camp_route_void"):
300:             _try_route_choice("void")
301:             return
302: 
303:     if not _room_active and _pending_next_rooms.size() > 1:
304:         if event.is_action_pressed("narrative_choice_1"):
305:             _selected_next_room_slot = 0
306:             _refresh_idle_route_prompt()
307:             return
308:         if event.is_action_pressed("narrative_choice_2"):
309:             _selected_next_room_slot = mini(1, _pending_next_rooms.size() - 1)
310:             _refresh_idle_route_prompt()
311:             return
312: 
313:     if event.is_action_pressed("interact") and not _room_active:
314:         _advance_to_next_room()
315: 
316:

318:     return "%d / %d" % [_kills_in_room, _required_kills]
319:

341: func get_accessories_text() -> String:

360: 
361: func get_chapter_effects_hud_text() -> String:
362:     if _chapter_effects_this_room.is_empty():
363:         return "-"
364: 
365:     var rows: Array[String] = []
366:     for item: Variant in _chapter_effects_this_room:
367:         if not (item is Dictionary):
368:             continue
369:         var row: Dictionary = item
370:         rows.append("%s %s (%dR)" % [
371:             str(row.get("icon", "[~]")),
372:             str(row.get("title", "Effect")),
373:             int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 1))
374:         ])
375: 
376:     if rows.is_empty():
377:         return "-"
378:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
379: 
380: 
381: func get_route_style_hud_text() -> String:
382:     var rows: Array[String] = []
383:     rows.append("Current: %s" % _get_route_style_label())
384: 
385:     var chapter_rows: Array[String] = []
386:     for idx in range(1, 5):
387:         var chapter_id: String = "chapter_%d" % idx
388:         var style_id: String = str(_chapter_route_styles.get(chapter_id, "neutral"))
389:         chapter_rows.append("CH%d:%s" % [idx, _get_route_style_label(style_id)])
390:     rows.append(" | ".join(PackedStringArray(chapter_rows)))
391: 
392:     if not _route_style_timeline.is_empty():
393:         var latest: Dictionary = _route_style_timeline[_route_style_timeline.size() - 1]
394:         rows.append("Latest lock: R%d %s -> %s" % [
395:             int(latest.get("room_index", _room_index)),
396:             str(latest.get("chapter_id", "chapter")),
397:             _get_route_style_label(str(latest.get("style_id", "neutral")))
398:         ])
399: 
400:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
401: 
402: 
403: func get_minimap_text() -> String:
404:     var coordinate_lookup: Dictionary = _build_minimap_coordinate_lookup()
405:     if not coordinate_lookup.is_empty():
406:         var bounds: Dictionary = _get_minimap_bounds()
407:         var min_x: int = int(bounds.get("min_x", 0))
408:         var max_x: int = int(bounds.get("max_x", 0))
409:         var min_y: int = int(bounds.get("min_y", 0))
410:         var max_y: int = int(bounds.get("max_y", 0))
411: 
412:         var coord_rows: Array[String] = []
413:         for map_y in range(min_y, max_y + 1):
414:             var parts: Array[String] = []
415:             for map_x in range(min_x, max_x + 1):
416:                 var coord_key: String = "%d:%d" % [map_x, map_y]
417:                 if not coordinate_lookup.has(coord_key):
418:                     parts.append("----")
419:                     continue
420: 
421:                 var room_id: int = int(coordinate_lookup.get(coord_key, 0))
422:                 parts.append(_build_minimap_room_token(room_id))
423:             coord_rows.append(" ".join(PackedStringArray(parts)))
424:         return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(coord_rows))
425: 
426:     return _build_minimap_index_grid()
427: 
428: 
429: func _build_minimap_index_grid() -> String:
430:     var room_count: int = _get_run_room_count()
431:     var cols: int = _get_run_layout_cols()
432:     var rows_count: int = int(ceil(float(room_count) / float(cols)))
433:     var rows: Array[String] = []
434:     for row_index in range(rows_count):
435:         var parts: Array[String] = []
436:         for col_index in range(cols):
437:             var room_id: int = row_index * cols + col_index + 1
438:             if room_id > room_count:
439:                 parts.append("----")
440:             else:
441:                 parts.append(_build_minimap_room_token(room_id))
442:         rows.append(" ".join(PackedStringArray(parts)))
443:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
444: 
445: 
446: func _build_minimap_coordinate_lookup() -> Dictionary:
447:     var lookup: Dictionary = {}
448:     for room_id_var: Variant in _room_plan_map.keys():
449:         var room_id: int = int(room_id_var)
450:         var row_var: Variant = _room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
451:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
452:             continue
453:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
454:         if not row.has("map_x") or not row.has("map_y"):
455:             continue
456:         var key: String = "%d:%d" % [int(row.get("map_x", 0)), int(row.get("map_y", 0))]
457:         lookup[key] = room_id
458:     return lookup
459: 
460: 
461: func _get_minimap_bounds() -> Dictionary:
462:     if not _run_map_bounds.is_empty():
463:         return _run_map_bounds
464: 
465:     var has_any: bool = false
466:     var min_x: int = 0
467:     var max_x: int = 0
468:     var min_y: int = 0
469:     var max_y: int = 0
470:     for row_var: Variant in _room_plan_map.values():
471:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
472:             continue
473:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
474:         if not row.has("map_x") or not row.has("map_y"):
475:             continue
476:         var map_x: int = int(row.get("map_x", 0))
477:         var map_y: int = int(row.get("map_y", 0))
478:         if not has_any:
479:             min_x = map_x
480:             max_x = map_x
481:             min_y = map_y
482:             max_y = map_y
483:             has_any = true
484:         else:
485:             min_x = mini(min_x, map_x)
486:             max_x = maxi(max_x, map_x)
487:             min_y = mini(min_y, map_y)
488:             max_y = maxi(max_y, map_y)
489: 
490:     if has_any:
491:         return {
492:             "min_x": min_x,
493:             "max_x": max_x,
494:             "min_y": min_y,
495:             "max_y": max_y,
496:             "cols": max_x - min_x + 1,
497:             "rows": max_y - min_y + 1
498:         }
499: 
500:     var cols: int = _get_run_layout_cols()
501:     var rows_count: int = int(ceil(float(_get_run_room_count()) / float(cols)))
502:     return {
503:         "min_x": 0,
504:         "max_x": cols - 1,
505:         "min_y": 0,
506:         "max_y": maxi(0, rows_count - 1),
507:         "cols": cols,
508:         "rows": rows_count
509:     }
510: 
511: 
512: func _build_minimap_room_token(room_id: int) -> String:
513:     if not _room_history.has(room_id):
514:         return "??"
515: 
516:     var row_var: Variant = _room_history.get(room_id, {})
517:     if not (row_var is Dictionary):
518:         return "??"
519: 
520:     var row: Dictionary = row_var
521:     var room_type: String = str(row.get("type", ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT))
522:     var completed: bool = bool(row.get("completed", false))
523:     var marker: String = _room_type_to_minimap_marker(room_type)
524:     if completed:
525:         marker = marker.to_lower()
526: 
527:     var token: String = "%02d%s" % [room_id, marker]
528:     if room_id == _room_index and not _run_finished:
529:         return ">%s<" % token
530:     return token
531: 
532: 
533: func _room_type_to_minimap_marker(room_type: String) -> String:
534:     match room_type:
535:         ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
536:             return "B"
537:         ROOM_TYPE_EVENT:
538:             return "E"
539:         ROOM_TYPE_SHOP:
540:             return "S"
541:         ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE:
542:             return "T"
543:         ROOM_TYPE_SAFE_CAMP:
544:             return "H"
545:         ROOM_TYPE_ELITE:
546:             return "L"
547:         _:
548:             return "C"
549: 
550: 
551: func _ensure_room_history(index: int, room_type: String) -> void:
552:     _room_history[index] = {
553:         "type": room_type,
554:         "completed": bool((_room_history.get(index, {}) as Dictionary).get("completed", false))
555:     }
556: 
557: 
558: func _mark_room_completed(index: int) -> void:
559:     if not _room_history.has(index):
560:         return
561:     var row_var: Variant = _room_history.get(index, {})
562:     if row_var is Dictionary:
563:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
564:         row["completed"] = true
565:         _room_history[index] = row
566: 
567: 
568: func _start_room() -> void:
569:     if _room_index > _get_run_room_count():
570:         _finish_run("victory")
571:         return
572: 
573:     _clear_active_enemies()
574:     _clear_active_pickups()
575:     _chapter_intro_pending = false
576:     _narrative_event_pending = false
577:     _chapter_transition_pending = false
578:     _memory_altar_pending = false
579:     _pause_menu_pending = false
580:     _pending_next_rooms.clear()
581:     _selected_next_room_slot = 0
582:     _current_room_type = _resolve_room_type(_room_index)
583:     _sync_route_style_for_room(_room_index)
584:     if GameManager != null and GameManager.has_method("set_run_context"):
585:         GameManager.set_run_context(_room_index, _current_room_type, _get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index))
586:     _ensure_room_history(_room_index, _current_room_type)
587:     _active_hazards = _get_hazards_for_room(_room_index)
588:     _advance_chapter_effects_for_room()
589:     _apply_room_theme(_room_index)
590: 
591:     _kills_in_room = 0
592:     _required_kills = 0
593:     _hazard_tick_timer = 0.0
594:     EventBus.room_entered.emit("room_%d" % _room_index, _current_room_type)
595: 
596:     if _should_show_chapter_intro(_room_index):
597:         _show_chapter_intro(_room_index)
598:         return
599: 
600:     _enter_current_room_type()
601: 
602: 
603: func _enter_current_room_type() -> void:
604:     if _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT:
605:         _enter_combat_room()
606:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_ELITE:
607:         _enter_elite_room()
608:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
609:         _enter_boss_room()
610:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_EVENT:
611:         _enter_event_room()
612:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SHOP:
613:         _enter_shop_room()
614:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE:
615:         _enter_treasure_room()
616:     else:
617:         _enter_safe_camp_room()
618: 
619: 
620: func _should_show_chapter_intro(index: int) -> bool:
621:     var room_plan: Dictionary = _get_room_plan(index)
622:     if room_plan.is_empty():
623:         return false
624:     if not bool(room_plan.get("show_intro", false)):
625:         return false
626:     var chapter_key: String = str(room_plan.get("chapter_id", _get_chapter_id_for_room(index)))
627:     return not bool(_shown_chapter_intro.get(chapter_key, false))
628: 
629: 
630: func _show_chapter_intro(index: int) -> void:
631:     _room_active = false
632:     _chapter_intro_pending = true
633:     _set_doors_locked(false)
634:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
635:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
636: 
637:     _room_timer_label.text = "-"
638:     _room_status_label.text = "Chapter briefing..."
639: 
640:     var chapter_index: int = _get_chapter_index_for_room(index)
641:     if _chapter_intro_panel != null and _chapter_intro_panel.has_method("show_intro"):
642:         _chapter_intro_panel.show_intro(chapter_index, get_active_hazards_text(), _get_active_blessing_text())
643: 
644: 
645: func _on_intro_closed() -> void:
646:     _chapter_intro_pending = false
647:     _shown_chapter_intro[_get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index)] = true
648:     _enter_current_room_type()
649: 
650: 
651: func _enter_combat_room() -> void:
652:     _required_kills = 10 + _room_index * 3
653:     _room_active = true
654:     _room_timer_label.text = "0.0 s"
655:     _room_status_label.text = "Combat Room %d: Defeat %d enemies | Hazards: %s | Effects: %s" % [
656:         _room_index,
657:         _required_kills,
658:         get_active_hazards_text(),
659:         _get_active_chapter_effects_text()
660:     ]
661:     _room_status_label.text += " | Style: %s" % _get_route_style_label()
662:     _set_doors_locked(true)
663: 
664:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("start_room_combat"):
665:         _spawner.start_room_combat(_room_index, "normal")
666: 
667: 
668: func _enter_elite_room() -> void:
669:     _required_kills = 6 + _room_index * 2
670:     _room_active = true
671:     _room_timer_label.text = "0.0 s"
672:     _room_status_label.text = "Elite Room %d: Eliminate %d elites | Hazards: %s | Effects: %s" % [
673:         _room_index,
674:         _required_kills,
675:         get_active_hazards_text(),
676:         _get_active_chapter_effects_text()
677:     ]
678:     _room_status_label.text += " | Style: %s" % _get_route_style_label()
679:     _set_doors_locked(true)
680: 
681:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("start_room_combat"):
682:         _spawner.start_room_combat(_room_index, "elite")
683: 
684: 
685: func _enter_boss_room() -> void:
686:     _required_kills = 1
687:     _room_active = true
688:     _room_timer_label.text = "0.0 s"
689:     var boss_id: String = _get_boss_id_for_room(_room_index)
690:     _room_status_label.text = "Boss Room %d: Defeat %s | Hazards: %s | Effects: %s" % [
691:         _room_index,
692:         _get_boss_title(boss_id),
693:         get_active_hazards_text(),
694:         _get_active_chapter_effects_text()
695:     ]
696:     _room_status_label.text += " | Style: %s" % _get_route_style_label()
697:     _set_doors_locked(true)
698: 
699:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("start_room_combat"):
700:         _spawner.start_room_combat(_room_index, "boss", boss_id, _route_boss_style_profile)
701: 
702: 
703: func _enter_shop_room() -> void:
704:     _room_active = false
705:     _set_doors_locked(false)
706:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
707:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
708: 
709:     _apply_shop_chapter_profile(_get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index))
710: 
711:     _set_frostbite(maxf(0.0, _frostbite - 18.0))
712:     _set_void_corruption(maxf(0.0, _void_corruption - 14.0))
713: 
714:     _shop_restock_count = 0
715:     _shop_ore_exchange_count = 0
716:     _shop_restock_cost = _shop_restock_base_cost
717:     _shop_offers = _build_shop_offers()
718:     _prepare_next_room_candidates()
719:     _shop_message = "Shop refreshed. Buy with 1-4."
720:     _update_shop_text()
721: 
722: 
723: func _enter_treasure_room() -> void:
724:     _room_active = false
725:     _set_doors_locked(false)
726:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
727:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
728: 
729:     _room_timer_label.text = "-"
730:     _prepare_next_room_candidates()
731: 
732:     var player_pos: Vector2 = _player.global_position if _player != null else global_position
733:     var gold_reward: int = _scale_drop_amount(32 + _room_index * 2, _route_gold_drop_mult)
734:     var ore_reward: int = _scale_drop_amount(1 + int((_room_index + 1) / 5), _route_ore_drop_mult)
735:     _spawn_direct_pickup("gold", gold_reward, "treasure_gold", player_pos + Vector2(-18.0, -8.0))
736:     _spawn_direct_pickup("ore", ore_reward, "treasure_ore", player_pos + Vector2(18.0, -10.0))
737: 
738:     var accessory_chance: float = 0.28
739:     if _current_route_style == "vanguard":
740:         accessory_chance = 0.34
741:     elif _current_route_style == "raider":
742:         accessory_chance = 0.24
743: 
744:     var accessory_note: String = ""
745:     if randf() <= accessory_chance:
746:         _spawn_direct_pickup("accessory", 1, "accessory_drop", player_pos + Vector2(0.0, 10.0))
747:         accessory_note = " + accessory cache"
748: 
749:     _room_status_label.text = "Treasure Room %d: Loot deployed (Gold +%d, Ore +%d%s) | Style: %s\n%s" % [
750:         _room_index,
751:         gold_reward,
752:         ore_reward,
753:         accessory_note,
754:         _get_route_style_label(),
755:         _get_next_route_hint_text()
756:     ]
757: 
758: 
759: func _enter_event_room() -> void:
760:     _room_active = false
761:     _narrative_event_pending = false
762:     _set_doors_locked(false)
763:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
764:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
765: 
766:     var chapter_index: int = _get_chapter_index_for_room(_room_index)
767:     var event_data: Dictionary = {}
768:     if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("get_chapter_event"):
769:         event_data = _narrative_system.get_chapter_event(chapter_index, _alignment, _current_route_style, _route_event_weight_mult)
770: 
771:     if event_data.is_empty():
772:         _room_status_label.text = "Event Room: no event data. Press E for next room"
773:         return
774: 
775:     _room_timer_label.text = "-"
776:     _prepare_next_room_candidates()
777:     _room_status_label.text = "Event Room: choose your path | Effects: %s | Style: %s" % [_get_active_chapter_effects_text(), _get_route_style_label()]
778:     _narrative_event_pending = true
779:     if _narrative_event_panel != null and _narrative_event_panel.has_method("show_event_panel"):
780:         _narrative_event_panel.show_event_panel(event_data, _alignment)
781: 
782: 
783: func _enter_safe_camp_room() -> void:
784:     _room_active = false
785:     _set_doors_locked(false)
786:     _camp_route_chosen = false
787:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
788:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
789: 
790:     var health_component: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("HealthComponent")
791:     if health_component != null and health_component.has_method("heal"):
792:         health_component.heal(25.0)
793: 
794:     var stats: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("StatsComponent")
795:     if stats != null and stats.get("stamina_max") != null:
796:         stats.current_stamina = stats.stamina_max
797: 
798:     _set_frostbite(maxf(0.0, _frostbite - 45.0))
799:     _set_void_corruption(maxf(0.0, _void_corruption - 40.0))
800: 
801:     _prepare_next_room_candidates()
802:     _camp_message = "Recovered: +25 HP, stamina refilled"
803:     _update_camp_text()
804: 
805: 
806: func _on_enemy_killed(_enemy_id: String, _position: Vector2) -> void:
807:     _run_kills += 1
808:     var drop_table_id: String = _resolve_drop_table_for_enemy(_enemy_id)
809:     _spawn_drops(_position, drop_table_id)
810: 
811:     if not _room_active:
812:         return
813: 
814:     if _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT and _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_ELITE and _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
815:         return
816: 
817:     _kills_in_room += 1
818: 
819:     if _kills_in_room >= _required_kills:
820:         call_deferred("_try_clear_room")
821: 
822: 
823: func _try_clear_room() -> void:
824:     if _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT and _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_ELITE and _current_room_type != ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
825:         return
826: 
827:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("get_alive_count"):
828:         if _spawner.get_alive_count() > 0:
829:             return
830: 
831:     _room_active = false
832:     _run_rooms_cleared += 1
833:     _mark_room_completed(_room_index)
834:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
835:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
836: 
837:     EventBus.room_cleared.emit("room_%d" % _room_index)
838:     _set_doors_locked(false)
839:     var next_rooms: Array[int] = _prepare_next_room_candidates()
840:     if _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
841:         if next_rooms.is_empty():
842:             _finish_run("victory")
843:             return
844:         var chapter: int = _get_chapter_index_for_room(_room_index)
845:         EventBus.memory_fragment_found.emit("memory_ch%d_boss" % chapter)
846:         _begin_chapter_transition(chapter)
847:     else:
848:         if next_rooms.is_empty():
849:             _finish_run("victory")
850:             return
851:         _room_status_label.text = "Room Cleared! %s" % _get_next_route_hint_text()
852: 
853: 
854: func _on_player_died(_reason: String) -> void:
855:     _finish_run("death")
856: 
857: 
858: func _finish_run(outcome: String) -> void:
859:     if _run_finished:
860:         return
861:     _run_finished = true
862:     _reset_pause_state()
863: 
864:     GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.GAME_OVER)
865:     _room_active = false
866:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
867:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
868: 
869:     var level_reached: int = 1
870:     var progression: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("ProgressionComponent")
871:     if progression != null and progression.get("current_level") != null:
872:         level_reached = int(progression.current_level)
873: 
874:     var run_result: Dictionary = SaveManager.submit_run_result({
875:         "outcome": outcome,
876:         "rooms_cleared": _run_rooms_cleared,
877:         "kills": _run_kills,
878:         "level_reached": level_reached,
879:         "gold": _gold,
880:         "ore": _ore,
881:         "alignment": _alignment,
882:         "narrative_choices": _narrative_system.get_run_choices() if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("get_run_choices") else [],
883:         "chapter_effect_timeline": _chapter_effect_timeline.duplicate(true),
884:         "chapter_route_styles": _chapter_route_styles.duplicate(true),
885:         "route_style_timeline": _route_style_timeline.duplicate(true)
886:     })
887: 
888:     _room_status_label.text = "Run Ended: %s | Meta +%d" % [
889:         outcome.to_upper(),
890:         int(run_result.get("meta_reward", 0))
891:     ]
892: 
893:     if _run_result_panel != null and _run_result_panel.has_method("show_result"):
894:         _run_result_panel.show_result(run_result)
895:     else:
896:         call_deferred("_return_to_main_menu")
897: 
898: 
899: func _return_to_main_menu() -> void:
900:     if _returning_to_menu:
901:         return
902:     _returning_to_menu = true
903:     GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.MENU)
904:     SceneManager.go_to_main_menu()
905: 
906: 
907: func _on_run_result_back_to_menu() -> void:
908:     _return_to_main_menu()
909: 
910: 
911: func _open_pause_panel() -> void:
912:     if _run_finished or _pause_menu_pending:
913:         return
914: 
915:     _pause_menu_pending = true
916:     GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.PAUSED)
917:     get_tree().paused = true
918:     EventBus.game_paused.emit(true)
919: 
920:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_method("open_panel"):
921:         _pause_panel.open_panel(_room_index, _current_room_type, _alignment)
922: 
923: 
924: func _close_pause_panel() -> void:
925:     if not _pause_menu_pending:
926:         return
927:     _reset_pause_state()
928: 
929: 
930: func _reset_pause_state() -> void:
931:     _pause_menu_pending = false
932:     get_tree().paused = false
933:     EventBus.game_paused.emit(false)
934: 
935:     if _pause_panel != null and _pause_panel.has_method("close_panel"):
936:         _pause_panel.close_panel()
937: 
938:     if not _run_finished:
939:         GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.PLAYING)
940: 
941: 
942: func _on_pause_resume_requested() -> void:
943:     _close_pause_panel()
944: 
945: 
946: func _on_pause_retreat_requested() -> void:
947:     _reset_pause_state()
948:     _finish_run("retreat")
949: 
950: 
951: func _on_pause_quit_to_menu_requested() -> void:
952:     _reset_pause_state()
953:     GameManager.set_state(GameManager.GameState.MENU)
954:     SceneManager.go_to_main_menu()
955: 
956: 
957: func _begin_chapter_transition(chapter: int) -> void:
958:     _chapter_transition_pending = true
959:     _room_status_label.text = "Boss down! Chapter %d cleared. Resolve chapter transition..." % chapter
960:     if _chapter_transition_panel != null and _chapter_transition_panel.has_method("show_transition"):
961:         _chapter_transition_panel.show_transition(chapter, _alignment)
962: 
963: 
964: func _on_transition_choice_committed(chapter_id: String, choice_id: String, alignment_delta: float) -> void:
965:     _alignment = clampf(_alignment + alignment_delta, -100.0, 100.0)
966:     EventBus.route_changed.emit(_alignment)
967:     EventBus.narrative_choice.emit(chapter_id, "chapter_transition", choice_id)
968:     var transition_segment_id: String = _get_transition_segment_id(chapter_id)
969:     if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("is_registered_narrative_id"):
970:         if not _narrative_system.is_registered_narrative_id(transition_segment_id):
971:             push_warning("Missing narrative index id: %s" % transition_segment_id)
972:     if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("record_choice"):
973:         _narrative_system.record_choice(chapter_id, transition_segment_id, choice_id, alignment_delta)
974:     _apply_transition_blessing(choice_id)
975:     _room_status_label.text = "Transition choice: %s (%+.0f). Press E to continue" % [
976:         choice_id,
977:         alignment_delta
978:     ]
979: 
980: 
981: func _on_transition_closed() -> void:
982:     _chapter_transition_pending = false
983:     _room_status_label.text = "Chapter transition resolved. %s" % _get_next_route_hint_text()
984: 
985: 
986: func _on_event_choice_committed(event_id: String, choice_id: String, choice_data: Dictionary) -> void:
987:     var chapter_id: String = _get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index)
988:     _apply_event_choice_effects(choice_data)
989:     EventBus.narrative_choice.emit(chapter_id, event_id, choice_id)
990:     if _narrative_system != null and _narrative_system.has_method("record_choice"):
991:         _narrative_system.record_choice(chapter_id, event_id, choice_id, float(choice_data.get("alignment_delta", 0.0)))
992: 
993:     var effect_var: Variant = choice_data.get("chapter_effect", {})
994:     if effect_var is Dictionary and not (effect_var as Dictionary).is_empty():
995:         _room_status_label.text = "Event committed: %s | New chapter effect queued: %s" % [
996:             choice_id,
997:             str((effect_var as Dictionary).get("title", "effect"))
998:         ]
999: 
1000: 
1001: func _on_event_closed() -> void:
1002:     _narrative_event_pending = false
1003:     _room_status_label.text = "Event resolved. Next room effects: %s | %s" % [_get_pending_chapter_effects_text(), _get_next_route_hint_text()]
1004: 
1005: 
1006: func _apply_event_choice_effects(choice_data: Dictionary) -> void:
1007:     _gold = maxi(0, _gold + int(choice_data.get("gold", 0)))
1008:     _ore = maxi(0, _ore + int(choice_data.get("ore", 0)))
1009:     EventBus.gold_changed.emit(_gold)
1010:     EventBus.ore_changed.emit(_ore)
1011: 
1012:     var alignment_delta: float = float(choice_data.get("alignment_delta", 0.0))
1013:     if not is_zero_approx(alignment_delta):
1014:         _alignment = clampf(_alignment + alignment_delta, -100.0, 100.0)
1015:         EventBus.route_changed.emit(_alignment)
1016: 
1017:     _set_frostbite(_frostbite + float(choice_data.get("frostbite_delta", 0.0)))
1018:     _set_void_corruption(_void_corruption + float(choice_data.get("void_delta", 0.0)))
1019: 
1020:     var blessing: String = str(choice_data.get("blessing", ""))
1021:     if blessing != "":
1022:         _apply_transition_blessing(blessing)
1023: 
1024:     var chapter_effect_var: Variant = choice_data.get("chapter_effect", {})
1025:     if chapter_effect_var is Dictionary:
1026:         _queue_chapter_effect(chapter_effect_var)
1027: 
1028: 
1029: func _apply_transition_blessing(choice_id: String) -> void:
1030:     _clear_active_blessing_effects()
1031: 
1032:     var stats: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("StatsComponent")
1033:     var health: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("HealthComponent")
1034:     var weapon: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("AutoWeapon")
1035:     if stats == null:
1036:         _active_blessing_id = "none"
1037:         return
1038: 
1039:     if choice_id == "holy_vow":
1040:         _active_blessing_id = "holy_vow"
1041:         if stats.get("armor") != null:
1042:             stats.armor = minf(0.75, stats.armor + 0.05)
1043:         if stats.get("frostbite_resistance") != null:
1044:             stats.frostbite_resistance = minf(0.75, stats.frostbite_resistance + 0.04)
1045:         if health != null and health.has_method("heal"):
1046:             health.heal(20.0)
1047:     elif choice_id == "void_oath":
1048:         _active_blessing_id = "void_oath"
1049:         if weapon != null and weapon.get("base_damage") != null:
1050:             weapon.base_damage += 1.8
1051:         if stats.get("crit_chance") != null:
1052:             stats.crit_chance = minf(0.95, stats.crit_chance + 0.04)
1053:         if stats.get("armor") != null:
1054:             stats.armor = maxf(0.0, stats.armor - 0.04)
1055:         if stats.get("void_resistance") != null:
1056:             stats.void_resistance = minf(0.75, stats.void_resistance + 0.05)
1057:     else:
1058:         _active_blessing_id = "none"
1059: 
1060:     if health != null and health.get("current_hp") != null and health.get("max_hp") != null:
1061:         EventBus.health_changed.emit(float(health.current_hp), float(health.max_hp))
1062: 
1063: 
1064: func _clear_active_blessing_effects() -> void:
1065:     if _active_blessing_id == "none":
1066:         return
1067: 
1068:     var stats: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("StatsComponent")
1069:     var weapon: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("AutoWeapon")
1070:     if stats == null:
1071:         _active_blessing_id = "none"
1072:         return
1073: 
1074:     match _active_blessing_id:
1075:         "holy_vow":
1076:             if stats.get("armor") != null:
1077:                 stats.armor = maxf(0.0, stats.armor - 0.05)
1078:             if stats.get("frostbite_resistance") != null:
1079:                 stats.frostbite_resistance = maxf(0.0, stats.frostbite_resistance - 0.04)
1080:         "void_oath":
1081:             if weapon != null and weapon.get("base_damage") != null:
1082:                 weapon.base_damage = maxf(1.0, weapon.base_damage - 1.8)
1083:             if stats.get("crit_chance") != null:
1084:                 stats.crit_chance = maxf(0.0, stats.crit_chance - 0.04)
1085:             if stats.get("armor") != null:
1086:                 stats.armor = minf(0.75, stats.armor + 0.04)
1087:             if stats.get("void_resistance") != null:
1088:                 stats.void_resistance = maxf(0.0, stats.void_resistance - 0.05)
1089: 
1090:     _active_blessing_id = "none"
1091: 
1092: 
1093: func _queue_chapter_effect(effect_data: Dictionary) -> void:
1094:     if effect_data.is_empty():
1095:         return
1096: 
1097:     var duration_rooms: int = maxi(1, int(effect_data.get("duration_rooms", 2)))
1098:     var effects_var: Variant = effect_data.get("effects", {})
1099:     if not (effects_var is Dictionary):
1100:         return
1101: 
1102:     var packed_effect: Dictionary = {
1103:         "id": str(effect_data.get("id", "effect_unknown")),
1104:         "title": str(effect_data.get("title", "Chapter Effect")),
1105:         "desc": str(effect_data.get("desc", "")),
1106:         "remaining_rooms": duration_rooms,
1107:         "effects": (effects_var as Dictionary).duplicate(true)
1108:     }
1109:     var icon: String = "[~]"
1110:     var score: float = 0.0
1111:     var packed_effects_var: Variant = packed_effect.get("effects", {})
1112:     if packed_effects_var is Dictionary:
1113:         icon = _get_chapter_effect_icon(packed_effects_var)
1114:         score = _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(packed_effects_var)
1115: 
1116:     _active_chapter_effects.append(packed_effect)
1117:     _chapter_effect_timeline.append({
1118:         "room_index": _room_index,
1119:         "chapter_id": _get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index),
1120:         "effect_id": str(packed_effect.get("id", "effect_unknown")),
1121:         "title": str(packed_effect.get("title", "Chapter Effect")),
1122:         "desc": str(packed_effect.get("desc", "")),
1123:         "duration_rooms": duration_rooms,
1124:         "icon": icon,
1125:         "score": score
1126:     })
1127:     _camp_message = "Gained chapter effect: %s (%d rooms)" % [packed_effect["title"], duration_rooms]
1128: 
1129: 
1130: func _advance_chapter_effects_for_room() -> void:
1131:     _chapter_effect_spawn_rate_mult = 1.0
1132:     _chapter_effect_enemy_hp_mult = 1.0
1133:     _chapter_effect_enemy_damage_mult = 1.0
1134:     _chapter_effect_hazard_mult = 1.0
1135:     _chapter_effect_move_speed_mult = 1.0
1136:     _chapter_effect_damage_bonus = 0.0
1137:     _chapter_effect_armor_bonus = 0.0
1138:     _chapter_effects_this_room.clear()
1139: 
1140:     var retained_effects: Array[Dictionary] = []
1141:     for item: Variant in _active_chapter_effects:
1142:         if not (item is Dictionary):
1143:             continue
1144: 
1145:         var row: Dictionary = (item as Dictionary).duplicate(true)
1146:         var remaining_rooms: int = int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 0))
1147:         if remaining_rooms <= 0:
1148:             continue
1149: 
1150:         var effects_var: Variant = row.get("effects", {})
1151:         var effects_map: Dictionary = {}
1152:         if effects_var is Dictionary:
1153:             effects_map = (effects_var as Dictionary).duplicate(true)
1154:             _accumulate_chapter_effect_modifiers(effects_var)
1155: 
1156:         _chapter_effects_this_room.append({
1157:             "id": str(row.get("id", "effect")),
1158:             "title": str(row.get("title", "Chapter Effect")),
1159:             "remaining_rooms": remaining_rooms,
1160:             "icon": _get_chapter_effect_icon(effects_map),
1161:             "score": _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(effects_map)
1162:         })
1163: 
1164:         row["remaining_rooms"] = remaining_rooms - 1
1165:         if int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 0)) > 0:
1166:             retained_effects.append(row)
1167: 
1168:     _active_chapter_effects = retained_effects
1169:     _apply_chapter_effect_runtime()
1170: 
1171: 
1172: func _accumulate_chapter_effect_modifiers(effects: Dictionary) -> void:
1173:     _chapter_effect_spawn_rate_mult *= maxf(0.55, float(effects.get("enemy_spawn_rate_mult", 1.0)))
1174:     _chapter_effect_enemy_hp_mult *= maxf(0.55, float(effects.get("enemy_hp_mult", 1.0)))
1175:     _chapter_effect_enemy_damage_mult *= maxf(0.55, float(effects.get("enemy_damage_mult", 1.0)))
1176:     _chapter_effect_hazard_mult *= maxf(0.5, float(effects.get("hazard_intensity_mult", 1.0)))
1177:     _chapter_effect_move_speed_mult *= clampf(float(effects.get("move_speed_mult", 1.0)), 0.6, 1.4)
1178:     _chapter_effect_damage_bonus += float(effects.get("damage_bonus_pct", 0.0))
1179:     _chapter_effect_armor_bonus += float(effects.get("armor_bonus", 0.0))
1180: 
1181: 
1182: func _apply_chapter_effect_runtime() -> void:
1183:     var stats: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("StatsComponent")
1184:     var weapon: Node = _player.get_node_or_null("AutoWeapon")
1185: 
1186:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("set_runtime_modifiers"):
1187:         _spawner.set_runtime_modifiers(_chapter_effect_spawn_rate_mult, _chapter_effect_enemy_hp_mult, _chapter_effect_enemy_damage_mult)
1188: 
1189:     if weapon != null and weapon.get("external_damage_bonus_pct") != null:
1190:         weapon.external_damage_bonus_pct = _chapter_effect_damage_bonus
1191: 
1192:     var desired_armor_bonus: float = clampf(_chapter_effect_armor_bonus, -0.3, 0.3)
1193:     if stats != null and stats.get("armor") != null:
1194:         var delta: float = desired_armor_bonus - _chapter_effect_applied_armor_bonus
1195:         if not is_zero_approx(delta):
1196:             stats.armor = clampf(stats.armor + delta, 0.0, 0.75)
1197:         _chapter_effect_applied_armor_bonus = desired_armor_bonus
1198:     else:
1199:         _chapter_effect_applied_armor_bonus = 0.0
1200: 
1201: 
1202: func _get_active_chapter_effects_text() -> String:
1203:     if _chapter_effects_this_room.is_empty():
1204:         return "none"
1205: 
1206:     var rows: Array[String] = []
1207:     for item: Variant in _chapter_effects_this_room:
1208:         if not (item is Dictionary):
1209:             continue
1210:         var row: Dictionary = item
1211:         rows.append("%s %s(%d)" % [
1212:             str(row.get("icon", "[~]")),
1213:             str(row.get("title", "Effect")),
1214:             int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 1))
1215:         ])
1216:     if rows.is_empty():
1217:         return "none"
1218:     return ", ".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
1219: 
1220:

1222:     if _active_chapter_effects.is_empty():
1223:         return "none"
1224:

1226:     for item: Variant in _active_chapter_effects:
1227:         if not (item is Dictionary):
1228:             continue
1229:         var row: Dictionary = item
1230:         var effects_var: Variant = row.get("effects", {})
1231:         var icon: String = "[~]"
1232:         if effects_var is Dictionary:
1233:             icon = _get_chapter_effect_icon(effects_var)
1234:         rows.append("%s(%d)" % [
1235:             "%s %s" % [icon, str(row.get("title", "Effect"))],
1236:             int(row.get("remaining_rooms", 0))
1237:         ])
1238:     if rows.is_empty():
1239:         return "none"
1240:     return ", ".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
1241: 
1242: 
1243: func _get_chapter_effect_icon(effects: Dictionary) -> String:
1244:     var score: float = _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(effects)
1245:     if score >= 0.25:
1246:         return "[+]"
1247:     if score <= -0.25:
1248:         return "[-]"
1249:     return "[~]"
1250: 
1251: 
1252: func _evaluate_chapter_effect_score(effects: Dictionary) -> float:
1253:     if effects.is_empty():
1254:         return 0.0
1255: 
1256:     var score: float = 0.0
1257:     score += float(effects.get("damage_bonus_pct", 0.0)) * 1.0
1258:     score += float(effects.get("armor_bonus", 0.0)) * 1.2
1259: 
1260:     var move_mult: float = float(effects.get("move_speed_mult", 1.0))
1261:     score += (move_mult - 1.0) * 1.4
1262: 
1263:     var spawn_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_spawn_rate_mult", 1.0))
1264:     score += (1.0 - spawn_mult) * 0.9
1265: 
1266:     var hp_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_hp_mult", 1.0))
1267:     score += (1.0 - hp_mult) * 0.9
1268: 
1269:     var dmg_mult: float = float(effects.get("enemy_damage_mult", 1.0))
1270:     score += (1.0 - dmg_mult) * 1.1
1271: 
1272:     var hazard_mult: float = float(effects.get("hazard_intensity_mult", 1.0))
1273:     score += (1.0 - hazard_mult) * 1.1
1274:     return score
1275: 
1276: 
1277: func _get_active_blessing_text() -> String:
1278:     match _active_blessing_id:
1279:         "holy_vow":
1280:             return "Holy Vow (+armor, +frost resist, +heal)"
1281:         "void_oath":
1282:             return "Void Oath (+damage, +crit, -armor)"
1283:         _:
1284:             return "None"
1285:

336:             min_room_type_per_chapter = constraints.get("min_room_type_per_chapter")

339:             if not isinstance(max_treasure_per_chapter, int) or max_treasure_per_chapter < 0 or max_treasure_per_chapter > 5:
340:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_treasure_per_chapter must be int within [0, 5]")

380: def _validate_enemy_scaling(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
381:     brackets = data.get("room_time_brackets")
382:     multipliers = data.get("floor_multipliers")
383:     elite_wave_interval = data.get("elite_wave_interval")
384:     type_weights = data.get("enemy_type_weights")
385:     if not isinstance(brackets, list) or not brackets:
386:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be a non-empty array")
387:     else:
388:         last_max = -1.0
389:         for i, row in enumerate(brackets):
390:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
391:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}] must be object")
392:                 continue
393:             max_seconds = row.get("max_seconds")
394:             hp_mult = row.get("hp_mult")
395:             dmg_mult = row.get("damage_mult")
396:             max_seconds_f = _to_float(max_seconds)
397:             if max_seconds_f is None:
398:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
399:             elif max_seconds_f <= 0:
400:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
401:             elif max_seconds_f <= last_max:
402:                 _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be strictly increasing")
403:             else:
404:                 last_max = max_seconds_f
405: 
406:             hp_mult_f = _to_float(hp_mult)
407:             if hp_mult_f is None:
408:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
409:             elif hp_mult_f <= 0:
410:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
411: 
412:             dmg_mult_f = _to_float(dmg_mult)
413:             if dmg_mult_f is None:
414:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
415:             elif dmg_mult_f <= 0:
416:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
417: 
418:     if not isinstance(multipliers, dict):
419:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json floor_multipliers must be an object")
420:     else:
421:         for floor in range(1, 16):
422:             key = str(floor)
423:             if key not in multipliers:
424:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json missing floor multiplier for floor {floor}")
425:                 continue
426:             value = multipliers[key]
427:             value_f = _to_float(value)
428:             if value_f is None:
429:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json floor {floor} multiplier must be > 0")
430:             elif value_f <= 0:
431:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json floor {floor} multiplier must be > 0")
432:

434:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json elite_wave_interval must be int >= 3")

437:     if not isinstance(type_weights, dict):

230:     var cumulative: float = 0.0

233:         cumulative += weight
234:         if roll <= cumulative:

328:     if enemy == null and enemy_scene != null:

335: func _get_spawn_interval() -> float:
336:     var floor_ratio: float = 1.0 + float(floor_index - 1) * 0.09
337:     var time_ratio: float = 1.0
338:     if _room_time > 120.0:
339:         time_ratio = 1.8
340:     elif _room_time > 60.0:
341:         time_ratio = 1.5
342:     elif _room_time > 30.0:
343:         time_ratio = 1.25
344: 
345:     var interval: float = 1.3 / (floor_ratio * time_ratio * _runtime_spawn_rate_mult)
346:     if _combat_mode == "elite":

348:     return clampf(interval, 0.2, 1.3)

354:     return float(multipliers.get(str(floor_index), 1.0))

357: func _get_room_pressure_values() -> Dictionary:
358:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
359:     var brackets: Array = scaling.get("room_time_brackets", [])
360:     for item: Variant in brackets:

362:             continue
363:         var row: Dictionary = item

198:         health_component.current_hp = health_component.max_hp

222: func _pick_enemy_archetype() -> String:
223:     var total: float = 0.0
224:     for value: Variant in _enemy_type_weights.values():
225:         total += maxf(0.0, float(value))
226:     if total <= 0.0:
227:         return "normal"
228: 
229:     var roll: float = randf() * total
230:     var cumulative: float = 0.0
231:     for key: Variant in _enemy_type_weights.keys():
232:         var weight: float = maxf(0.0, float(_enemy_type_weights.get(key, 0.0)))
233:         cumulative += weight
234:         if roll <= cumulative:
235:             return str(key)
236:     return "normal"
237: 
238: 
239: func _build_enemy_id(archetype: String, is_elite: bool) -> String:
240:     var base_map: Dictionary = {
241:         "normal": "enemy_shadowling",
242:         "fast": "enemy_stalker",
243:         "tank": "enemy_brute",
244:         "ranged": "enemy_hexcaster"
245:     }
246:     var base_name: String = str(base_map.get(archetype, "enemy_shadowling"))
247:     if is_elite:
248:         return "elite_%s" % base_name.trim_prefix("enemy_")
249:     return base_name
