335: func _get_spawn_interval() -> float:
336:     var floor_ratio: float = 1.0 + float(floor_index - 1) * 0.09
337:     var time_ratio: float = 1.0
338:     if _room_time > 120.0:
339:         time_ratio = 1.8
340:     elif _room_time > 60.0:
341:         time_ratio = 1.5
342:     elif _room_time > 30.0:
343:         time_ratio = 1.25
344: 
345:     var interval: float = 1.3 / (floor_ratio * time_ratio * _runtime_spawn_rate_mult)
346:     if _combat_mode == "elite":
347:         interval *= 1.18
348:     return clampf(interval, 0.2, 1.3)
349: 
350: 
351: func _get_floor_multiplier() -> float:
352:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
353:     var multipliers: Dictionary = scaling.get("floor_multipliers", {})
354:     return float(multipliers.get(str(floor_index), 1.0))
355: 
356: 
357: func _get_room_pressure_values() -> Dictionary:
358:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
359:     var brackets: Array = scaling.get("room_time_brackets", [])
360:     for item: Variant in brackets:
361:         if not (item is Dictionary):
362:             continue
363:         var row: Dictionary = item
364:         if _room_time <= float(row.get("max_seconds", 9999.0)):
365:             return row
366:     return {"hp_mult": 1.0, "damage_mult": 1.0}

338:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_consecutive_same_type must be int within [1, 5]")
339:             if not isinstance(max_treasure_per_chapter, int) or max_treasure_per_chapter < 0 or max_treasure_per_chapter > 5:
340:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_treasure_per_chapter must be int within [0, 5]")
341: 
342:             required_cap_keys = ("event", "shop", "elite", "treasure")
343:             if not isinstance(max_room_type_per_chapter, dict) or not max_room_type_per_chapter:
344:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_room_type_per_chapter must be non-empty object")
345:             else:
346:                 for key in required_cap_keys:
347:                     value = max_room_type_per_chapter.get(key)
348:                     if not isinstance(value, int) or value < 0 or value > room_count:
349:                         _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json constraints.max_room_type_per_chapter.{key} must be int within [0, room_count]")
350: 
351:                 if isinstance(max_treasure_per_chapter, int):
352:                     treasure_cap = max_room_type_per_chapter.get("treasure")
353:                     if isinstance(treasure_cap, int) and treasure_cap != max_treasure_per_chapter:
354:                         _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_treasure_per_chapter must match max_room_type_per_chapter.treasure")
355: 
356:             required_min_keys = ("event", "shop", "elite", "treasure")
357:             if not isinstance(min_room_type_per_chapter, dict) or not min_room_type_per_chapter:
358:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.min_room_type_per_chapter must be non-empty object")
359:             else:
360:                 for key in required_min_keys:
361:                     value = min_room_type_per_chapter.get(key)
362:                     if not isinstance(value, int) or value < 0 or value > room_count:
363:                         _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json constraints.min_room_type_per_chapter.{key} must be int within [0, room_count]")
364: 
365:                     if isinstance(max_room_type_per_chapter, dict):
366:                         max_value = max_room_type_per_chapter.get(key)
367:                         if isinstance(value, int) and isinstance(max_value, int) and value > max_value:
368:                             _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json constraints.min_room_type_per_chapter.{key} cannot exceed max_room_type_per_chapter.{key}")
369: 
370:                 if isinstance(max_treasure_per_chapter, int):
371:                     treasure_min = min_room_type_per_chapter.get("treasure")
372:                     if isinstance(treasure_min, int) and treasure_min > max_treasure_per_chapter:
373:                         _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.min_room_type_per_chapter.treasure cannot exceed max_treasure_per_chapter")
374:             for key in ("avoid_shop_near_boss", "avoid_event_near_boss"):
375:                 value = constraints.get(key)
376:                 if not isinstance(value, bool):
377:                     _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json constraints.{key} must be bool")
378: 
379: 
380: def _validate_enemy_scaling(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
381:     brackets = data.get("room_time_brackets")
382:     multipliers = data.get("floor_multipliers")
383:     elite_wave_interval = data.get("elite_wave_interval")
384:     type_weights = data.get("enemy_type_weights")
385:     if not isinstance(brackets, list) or not brackets:
386:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be a non-empty array")
387:     else:
388:         last_max = -1.0
389:         for i, row in enumerate(brackets):
390:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
391:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}] must be object")
392:                 continue
393:             max_seconds = row.get("max_seconds")
394:             hp_mult = row.get("hp_mult")
395:             dmg_mult = row.get("damage_mult")
396:             max_seconds_f = _to_float(max_seconds)
397:             if max_seconds_f is None:
398:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
399:             elif max_seconds_f <= 0:
400:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
401:             elif max_seconds_f <= last_max:
402:                 _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be strictly increasing")
403:             else:
404:                 last_max = max_seconds_f
405: 
406:             hp_mult_f = _to_float(hp_mult)
407:             if hp_mult_f is None:
408:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
409:             elif hp_mult_f <= 0:
410:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
411: 
412:             dmg_mult_f = _to_float(dmg_mult)
413:             if dmg_mult_f is None:
414:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
415:             elif dmg_mult_f <= 0:
416:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
417: 
418:     if not isinstance(multipliers, dict):
419:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json floor_multipliers must be an object")
420:     else:
421:         for floor in range(1, 16):
422:             key = str(floor)
423:             if key not in multipliers:
424:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json missing floor multiplier for floor {floor}")
425:                 continue
426:             value = multipliers[key]
427:             value_f = _to_float(value)
428:             if value_f is None:
429:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json floor {floor} multiplier must be > 0")
430:             elif value_f <= 0:
431:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json floor {floor} multiplier must be > 0")
432: 
433:     if not isinstance(elite_wave_interval, int) or elite_wave_interval < 3:
434:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json elite_wave_interval must be int >= 3")
435: 
436:     required_enemy_types = ("normal", "fast", "tank", "ranged")
437:     if not isinstance(type_weights, dict):
438:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json enemy_type_weights must be an object")
439:     else:
440:         total_weight = 0.0
441:         for enemy_type in required_enemy_types:
442:             if enemy_type not in type_weights:
443:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json enemy_type_weights missing '{enemy_type}'")
444:                 continue
445:             weight_f = _to_float(type_weights.get(enemy_type))
446:             if weight_f is None:
447:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json enemy_type_weights['{enemy_type}'] must be >= 0")
448:                 continue
449:             if weight_f < 0:
450:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json enemy_type_weights['{enemy_type}'] must be >= 0")
451:                 continue
452:             total_weight += weight_f
453:         if total_weight <= 0:
454:             _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json enemy_type_weights total must be > 0")
455: 
456: 
457: def _validate_drop_tables(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
458:     for table_name in ("normal", "elite", "boss"):
459:         table = data.get(table_name)
460:         if not isinstance(table, dict):
461:             _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json missing table '{table_name}'")
462:             continue
463: 
464:         guaranteed = table.get("guaranteed")
465:         weighted = table.get("weighted")
466:         if not isinstance(guaranteed, list) or not guaranteed:
467:             _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.guaranteed must be non-empty array")
468:         if not isinstance(weighted, list) or not weighted:
469:             _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.weighted must be non-empty array")
470:             continue
471: 
472:         for i, row in enumerate(weighted):
473:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
474:                 _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.weighted[{i}] must be object")
475:                 continue
476:             item_id = row.get("id")
477:             weight = row.get("weight")
478:             if not isinstance(item_id, str) or not item_id:
479:                 _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.weighted[{i}].id invalid")
480:             weight_f = _to_float(weight)
481:             if weight_f is None:
482:                 _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.weighted[{i}].weight must be > 0")
483:             elif weight_f <= 0:
484:                 _add_error(errors, f"drop_tables.json {table_name}.weighted[{i}].weight must be > 0")
485: 
486: 
487: def _validate_shop_items(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
488:     slots = data.get("slots")
489:     restock_cost = data.get("restock_cost")
490:     restock_growth = data.get("restock_growth")
491:     restock_cost_cap = data.get("restock_cost_cap")
492:     catchup_discount = data.get("catchup_discount")
493:     ore_exchange = data.get("ore_exchange")
494:     chapter_overrides = data.get("chapter_overrides")
495:     route_style_overrides = data.get("route_style_overrides")
496:     quality_weights = data.get("quality_weights")
497:     category_weights = data.get("category_weights")
498:     pools = data.get("pools")
499: 
500:     if not isinstance(slots, int) or slots < 1:
501:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json slots must be int >= 1")
502:     if isinstance(slots, int) and slots > 8:
503:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json slots should be <= 8")
504:     if not isinstance(restock_cost, int) or restock_cost < 0:
505:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json restock_cost must be int >= 0")
506:     restock_growth_f = _to_float(restock_growth)
507:     if restock_growth_f is None or restock_growth_f < 0.0:
508:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json restock_growth must be numeric >= 0")
509:     elif restock_growth_f > 1.2:
510:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json restock_growth should be <= 1.2")
511:     if not isinstance(restock_cost_cap, int) or restock_cost_cap < int(restock_cost if isinstance(restock_cost, int) else 0):
512:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json restock_cost_cap must be int >= restock_cost")
513: 
514:     if not isinstance(catchup_discount, dict):
515:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json catchup_discount must be object")
516:     else:
517:         target_gold = catchup_discount.get("target_gold_per_room")
518:         max_discount = catchup_discount.get("max_discount")
519:         high_markup = catchup_discount.get("high_gold_markup")
520:         high_threshold = catchup_discount.get("high_gold_threshold_mult")
521: 
522:         target_gold_f = _to_float(target_gold)
523:         max_discount_f = _to_float(max_discount)
524:         high_markup_f = _to_float(high_markup)
525:         high_threshold_f = _to_float(high_threshold)
526: 
527:         if target_gold_f is None or target_gold_f <= 0:
528:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json catchup_discount.target_gold_per_room must be > 0")
529:         if max_discount_f is None or max_discount_f < 0.0 or max_discount_f > 0.75:
530:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json catchup_discount.max_discount must be within [0, 0.75]")
531:         if high_markup_f is None or high_markup_f < 0.0 or high_markup_f > 0.45:
532:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json catchup_discount.high_gold_markup must be within [0, 0.45]")
533:         if high_threshold_f is None or high_threshold_f < 1.0:
534:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json catchup_discount.high_gold_threshold_mult must be >= 1.0")
535: 
536:     if not isinstance(ore_exchange, dict):
537:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange must be object")
538:     else:
539:         enabled = ore_exchange.get("enabled")
540:         ore_per_trade = ore_exchange.get("ore_per_trade")
541:         gold_per_trade = ore_exchange.get("gold_per_trade")
542:         max_trades = ore_exchange.get("max_trades_per_shop")
543:         bonus_chance = ore_exchange.get("bonus_trade_chance")
544:         bonus_gold = ore_exchange.get("bonus_gold")
545: 
546:         if not isinstance(enabled, bool):
547:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.enabled must be bool")
548:         if not isinstance(ore_per_trade, int) or ore_per_trade < 1:
549:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.ore_per_trade must be int >= 1")
550:         if not isinstance(gold_per_trade, int) or gold_per_trade < 1:
551:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.gold_per_trade must be int >= 1")
552:         if not isinstance(max_trades, int) or max_trades < 1:
553:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.max_trades_per_shop must be int >= 1")
554:         bonus_chance_f = _to_float(bonus_chance)
555:         if bonus_chance_f is None or bonus_chance_f < 0.0 or bonus_chance_f > 1.0:
556:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.bonus_trade_chance must be within [0, 1]")
557:         if not isinstance(bonus_gold, int) or bonus_gold < 0:
558:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json ore_exchange.bonus_gold must be int >= 0")
559: 
560:     if not isinstance(chapter_overrides, dict):
561:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json chapter_overrides must be object")
562:     else:
563:         expected_chapters = ("chapter_1", "chapter_2", "chapter_3", "chapter_4")
564:         for chapter_id in expected_chapters:
565:             chapter_row = chapter_overrides.get(chapter_id)
566:             if not isinstance(chapter_row, dict):
567:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id} must be object")
568:                 continue
569: 
570:             price_mult = _to_float(chapter_row.get("price_mult"))
571:             restock_cost_mult = _to_float(chapter_row.get("restock_cost_mult"))
572:             restock_growth_add = _to_float(chapter_row.get("restock_growth_add"))
573:             target_gold_mult = _to_float(chapter_row.get("target_gold_mult"))
574:             max_discount_add = _to_float(chapter_row.get("max_discount_add"))
575:             high_markup_add = _to_float(chapter_row.get("high_markup_add"))
576:             exchange_gold_add = chapter_row.get("ore_exchange_gold_add")
577:             exchange_trades_add = chapter_row.get("ore_exchange_max_trades_add")
578:             exchange_bonus_chance_add = _to_float(chapter_row.get("ore_exchange_bonus_chance_add"))
579:             exchange_bonus_gold_add = chapter_row.get("ore_exchange_bonus_gold_add")
580:             chapter_quality_mult = chapter_row.get("quality_weight_mult")
581:             chapter_category_mult = chapter_row.get("category_weight_mult")
582:             chapter_pool_overrides = chapter_row.get("pool_overrides")
583: 
584:             if price_mult is None or price_mult < 0.6 or price_mult > 1.6:
585:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.price_mult must be within [0.6, 1.6]")
586:             if restock_cost_mult is None or restock_cost_mult < 0.6 or restock_cost_mult > 1.9:
587:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.restock_cost_mult must be within [0.6, 1.9]")
588:             if restock_growth_add is None or restock_growth_add < -0.5 or restock_growth_add > 0.8:
589:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.restock_growth_add must be within [-0.5, 0.8]")
590:             if target_gold_mult is None or target_gold_mult < 0.5 or target_gold_mult > 2.0:
591:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.target_gold_mult must be within [0.5, 2.0]")
592:             if max_discount_add is None or max_discount_add < -0.4 or max_discount_add > 0.4:
593:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.max_discount_add must be within [-0.4, 0.4]")
594:             if high_markup_add is None or high_markup_add < -0.3 or high_markup_add > 0.3:
595:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.high_markup_add must be within [-0.3, 0.3]")
596:             if not isinstance(exchange_gold_add, int) or exchange_gold_add < -30 or exchange_gold_add > 30:
597:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.ore_exchange_gold_add must be int within [-30, 30]")
598:             if not isinstance(exchange_trades_add, int) or exchange_trades_add < -3 or exchange_trades_add > 5:
599:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.ore_exchange_max_trades_add must be int within [-3, 5]")
600:             if exchange_bonus_chance_add is None or exchange_bonus_chance_add < -0.6 or exchange_bonus_chance_add > 0.6:
601:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.ore_exchange_bonus_chance_add must be within [-0.6, 0.6]")
602:             if not isinstance(exchange_bonus_gold_add, int) or exchange_bonus_gold_add < -10 or exchange_bonus_gold_add > 20:
603:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.ore_exchange_bonus_gold_add must be int within [-10, 20]")
604: 
605:             if not isinstance(chapter_quality_mult, dict):
606:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.quality_weight_mult must be object")
607:             else:
608:                 for quality_key in ("common", "rare", "epic", "legendary"):
609:                     quality_mult_value = _to_float(chapter_quality_mult.get(quality_key))
610:                     if quality_mult_value is None or quality_mult_value < 0.0 or quality_mult_value > 3.5:
611:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.quality_weight_mult.{quality_key} must be within [0.0, 3.5]")
612: 
613:             if not isinstance(chapter_category_mult, dict):
614:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.category_weight_mult must be object")
615:             else:
616:                 for category_key in ("consumable", "passive", "weapon"):
617:                     category_mult_value = _to_float(chapter_category_mult.get(category_key))
618:                     if category_mult_value is None or category_mult_value < 0.0 or category_mult_value > 3.0:
619:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.category_weight_mult.{category_key} must be within [0.0, 3.0]")
620: 
621:             if not isinstance(chapter_pool_overrides, dict):
622:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.pool_overrides must be object")
623:             else:
624:                 for category_key, rows in chapter_pool_overrides.items():
625:                     if category_key not in ("consumable", "passive", "weapon"):
626:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.pool_overrides has unknown category '{category_key}'")
627:                         continue
628:                     if not isinstance(rows, list) or not rows:
629:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.pool_overrides['{category_key}'] must be non-empty array")
630:                         continue
631:                     for row in rows:
632:                         if not isinstance(row, str) or not row:
633:                             _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json chapter_overrides.{chapter_id}.pool_overrides['{category_key}'] entries must be non-empty strings")
634: 
635:     if not isinstance(route_style_overrides, dict) or not route_style_overrides:
636:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json route_style_overrides must be non-empty object")
637:     else:
638:         expected_styles = ("neutral", "vanguard", "raider")
639:         for style_id in expected_styles:
640:             style_row = route_style_overrides.get(style_id)
641:             if not isinstance(style_row, dict):
642:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id} must be object")
643:                 continue
644: 
645:             price_mult = _to_float(style_row.get("price_mult"))
646:             target_gold_mult = _to_float(style_row.get("target_gold_mult"))
647:             max_discount_add = _to_float(style_row.get("max_discount_add"))
648:             high_markup_add = _to_float(style_row.get("high_markup_add"))
649:             exchange_gold_add = style_row.get("exchange_gold_add")
650:             quality_mult = style_row.get("quality_weight_mult")
651:             category_mult = style_row.get("category_weight_mult")
652: 
653:             if price_mult is None or price_mult < 0.7 or price_mult > 1.5:
654:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.price_mult must be within [0.7, 1.5]")
655:             if target_gold_mult is None or target_gold_mult < 0.6 or target_gold_mult > 1.8:
656:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.target_gold_mult must be within [0.6, 1.8]")
657:             if max_discount_add is None or max_discount_add < -0.35 or max_discount_add > 0.35:
658:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.max_discount_add must be within [-0.35, 0.35]")
659:             if high_markup_add is None or high_markup_add < -0.25 or high_markup_add > 0.35:
660:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.high_markup_add must be within [-0.25, 0.35]")
661:             if not isinstance(exchange_gold_add, int) or exchange_gold_add < -15 or exchange_gold_add > 25:
662:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.exchange_gold_add must be int within [-15, 25]")
663: 
664:             if not isinstance(quality_mult, dict):
665:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.quality_weight_mult must be object")
666:             else:
667:                 for quality_key in ("common", "rare", "epic", "legendary"):
668:                     quality_mult_value = _to_float(quality_mult.get(quality_key))
669:                     if quality_mult_value is None or quality_mult_value < 0.0 or quality_mult_value > 3.0:
670:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.quality_weight_mult.{quality_key} must be within [0.0, 3.0]")
671: 
672:             if not isinstance(category_mult, dict):
673:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.category_weight_mult must be object")
674:             else:
675:                 for category_key in ("consumable", "passive", "weapon"):
676:                     category_mult_value = _to_float(category_mult.get(category_key))
677:                     if category_mult_value is None or category_mult_value < 0.0 or category_mult_value > 3.0:
678:                         _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json route_style_overrides.{style_id}.category_weight_mult.{category_key} must be within [0.0, 3.0]")
679: 
680:     if not isinstance(quality_weights, dict) or not quality_weights:
681:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json quality_weights must be non-empty object")
682:     else:
683:         total = 0.0
684:         for key, value in quality_weights.items():
685:             if not _is_number(value) or float(value) < 0:
686:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json quality_weights['{key}'] must be >= 0")
687:             else:
688:                 total += float(value)
689:         if total <= 0:
690:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json quality_weights total must be > 0")
691: 
692:     if not isinstance(category_weights, dict) or not category_weights:
693:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json category_weights must be non-empty object")
694:     else:
695:         total = 0.0
696:         for category_key in ("consumable", "passive", "weapon"):
697:             value_f = _to_float(category_weights.get(category_key))
698:             if value_f is None or value_f < 0:
699:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json category_weights['{category_key}'] must be >= 0")
700:             else:
701:                 total += value_f
702:         if total <= 0:
703:             _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json category_weights total must be > 0")
704: 
705:     if not isinstance(pools, dict) or not pools:
706:         _add_error(errors, "shop_items.json pools must be non-empty object")
707:     else:
708:         for category, rows in pools.items():
709:             if not isinstance(rows, list) or not rows:
710:                 _add_error(errors, f"shop_items.json pools['{category}'] must be non-empty array")
711: 
712: 
713: def _validate_environment_config(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
714:     chapters = data.get("chapters")
715:     if not isinstance(chapters, dict):
716:         _add_error(errors, "environment_config.json chapters must be an object")
717:         return
718: 
719:     for chapter_key in ("chapter_1", "chapter_2", "chapter_3", "chapter_4"):
720:         row = chapters.get(chapter_key)
721:         if not isinstance(row, dict):
722:             _add_error(errors, f"environment_config.json missing '{chapter_key}'")
723:             continue
724:         if not isinstance(row.get("theme"), str) or not row["theme"]:
725:             _add_error(errors, f"environment_config.json {chapter_key}.theme invalid")
726:         hazards = row.get("hazards")
727:         if not isinstance(hazards, list) or not hazards:
728:             _add_error(errors, f"environment_config.json {chapter_key}.hazards must be non-empty array")
729: 
730: 
731: def _validate_boss_phases(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
732:     bosses = data.get("bosses")
733:     if not isinstance(bosses, dict) or not bosses:
734:         _add_error(errors, "boss_phases.json bosses must be non-empty object")
735:         return
736: 
737:     for boss_id, thresholds in bosses.items():
738:         if not isinstance(thresholds, list) or len(thresholds) < 2:
739:             _add_error(errors, f"boss_phases.json {boss_id} thresholds must contain at least 2 values")
740:             continue
741: 
742:         prev = None
743:         for i, value in enumerate(thresholds):
744:             if not _is_number(value):
745:                 _add_error(errors, f"boss_phases.json {boss_id}[{i}] must be numeric")
746:                 continue
747:             v = float(value)
748:             if v <= 0.0 or v > 1.0:
749:                 _add_error(errors, f"boss_phases.json {boss_id}[{i}] must be within (0, 1]")
750:             if i == 0 and abs(v - 1.0) > 0.001:
751:                 _add_error(errors, f"boss_phases.json {boss_id} first threshold must be 1.0")
752:             if prev is not None and v >= prev:
753:                 _add_error(errors, f"boss_phases.json {boss_id} thresholds must be strictly descending")
754:             prev = v
755: 
756: 
757: def _validate_narrative_index(root: Path, data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str], warnings: list[str]) -> None:
758:     segments = data.get("segments")
759:     if not isinstance(segments, list) or not segments:
760:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_index.json segments must be non-empty array")
761:         return
762: 
763:     seen_ids: set[str] = set()
764:     for i, row in enumerate(segments):
765:         if not isinstance(row, dict):
766:             _add_error(errors, f"narrative_index.json segments[{i}] must be object")
767:             continue
768:         seg_id = row.get("id")
769:         path = row.get("resource_path")
770:         if not isinstance(seg_id, str) or not seg_id:
771:             _add_error(errors, f"narrative_index.json segments[{i}].id invalid")
772:             continue
773:         if seg_id in seen_ids:
774:             _add_error(errors, f"narrative_index.json duplicate segment id '{seg_id}'")
775:         seen_ids.add(seg_id)
776:         if not isinstance(path, str) or not path.startswith("res://"):
777:             _add_error(errors, f"narrative_index.json segments[{i}].resource_path must start with res://")
778:             continue
779: 
780:         disk_path = root / path.replace("res://", "")
781:         if not disk_path.exists():
782:             warnings.append(f"narrative_index.json missing resource file: {path}")
783: 
784:     memory_fragments = data.get("memory_fragments")
785:     if not isinstance(memory_fragments, dict):
786:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_index.json memory_fragments must be object")
787:         return
788: 
789:     total = memory_fragments.get("total")
790:     categories = memory_fragments.get("categories")
791:     if not isinstance(total, int) or total <= 0:
792:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_index.json memory_fragments.total must be int > 0")
793:     if not isinstance(categories, list) or not categories:
794:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_index.json memory_fragments.categories must be non-empty array")
795: 
796: 
797: def _validate_narrative_content(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
798:     transitions = data.get("chapter_transitions")
799:     events = data.get("chapter_events")
800:     endings = data.get("endings")
801:     route_styles = data.get("route_styles")
802: 
803:     if not isinstance(transitions, dict):
804:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_content.json chapter_transitions must be object")
805:     else:
806:         for chapter_key in ("chapter_1", "chapter_2", "chapter_3"):
807:             row = transitions.get(chapter_key)
808:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
809:                 _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json missing transition '{chapter_key}'")
810:                 continue
811:             choices = row.get("choices")
812:             if not isinstance(choices, list) or len(choices) < 2:
813:                 _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}.choices must have at least 2 entries")
814: 
815:     if not isinstance(events, dict):
816:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_content.json chapter_events must be object")
817:     else:
818:         for chapter_key in ("chapter_1", "chapter_2", "chapter_3", "chapter_4"):
819:             rows = events.get(chapter_key)
820:             if not isinstance(rows, list) or not rows:
821:                 _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json chapter_events.{chapter_key} must be non-empty array")
822:                 continue
823:             for i, event_row in enumerate(rows):
824:                 if not isinstance(event_row, dict):
825:                     _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}] must be object")
826:                     continue
827: 
828:                 for route_key in ("weight_if_route_vanguard", "weight_if_route_raider"):
829:                     route_weight = _to_float(event_row.get(route_key))
830:                     if route_weight is None or route_weight <= 0.0 or route_weight > 3.0:
831:                         _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}].{route_key} must be within (0, 3]")
832: 
833:                 choices = event_row.get("choices")
834:                 if not isinstance(choices, list) or len(choices) < 2:
835:                     _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}] choices must have at least 2 entries")
836:                     continue
837:                 for j, choice in enumerate(choices):
838:                     if not isinstance(choice, dict):
839:                         _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}].choices[{j}] must be object")
840:                         continue

842:                     if effect is None:
843:                         continue
844:                     if not isinstance(effect, dict):
845:                         _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}].choices[{j}].chapter_effect must be object")
846:                         continue
847:                     if not isinstance(effect.get("duration_rooms"), int) or int(effect.get("duration_rooms", 0)) < 1:
848:                         _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}].choices[{j}] chapter_effect.duration_rooms must be >= 1")

851:                         _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json {chapter_key}[{i}].choices[{j}] chapter_effect.effects must be non-empty object")
852: 
853:     if not isinstance(route_styles, dict) or not route_styles:
854:         _add_error(errors, "narrative_content.json route_styles must be non-empty object")
855:     else:
856:         expected_styles = ("neutral", "vanguard", "raider")

860:                 _add_error(errors, f"narrative_content.json route_styles.{style_id} must be object")
861:                 continue

863:             event_weight_mult = _to_float(style_row.get("event_weight_mult"))

158:             _shift_codex_category(1)
159:             return
160:         if event is InputEventKey:
161:             var key_event: InputEventKey = event
162:             if key_event.pressed and not key_event.echo:
163:                 if key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_3 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_KP_3 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_Q:
164:                     _shift_codex_entry(-1)
165:                     return
166:                 if key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_4 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_KP_4 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_R:
167:                     _shift_codex_entry(1)
168:                     return
169:                 if key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_5 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_KP_5:
170:                     _cycle_codex_stats_source_filter(1)
171:                     return
172:                 if key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_6 or key_event.physical_keycode == KEY_KP_6:
173:                     _cycle_codex_stats_chapter_filter(1)
174:                     return
175: 
176:     if _settings_overlay == null or not _settings_overlay.visible:
177:         return
178: 
179:     if (event.is_action_pressed("pause") or event.is_action_pressed("interact")) and not _is_settings_capture_active():
180:         _close_settings_overlay()
181: 
182: 
183: func _on_start_pressed() -> void:
184:     if _codex_overlay != null and _codex_overlay.visible:
185:         _close_codex_overlay()
186:         return
187:     if _settings_overlay != null and _settings_overlay.visible:
188:         _close_settings_overlay()
189:         return
190:     if not _apply_selected_character():
191:         _shop_message = "Selected character is locked"
192:         _refresh_meta_text()
193:         return
194:     SceneManager.go_to_game_world()
195: 
196: 
197: func _on_quit_pressed() -> void:
198:     if _codex_overlay != null and _codex_overlay.visible:
199:         _close_codex_overlay()
200:         return
201:     if _settings_overlay != null and _settings_overlay.visible:
202:         _close_settings_overlay()
203:         return
204:     get_tree().quit()
205:

209:     _shop_message = "Meta data reset"
210:     _refresh_meta_text()
