299: func _refresh_meta_text() -> void:
300:     var meta: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_meta_data()
301:     var last_run: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_last_run()
302:     var unlocked_achievements: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_achievements()
303:     var unlocked_endings: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_endings()
304:     var achievements_config: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("achievements", {})
305:     var total_achievements: int = 0
306:     var rows: Variant = achievements_config.get("achievements", [])
307:     if rows is Array:
308:         total_achievements = (rows as Array).size()
309: 
310:     _meta_value.text = str(meta.get("meta_currency", 0))
311:     _refresh_character_preview()
312:     _run_value.text = "%d runs / %d kills" % [
313:         int(meta.get("total_runs", 0)),
314:         int(meta.get("total_kills", 0))
315:     ]
316:     _best_value.text = "Highest Room %d | Best Lv %d | Victories %d" % [
317:         int(meta.get("highest_room", 1)),
318:         int(meta.get("best_level", 1)),
319:         int(meta.get("total_victories", 0))
320:     ]
321:     _progress_value.text = "Achievements %d/%d | Endings %d/3" % [
322:         unlocked_achievements.size(),
323:         total_achievements,
324:         unlocked_endings.size()
325:     ]
326:     _refresh_upgrade_buttons()
327:     _refresh_achievement_list()
328:     _refresh_fragment_review()
329:     _refresh_ending_review()
330:     _refresh_codex_overlay()
331: 
332:     if last_run.is_empty():
333:         _last_run_value.text = "No run record yet"
334:         return
335: 
336:     var ending_text: String = str(last_run.get("ending_id", ""))
337:     if ending_text == "":
338:         ending_text = "-"
339:     var new_achievements_count: int = 0
340:     var new_achievements_var: Variant = last_run.get("new_achievements", [])
341:     if new_achievements_var is Array:
342:         new_achievements_count = (new_achievements_var as Array).size()
343: 
344:     _last_run_value.text = "Last: %s | Rooms %d | Kills %d | Lv %d | Meta +%d | Ending %s | NewAch %d" % [
345:         str(last_run.get("outcome", "death")).to_upper(),
346:         int(last_run.get("rooms_cleared", 0)),
347:         int(last_run.get("kills", 0)),
348:         int(last_run.get("level_reached", 1)),
349:         int(last_run.get("meta_reward", 0)),
350:         ending_text,
351:         new_achievements_count
352:     ]
353: 
354: 
355: func _try_buy_upgrade(index: int) -> void:
356:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_meta_upgrade_rows()
357:     if index < 0 or index >= rows.size():
358:         return
359: 
360:     var row: Dictionary = rows[index]
361:     var upgrade_id: String = str(row.get("id", ""))
362:     var title: String = str(row.get("title", upgrade_id))
363:     var result: Dictionary = SaveManager.purchase_upgrade(upgrade_id)
364: 
365:     if bool(result.get("ok", false)):
366:         _shop_message = "Purchased %s -> Lv.%d" % [title, int(result.get("new_level", 0))]
367:     else:
368:         var reason: String = str(result.get("reason", "failed"))
369:         if reason == "not_enough_currency":
370:             _shop_message = "Need %d meta (have %d)" % [
371:                 int(result.get("cost", 0)),
372:                 int(result.get("currency", 0))
373:             ]
374:         elif reason == "max_level":
375:             _shop_message = "%s is already maxed" % title
376:         else:
377:             _shop_message = "Upgrade purchase failed"
378: 
379:     _refresh_meta_text()
380: 
381: 
382: func _refresh_upgrade_buttons() -> void:
383:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_meta_upgrade_rows()
384:     var buttons: Array[Button] = [
385:         _upgrade_1_button,
386:         _upgrade_2_button,
387:         _upgrade_3_button,
388:         _upgrade_4_button,
389:         _upgrade_5_button
390:     ]
391: 
392:     for i in range(buttons.size()):
393:         var button: Button = buttons[i]
394:         if i >= rows.size():
395:             button.visible = false
396:             continue
397: 
398:         button.visible = true
399:         var row: Dictionary = rows[i]
400:         var upgrade_id: String = str(row.get("id", ""))
401:         var title: String = str(row.get("title", upgrade_id))
402:         var max_level: int = int(row.get("max_level", 1))
403:         var level: int = SaveManager.get_upgrade_level(upgrade_id)
404:         var cost: int = SaveManager.get_upgrade_cost(upgrade_id)
405: 
406:         if level >= max_level or cost < 0:
407:             button.text = "%d) %s Lv.%d/%d (MAX)" % [i + 1, title, level, max_level]
408:             button.disabled = true
409:         else:
410:             button.text = "%d) %s Lv.%d/%d  Cost:%d" % [i + 1, title, level, max_level, cost]
411:             button.disabled = false
412: 
413:     if _shop_message == "":
414:         _shop_message_value.text = "Meta Shop: buy permanent upgrades"
415:     else:
416:         _shop_message_value.text = _shop_message
417: 
418: 
419: func _refresh_achievement_list() -> void:
420:     var rows_var: Variant = ConfigManager.get_config("achievements", {}).get("achievements", [])
421:     var rows: Array = []
422:     if rows_var is Array:
423:         rows = rows_var
424: 
425:     var unlocked: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_achievements()
426:     var lines: Array[String] = []
427:     lines.append("Achievements:")
428:     for item: Variant in rows:
429:         if not (item is Dictionary):
430:             continue
431:         var row: Dictionary = item
432:         var ach_id: String = str(row.get("id", ""))
433:         var title: String = str(row.get("title", ach_id))
434:         var mark: String = "[ ]"
435:         if unlocked.has(ach_id):
436:             mark = "[x]"
437:         lines.append("%s %s" % [mark, title])
438: 
439:     var endings: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_endings()
440:     lines.append("Endings:")
441:     lines.append("%s Redeem" % ("[x]" if endings.has("nar_ending_redeem") else "[ ]"))
442:     lines.append("%s Fall" % ("[x]" if endings.has("nar_ending_fall") else "[ ]"))
443:     lines.append("%s Balance" % ("[x]" if endings.has("nar_ending_balance") else "[ ]"))
444: 
445:     var unlocked_fragments: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_fragments()
446:     var fragment_rows_var: Variant = ConfigManager.get_config("narrative_content", {}).get("memory_fragments", {})
447:     var fragment_rows: Dictionary = {}
448:     if fragment_rows_var is Dictionary:
449:         fragment_rows = fragment_rows_var
450: 
451:     lines.append("Memory Fragments:")
452:     lines.append("Unlocked %d / %d" % [unlocked_fragments.size(), fragment_rows.size()])
453:     for item: Variant in unlocked_fragments:
454:         var fragment_id: String = str(item)
455:         var fragment_title: String = fragment_id
456:         var row_var: Variant = fragment_rows.get(fragment_id, {})
457:         if row_var is Dictionary:
458:             fragment_title = str((row_var as Dictionary).get("title", fragment_id))
459:         lines.append("[x] %s" % fragment_title)
460: 
461:     _achievement_list_value.text = "\n".join(PackedStringArray(lines))
462: 
463: 
464: func _get_meta_upgrade_rows() -> Array[Dictionary]:
465:     var config: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("meta_upgrades", {})
466:     var rows_var: Variant = config.get("upgrades", [])
467:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = []
468:     if rows_var is Array:
469:         for item: Variant in rows_var:
470:             if item is Dictionary:
471:                 rows.append(item)
472:     return rows
473: 
474: 
475: func _get_character_rows() -> Array[Dictionary]:
476:     var config: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("characters", {})
477:     var rows_var: Variant = config.get("characters", [])
478:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = []
479:     if rows_var is Array:
480:         for item: Variant in rows_var:
481:             if item is Dictionary:
482:                 rows.append(item)
483:     return rows
484: 
485: 
486: func _get_default_character_id() -> String:
487:     var config: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("characters", {})
488:     return str(config.get("default_character_id", "char_knight"))
489: 
490: 
491: func _sync_character_cursor_from_save() -> void:
492:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
493:     if rows.is_empty():
494:         _character_cursor = 0
495:         return
496: 
497:     var selected_id: String = _get_default_character_id()
498:     if SaveManager != null and SaveManager.has_method("get_selected_character_id"):
499:         selected_id = SaveManager.get_selected_character_id()
500:     if selected_id == "":
501:         selected_id = _get_default_character_id()
502: 
503:     var matched_index: int = -1
504:     for i in range(rows.size()):
505:         var row: Dictionary = rows[i]
506:         if str(row.get("id", "")) == selected_id and _is_character_row_unlocked(row):
507:             matched_index = i
508:             break
509: 
510:     if matched_index >= 0:
511:         _character_cursor = matched_index
512:         _apply_selected_character()
513:         return
514: 
515:     var fallback_index: int = _get_first_unlocked_character_index(rows)
516:     if fallback_index >= 0:
517:         _character_cursor = fallback_index
518:         _apply_selected_character()
519:         return
520: 
521:     _character_cursor = 0
522: 
523: 
524: func _refresh_character_preview() -> void:
525:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
526:     if rows.is_empty():
527:         if _character_prev_button != null:
528:             _character_prev_button.disabled = true
529:         if _character_next_button != null:
530:             _character_next_button.disabled = true
531:         _character_name_value.text = "Character: Missing config"
532:         _character_desc_value.text = "No character definitions found in data/balance/characters.json"
533:         _character_stats_value.text = "-"
534:         _character_trait_value.text = "Trait: -"
535:         _character_unlock_value.text = "Status: -"
536:         _character_unlock_value.modulate = Color(1, 1, 1, 1)
537:         return
538: 
539:     _character_cursor = posmod(_character_cursor, rows.size())
540:     if _character_prev_button != null:
541:         _character_prev_button.disabled = rows.size() <= 1
542:     if _character_next_button != null:
543:         _character_next_button.disabled = rows.size() <= 1
544: 
545:     var row: Dictionary = rows[_character_cursor]
546:     var is_unlocked: bool = _is_character_row_unlocked(row)
547:     var char_name: String = str(row.get("name", row.get("id", "Unknown")))
548:     var char_desc: String = str(row.get("description", ""))
549:     var lock_suffix: String = ""
550:     if not is_unlocked:
551:         lock_suffix = " [LOCKED]"
552:     _character_name_value.text = "Character (%d/%d): %s%s" % [_character_cursor + 1, rows.size(), char_name, lock_suffix]
553:     _character_desc_value.text = char_desc
554:     _character_stats_value.text = "HP %d | SPD %d | DMG %.1f | ATK %.2fs | ARM %.0f%% | CRIT %.0f%%" % [
555:         int(row.get("max_hp", 100)),
556:         int(row.get("move_speed", 180)),
557:         float(row.get("base_damage", 12.0)),
558:         float(row.get("attack_interval", 0.45)),
559:         float(row.get("armor", 0.0)) * 100.0,
560:         float(row.get("crit_chance", 0.08)) * 100.0
561:     ]
562:     _character_stats_value.text += "\nWeapon: %s" % _get_character_weapon_style_text(row)
563:     var trait_name: String = str(row.get("trait_name", "No Trait"))
564:     var trait_desc: String = str(row.get("trait_desc", "No additional effects."))
565:     _character_trait_value.text = "Trait: %s — %s" % [trait_name, trait_desc]
566:     if is_unlocked:
567:         _character_unlock_value.text = "Status: Unlocked"
568:         _character_unlock_value.modulate = Color(0.60, 0.95, 0.66, 1.0)
569:     else:
570:         _character_unlock_value.text = "Status: Locked — %s" % _get_character_unlock_hint(row)
571:         _character_unlock_value.modulate = Color(1.0, 0.62, 0.62, 1.0)
572:     _apply_selected_character()
573: 
574: 
575: func _apply_selected_character() -> bool:
576:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
577:     if rows.is_empty():
578:         return false
579:     _character_cursor = posmod(_character_cursor, rows.size())
580:     var row: Dictionary = rows[_character_cursor]
581:     if not _is_character_row_unlocked(row):
582:         return false
583: 
584:     var selected_id: String = str(row.get("id", _get_default_character_id()))
585:     if selected_id == "":
586:         selected_id = _get_default_character_id()
587:     GameManager.selected_character_id = selected_id
588:     if SaveManager != null and SaveManager.has_method("set_selected_character_id"):
589:         SaveManager.set_selected_character_id(selected_id)
590:     var profile_var: Variant = row.get("weapon_profile", {})
591:     if profile_var is Dictionary and SaveManager != null and SaveManager.has_method("unlock_codex_entry"):
592:             var style_id: String = str((profile_var as Dictionary).get("projectile_style", "")).strip_edges()
593:             if style_id != "":
594:                 if not style_id.begins_with("wpn_"):
595:                     style_id = "wpn_%s" % style_id
596:                 SaveManager.unlock_codex_entry("weapons", style_id, "character_select", "global")
597:     return true
598: 
599: 
600: func _get_first_unlocked_character_index(rows: Array[Dictionary]) -> int:
601:     for i in range(rows.size()):
602:         if _is_character_row_unlocked(rows[i]):
603:             return i
604:     return -1
605: 
606: 
607: func _is_character_row_unlocked(row: Dictionary) -> bool:
608:     var unlock_type: String = str(row.get("unlock_type", "default"))
609:     var unlock_value: String = str(row.get("unlock_value", ""))
610:     match unlock_type:
611:         "default":
612:             return true
613:         "achievement":
614:             return SaveManager.get_unlocked_achievements().has(unlock_value)
615:         "ending":
616:             return SaveManager.get_unlocked_endings().has(unlock_value)
617:         "meta_runs":
618:             var needed_runs: int = int(unlock_value)
619:             return int(SaveManager.get_meta_data().get("total_runs", 0)) >= needed_runs
620:         _:
621:             return true
622: 
623: 
624: func _get_character_unlock_hint(row: Dictionary) -> String:
625:     var custom_hint: String = str(row.get("unlock_desc", ""))
626:     if custom_hint != "":
627:         return custom_hint
628: 
629:     var unlock_type: String = str(row.get("unlock_type", "default"))
630:     var unlock_value: String = str(row.get("unlock_value", ""))
631:     match unlock_type:
632:         "default":
633:             return "Default unlocked"
634:         "achievement":
635:             return "Unlock achievement: %s" % unlock_value
636:         "ending":
637:             return "Unlock ending: %s" % unlock_value
638:         "meta_runs":
639:             return "Complete %s runs" % unlock_value
640:         _:
641:             return "Unavailable"
642: 
643: 
644: func _get_character_weapon_style_text(row: Dictionary) -> String:
645:     var profile_var: Variant = row.get("weapon_profile", {})
646:     if not (profile_var is Dictionary):
647:         return "Single Shot"
648: 
649:     var profile: Dictionary = profile_var
650:     var mode: String = str(profile.get("mode", "single")).to_lower()
651:     var count: int = max(1, int(profile.get("projectile_count", 1)))
652:     var hits: int = max(1, int(profile.get("projectile_hits", 1)))
653:     var spread: float = maxf(0.0, float(profile.get("spread_angle_deg", 0.0)))
654:     var jitter: float = maxf(0.0, float(profile.get("spread_jitter_deg", 0.0)))
655:     var style: String = str(profile.get("projectile_style", "default"))
656: 
657:     if mode == "spread":
658:         return "Spread x%d (%.0f deg +/- %.1f), Hits %d, Style %s" % [count, spread, jitter, hits, style]
659:     return "Single x%d, Hits %d, Style %s" % [count, hits, style]
660: 
661: 
662: func _open_codex_overlay() -> void:
663:     if _codex_overlay == null:
664:         return
665:     _codex_overlay.visible = true
666:     _codex_entry_index = 0
667:     _refresh_codex_overlay()
668: 
669: 
670: func _close_codex_overlay() -> void:
671:     if _codex_overlay == null:
672:         return
673:     _codex_overlay.visible = false
674: 
675: 
676: func _shift_codex_category(delta: int) -> void:
677:     if CODEX_CATEGORIES.is_empty():
678:         return
679:     _codex_category_index = posmod(_codex_category_index + delta, CODEX_CATEGORIES.size())
680:     _codex_entry_index = 0
681:     _refresh_codex_overlay()
682: 
683: 
684: func _shift_codex_entry(delta: int) -> void:
685:     var category: String = CODEX_CATEGORIES[posmod(_codex_category_index, CODEX_CATEGORIES.size())]
686:     var catalog: Array[Dictionary] = _build_codex_catalog(category)
687:     if catalog.is_empty():
688:         _codex_entry_index = 0
689:         _refresh_codex_overlay()
690:         return
691:     _codex_entry_index = posmod(_codex_entry_index + delta, catalog.size())
692:     _refresh_codex_overlay()
693: 
694: 
695: func _refresh_codex_overlay() -> void:
696:     if _codex_title == null or _codex_content == null:
697:         return
698:     if CODEX_CATEGORIES.is_empty():
699:         _codex_title.text = "Codex"
700:         _codex_content.text = "No codex categories configured"
701:         return
702: 
703:     _codex_category_index = posmod(_codex_category_index, CODEX_CATEGORIES.size())
704:     var category: String = CODEX_CATEGORIES[_codex_category_index]
705:     var codex: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_codex()
706:     var rows: Array[String] = []
707:     if codex.has(category):
708:         rows = _as_string_array(codex.get(category, []))
709: 
710:     var catalog: Array[Dictionary] = _build_codex_catalog(category)
711:     var unlocked_set: Dictionary = _to_string_set(rows)
712:     var unlocked_count: int = 0
713:     for item: Dictionary in catalog:
714:         if unlocked_set.has(str(item.get("id", ""))):
715:             unlocked_count += 1
716: 
717:     var category_name: String = str(CODEX_CATEGORY_NAMES.get(category, category.capitalize()))
718:     _codex_title.text = "Codex [%d/%d] - %s (%d/%d)" % [
719:         _codex_category_index + 1,
720:         CODEX_CATEGORIES.size(),
721:         category_name,
722:         unlocked_count,
723:         max(1, catalog.size())
724:     ]
725: 
726:     if _codex_prev_button != null:
727:         _codex_prev_button.disabled = CODEX_CATEGORIES.size() <= 1
728:     if _codex_next_button != null:
729:         _codex_next_button.disabled = CODEX_CATEGORIES.size() <= 1
730: 
731:     if not catalog.is_empty():
732:         _codex_entry_index = posmod(_codex_entry_index, catalog.size())
733:     else:
734:         _codex_entry_index = 0
735: 
736:     if _codex_entry_prev_button != null:
737:         _codex_entry_prev_button.disabled = catalog.size() <= 1
738:     if _codex_entry_next_button != null:
739:         _codex_entry_next_button.disabled = catalog.size() <= 1
740: 
741:     var lines: Array[String] = []
742:     lines.append("Unlocked %d / %d" % [unlocked_count, max(1, catalog.size())])
743:     if catalog.is_empty() and rows.is_empty():
744:         lines.append("-")
745:     else:
746:         for i in range(catalog.size()):
747:             var item: Dictionary = catalog[i]
748:             var entry_id: String = str(item.get("id", ""))
749:             var entry_name: String = str(item.get("name", _get_codex_entry_name(category, entry_id)))
750:             var hint: String = str(item.get("hint", ""))
751:             var mark: String = "[x]"
752:             if not unlocked_set.has(entry_id):
753:                 mark = "[ ]"
754:             var pointer: String = "  "
755:             if i == _codex_entry_index:
756:                 pointer = "> "
757:             var row_text: String = "%s%s %s" % [pointer, mark, entry_name]
758:             if mark == "[ ]" and hint != "":
759:                 row_text += "  (%s)" % hint
760:             lines.append(row_text)
761: 
762:         for entry_id: String in rows:
763:             if _catalog_has_entry(catalog, entry_id):
764:                 continue
765:             lines.append("[x] %s" % _get_codex_entry_name(category, entry_id))
766: 
767:     _codex_content.text = "\n".join(PackedStringArray(lines))
768:     _codex_detail.text = _build_codex_detail_text(category, catalog, unlocked_set)
769:     _refresh_codex_stats_panel()
770: 
771: 
772: func _refresh_codex_stats_panel() -> void:
773:     if _codex_stats_value == null:
774:         return
775: 
776:     var codex: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_codex()
777:     var lines: Array[String] = []
778:     lines.append("Codex Statistics")
779: 
780:     var global_total: int = 0
781:     var global_unlocked: int = 0
782: 
783:     for category: String in CODEX_CATEGORIES:
784:         var catalog: Array[Dictionary] = _build_codex_catalog(category)
785:         var total: int = catalog.size()
786:         var unlocked_rows: Array[String] = _as_string_array(codex.get(category, []))
787:         var unlocked_set: Dictionary = _to_string_set(unlocked_rows)
788:         var unlocked: int = 0
789:         for row: Dictionary in catalog:
790:             var entry_id: String = str(row.get("id", ""))
791:             if unlocked_set.has(entry_id):
792:                 unlocked += 1
793: 
794:         global_total += total
795:         global_unlocked += unlocked
796: 
797:         var category_name: String = str(CODEX_CATEGORY_NAMES.get(category, category.capitalize()))
798:         lines.append("- %s %d/%d %s" % [
799:             category_name,
800:             unlocked,
801:             max(1, total),
802:             _build_progress_bar(unlocked, total, 14)
803:         ])
804: 
805:     lines.append("Global %d/%d %s" % [
806:         global_unlocked,
807:         max(1, global_total),
808:         _build_progress_bar(global_unlocked, global_total, 18)
809:     ])
810: 
811:     lines.append("Chapter Completion:")
812:     var chapter_progress: Array[Dictionary] = _build_chapter_completion_rows(codex)
813:     for row: Dictionary in chapter_progress:
814:         lines.append("- %s %d/%d %s" % [
815:             str(row.get("label", "Global")),
816:             int(row.get("unlocked", 0)),
817:             max(1, int(row.get("total", 0))),
818:             _build_progress_bar(int(row.get("unlocked", 0)), int(row.get("total", 0)), 12)
819:         ])
820: 
821:     var source_filter: Dictionary = _get_codex_source_filter_row()
822:     var chapter_filter: Dictionary = _get_codex_chapter_filter_row()
823:     var source_filter_id: String = str(source_filter.get("id", "all"))
824:     var chapter_filter_id: String = str(chapter_filter.get("id", "all"))
825: 
826:     if _codex_stats_source_button != null:
827:         _codex_stats_source_button.text = "Source: %s (5)" % str(source_filter.get("label", "All Sources"))
828:     if _codex_stats_chapter_button != null:
829:         _codex_stats_chapter_button.text = "Chapter: %s (6)" % str(chapter_filter.get("label", "All Chapters"))
830: 
831:     lines.append("Recent Unlocks (last 5):")
832:     lines.append("Filters -> Source: %s | Chapter: %s" % [
833:         str(source_filter.get("label", "All Sources")),
834:         str(chapter_filter.get("label", "All Chapters"))
835:     ])
836: 
837:     var filtered_recent: Array[Dictionary] = []
838:     var recent_rows: Array[Dictionary] = SaveManager.get_codex_recent_unlocks(64)
839:     for row: Dictionary in recent_rows:
840:         if source_filter_id != "all":
841:             var row_source: String = str(row.get("source", ""))
842:             if row_source != source_filter_id:
843:                 continue
844: 
845:         if chapter_filter_id != "all":
846:             var row_category: String = str(row.get("category", ""))
847:             var row_entry_id: String = str(row.get("entry_id", ""))
848:             var row_chapter: String = _normalize_codex_chapter_id(str(row.get("chapter_id", "")))
849:             if row_chapter == "":
850:                 row_chapter = _resolve_codex_entry_chapter(row_category, row_entry_id)
851:             if row_chapter != chapter_filter_id:
852:                 continue
853: 
854:         filtered_recent.append(row)
855:         if filtered_recent.size() >= 5:
856:             break
857: 
858:     if filtered_recent.is_empty():
859:         lines.append("- No entries match current filters")
860:     else:
861:         for row: Dictionary in filtered_recent:
862:             var category: String = str(row.get("category", ""))
863:             var entry_id: String = str(row.get("entry_id", ""))
864:             var source: String = str(row.get("source", ""))
865:             var discovered_at: String = str(row.get("discovered_at", ""))
866:             var chapter_id: String = _normalize_codex_chapter_id(str(row.get("chapter_id", "")))
867:             if chapter_id == "":
868:                 chapter_id = _resolve_codex_entry_chapter(category, entry_id)
869:             var category_name: String = str(CODEX_CATEGORY_NAMES.get(category, category.capitalize()))
870:             var entry_name: String = _get_codex_entry_name(category, entry_id)
871:             var when_text: String = discovered_at
872:             if when_text == "":
873:                 when_text = "time-unknown"
874:             lines.append("- [%s] %s | %s | %s | %s" % [
875:                 category_name,
876:                 entry_name,
877:                 _prettify_source(source),
878:                 _prettify_chapter_id(chapter_id),
879:                 when_text
880:             ])
881: 
882:     _codex_stats_value.text = "\n".join(PackedStringArray(lines))
883: 
884: 
885: func _cycle_codex_stats_source_filter(delta: int) -> void:
886:     if CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS.is_empty():
887:         return
888:     _codex_stats_source_filter_index = posmod(_codex_stats_source_filter_index + delta, CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS.size())
889:     _persist_codex_stats_filters()
890:     _refresh_codex_stats_panel()
891: 
892: 
893: func _cycle_codex_stats_chapter_filter(delta: int) -> void:
894:     if CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS.is_empty():
895:         return
896:     _codex_stats_chapter_filter_index = posmod(_codex_stats_chapter_filter_index + delta, CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS.size())
897:     _persist_codex_stats_filters()
898:     _refresh_codex_stats_panel()
899: 
900: 
901: func _sync_codex_stats_filters_from_save() -> void:
902:     if SaveManager == null or not SaveManager.has_method("get_codex_stats_filters"):
903:         return
904: 
905:     var filters: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_codex_stats_filters()
906:     var source_id: String = str(filters.get("source", "all"))
907:     var chapter_id: String = str(filters.get("chapter", "all"))
908: 
909:     _codex_stats_source_filter_index = _find_filter_index(CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS, source_id)
910:     _codex_stats_chapter_filter_index = _find_filter_index(CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS, chapter_id)
911: 
912: 
913: func _persist_codex_stats_filters() -> void:
914:     if SaveManager == null or not SaveManager.has_method("set_codex_stats_filters"):
915:         return
916: 
917:     var source_row: Dictionary = _get_codex_source_filter_row()
918:     var chapter_row: Dictionary = _get_codex_chapter_filter_row()
919:     SaveManager.set_codex_stats_filters(
920:         str(source_row.get("id", "all")),
921:         str(chapter_row.get("id", "all"))
922:     )
923: 
924: 
925: func _find_filter_index(rows: Array[Dictionary], target_id: String) -> int:
926:     if rows.is_empty():
927:         return 0
928:     for i in range(rows.size()):
929:         if str(rows[i].get("id", "")) == target_id:
930:             return i
931:     return 0
932: 
933: 
934: func _get_codex_source_filter_row() -> Dictionary:
935:     if CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS.is_empty():
936:         return {"id": "all", "label": "All Sources"}
937:     _codex_stats_source_filter_index = posmod(_codex_stats_source_filter_index, CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS.size())
938:     return CODEX_SOURCE_FILTERS[_codex_stats_source_filter_index]
939: 
940: 
941: func _get_codex_chapter_filter_row() -> Dictionary:
942:     if CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS.is_empty():
943:         return {"id": "all", "label": "All Chapters"}
944:     _codex_stats_chapter_filter_index = posmod(_codex_stats_chapter_filter_index, CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS.size())
945:     return CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS[_codex_stats_chapter_filter_index]
946: 
947: 
948: func _resolve_codex_entry_chapter(category: String, entry_id: String) -> String:
949:     if SaveManager != null and SaveManager.has_method("get_codex_entry_meta"):
950:         var meta: Dictionary = SaveManager.get_codex_entry_meta(category, entry_id)
951:         var chapter_from_meta: String = _normalize_codex_chapter_id(str(meta.get("chapter_id", "")))
952:         if chapter_from_meta != "":
953:             return chapter_from_meta
954: 
955:     match category:
956:         "enemies":
957:             match entry_id:
958:                 "boss_rock_colossus":
959:                     return "chapter_1"
960:                 "boss_flame_lord":
961:                     return "chapter_2"
962:                 "boss_frost_king":
963:                     return "chapter_3"
964:                 "boss_void_lord":
965:                     return "chapter_4"
966:                 _:
967:                     return "global"
968:         "accessories":
969:             match entry_id:
970:                 "acc_heart_of_mine":
971:                     return "chapter_1"
972:                 "acc_flame_core":
973:                     return "chapter_2"
974:                 "acc_zero_mark":
975:                     return "chapter_3"
976:                 "acc_void_eye":
977:                     return "chapter_4"
978:                 _:
979:                     return "global"
980:         _:
981:             return "global"
982: 
983: 
984: func _build_chapter_completion_rows(codex: Dictionary) -> Array[Dictionary]:
985:     var chapter_order: Array[String] = []
986:     for row: Dictionary in CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS:
987:         var chapter_id: String = str(row.get("id", ""))
988:         if chapter_id == "" or chapter_id == "all":
989:             continue
990:         chapter_order.append(chapter_id)
991: 
992:     var totals: Dictionary = {}
993:     var unlocked: Dictionary = {}
994:     for chapter_id: String in chapter_order:
995:         totals[chapter_id] = 0
996:         unlocked[chapter_id] = 0
997: 
998:     for category: String in CODEX_CATEGORIES:
999:         var catalog: Array[Dictionary] = _build_codex_catalog(category)
1000:         if catalog.is_empty():
1001:             continue
1002: 
1003:         var unlocked_rows: Array[String] = _as_string_array(codex.get(category, []))
1004:         var unlocked_set: Dictionary = _to_string_set(unlocked_rows)
1005:         for item: Dictionary in catalog:
1006:             var entry_id: String = str(item.get("id", ""))
1007:             var chapter_id: String = _resolve_codex_entry_chapter(category, entry_id)
1008:             if not totals.has(chapter_id):
1009:                 chapter_id = "global"
1010:             totals[chapter_id] = int(totals.get(chapter_id, 0)) + 1
1011:             if unlocked_set.has(entry_id):
1012:                 unlocked[chapter_id] = int(unlocked.get(chapter_id, 0)) + 1
1013: 
1014:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = []
1015:     for chapter_id: String in chapter_order:
1016:         rows.append({
1017:             "id": chapter_id,
1018:             "label": _prettify_chapter_id(chapter_id),
1019:             "unlocked": int(unlocked.get(chapter_id, 0)),
1020:             "total": int(totals.get(chapter_id, 0))
1021:         })
1022:     return rows
1023: 
1024: 
1025: func _normalize_codex_chapter_id(value: String) -> String:
1026:     var chapter_id: String = value.strip_edges().to_lower()
1027:     if chapter_id == "":
1028:         return ""
1029:     for row: Dictionary in CODEX_CHAPTER_FILTERS:
1030:         if str(row.get("id", "")) == chapter_id:
1031:             return chapter_id
1032:     return ""
1033: 
1034: 
1035: func _prettify_chapter_id(chapter_id: String) -> String:
1036:     match chapter_id:
1037:         "chapter_1":
1038:             return "Chapter 1"
1039:         "chapter_2":
1040:             return "Chapter 2"
1041:         "chapter_3":
1042:             return "Chapter 3"
1043:         "chapter_4":
1044:             return "Chapter 4"
1045:         _:
1046:             return "Global"
1047: 
1048: 
1049: func _build_progress_bar(current: int, total: int, width: int) -> String:
1050:     var safe_total: int = maxi(0, total)
1051:     var safe_current: int = clampi(current, 0, safe_total)
1052:     var safe_width: int = maxi(4, width)
1053:     var ratio: float = 0.0
1054:     if safe_total > 0:
1055:         ratio = float(safe_current) / float(safe_total)
1056:     var filled: int = int(round(ratio * safe_width))
1057:     filled = clampi(filled, 0, safe_width)
1058:     var bar: String = "["
1059:     bar += "#".repeat(filled)
1060:     bar += "-".repeat(safe_width - filled)
1061:     bar += "]"
1062:     return "%s %3d%%" % [bar, int(round(ratio * 100.0))]
1063: 
1064: 
1065: func _get_codex_entry_name(category: String, entry_id: String) -> String:
1066:     match category:
1067:         "characters":
1068:             return _lookup_character_name(entry_id)
1069:         "weapons":
1070:             return _lookup_weapon_name(entry_id)
1071:         "passives":
1072:             return str(PASSIVE_NAME_MAP.get(entry_id, _prettify_id(entry_id)))
1073:         "enemies":
1074:             return str(ENEMY_NAME_MAP.get(entry_id, _prettify_id(entry_id)))
1075:         "accessories":
1076:             return str(ACCESSORY_NAME_MAP.get(entry_id, _prettify_id(entry_id)))
1077:         _:
1078:             return _prettify_id(entry_id)
1079: 
1080: 
1081: func _build_codex_catalog(category: String) -> Array[Dictionary]:
1082:     var result: Array[Dictionary] = []
1083:     match category:
1084:         "characters":
1085:             var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
1086:             for row: Dictionary in rows:
1087:                 var character_id: String = str(row.get("id", "")).strip_edges()
1088:                 if character_id == "":
1089:                     continue
1090:                 result.append({
1091:                     "id": character_id,
1092:                     "name": str(row.get("name", _prettify_id(character_id))),
1093:                     "hint": _get_character_unlock_hint(row)
1094:                 })
1095:         "weapons":
1096:             var map: Dictionary = _build_weapon_name_map()
1097:             var keys: Array[String] = _sorted_string_keys(map)
1098:             for weapon_id: String in keys:
1099:                 result.append({
1100:                     "id": weapon_id,
1101:                     "name": str(map.get(weapon_id, _prettify_id(weapon_id))),
1102:                     "hint": "Unlock by selecting a character using this style"
1103:                 })
1104:         "passives":
1105:             var passive_keys: Array[String] = _sorted_string_keys(PASSIVE_NAME_MAP)
1106:             for passive_id: String in passive_keys:
1107:                 result.append({
1108:                     "id": passive_id,
1109:                     "name": str(PASSIVE_NAME_MAP.get(passive_id, passive_id)),
1110:                     "hint": "Choose this upgrade during level up"
1111:                 })
1112:         "enemies":
1113:             var enemy_keys: Array[String] = _sorted_string_keys(ENEMY_NAME_MAP)
1114:             for enemy_id: String in enemy_keys:
1115:                 result.append({
1116:                     "id": enemy_id,
1117:                     "name": str(ENEMY_NAME_MAP.get(enemy_id, enemy_id)),
1118:                     "hint": "Defeat this enemy type"
1119:                 })
1120:         "accessories":
1121:             var accessory_keys: Array[String] = _sorted_string_keys(ACCESSORY_NAME_MAP)
1122:             for accessory_id: String in accessory_keys:
1123:                 result.append({
1124:                     "id": accessory_id,
1125:                     "name": str(ACCESSORY_NAME_MAP.get(accessory_id, accessory_id)),
1126:                     "hint": "Acquire from boss/event drops"
1127:                 })
1128:         _:
1129:             pass
1130:     return result
1131: 
1132: 
1133: func _catalog_has_entry(catalog: Array[Dictionary], entry_id: String) -> bool:
1134:     for row: Dictionary in catalog:
1135:         if str(row.get("id", "")) == entry_id:
1136:             return true
1137:     return false
1138: 
1139: 
1140: func _sorted_string_keys(source: Dictionary) -> Array[String]:
1141:     var out: Array[String] = []
1142:     for key: Variant in source.keys():
1143:         out.append(str(key))
1144:     out.sort()
1145:     return out
1146: 
1147: 
1148: func _to_string_set(rows: Array[String]) -> Dictionary:
1149:     var set_map: Dictionary = {}
1150:     for row: String in rows:
1151:         set_map[row] = true
1152:     return set_map
1153: 
1154: 
1155: func _build_codex_detail_text(category: String, catalog: Array[Dictionary], unlocked_set: Dictionary) -> String:
1156:     if catalog.is_empty():
1157:         return "Entry Detail\n-"
1158: 
1159:     var item: Dictionary = catalog[_codex_entry_index]
1160:     var entry_id: String = str(item.get("id", ""))
1161:     var entry_name: String = str(item.get("name", entry_id))
1162:     var hint: String = str(item.get("hint", ""))
1163:     var unlocked: bool = unlocked_set.has(entry_id)
1164: 
1165:     var meta: Dictionary = {}
1166:     if SaveManager != null and SaveManager.has_method("get_codex_entry_meta"):
1167:         meta = SaveManager.get_codex_entry_meta(category, entry_id)
1168: 
1169:     var source: String = str(meta.get("source", ""))
1170:     var chapter_id: String = _normalize_codex_chapter_id(str(meta.get("chapter_id", "")))
1171:     var discovered_at: String = str(meta.get("discovered_at", ""))
1172:     var run_index: int = int(meta.get("run_index", 0))
1173: 
1174:     var lines: Array[String] = []
1175:     lines.append("Entry Detail")
1176:     lines.append("Name: %s" % entry_name)
1177:     lines.append("Status: %s" % ("Unlocked" if unlocked else "Locked"))
1178:     lines.append("ID: %s" % entry_id)
1179:     if hint != "":
1180:         lines.append("Hint: %s" % hint)
1181: 
1182:     if unlocked:
1183:         if source != "":
1184:             lines.append("Source: %s" % _prettify_source(source))
1185:         if chapter_id != "":
1186:             lines.append("Chapter: %s" % _prettify_chapter_id(chapter_id))
1187:         if discovered_at != "":
1188:             lines.append("First Discover: %s" % discovered_at)
1189:         if run_index > 0:
1190:             lines.append("Run Index: #%d" % run_index)
1191: 
1192:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(lines))
1193: 
1194: 
1195: func _prettify_source(source: String) -> String:
1196:     match source:
1197:         "default":
1198:             return "Default"
1199:         "profile_sync":
1200:             return "Profile Sync"
1201:         "character_select":
1202:             return "Character Selection"
1203:         "run_start":
1204:             return "Run Start"
1205:         "level_up_choice":
1206:             return "Level Up Choice"
1207:         "enemy_kill":
1208:             return "Enemy Defeat"
1209:         "accessory_pickup":
1210:             return "Accessory Pickup"
1211:         _:
1212:             return _prettify_id(source)
1213: 
1214: 
1215: func _lookup_character_name(character_id: String) -> String:
1216:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
1217:     for row: Dictionary in rows:
1218:         if str(row.get("id", "")) == character_id:
1219:             return str(row.get("name", character_id))
1220:     return _prettify_id(character_id)
1221: 
1222: 
1223: func _lookup_weapon_name(weapon_id: String) -> String:
1224:     var names: Dictionary = _build_weapon_name_map()
1225:     if names.has(weapon_id):
1226:         return str(names.get(weapon_id, weapon_id))
1227:     return _prettify_id(weapon_id)
1228: 
1229: 
1230: func _build_weapon_name_map() -> Dictionary:
1231:     var map: Dictionary = {}
1232:     var rows: Array[Dictionary] = _get_character_rows()
1233:     for row: Dictionary in rows:
1234:         var character_name: String = str(row.get("name", row.get("id", "Character")))
1235:         var profile_var: Variant = row.get("weapon_profile", {})
1236:         if profile_var is Dictionary:
1237:             var profile: Dictionary = profile_var
1238:             var style: String = str(profile.get("projectile_style", "default")).strip_edges()
1239:             if style != "":
1240:                 var weapon_key: String = style
1241:                 if not weapon_key.begins_with("wpn_"):
1242:                     weapon_key = "wpn_%s" % weapon_key
1243:                 map[weapon_key] = "%s Signature Weapon" % character_name
1244:     return map
1245: 
1246: 
1247: func _prettify_id(raw_id: String) -> String:
1248:     var text: String = raw_id
1249:     if text.begins_with("char_") or text.begins_with("wpn_") or text.begins_with("acc_") or text.begins_with("enemy_"):
1250:         var parts: PackedStringArray = text.split("_", false, 1)
1251:         if parts.size() == 2:
1252:             text = parts[1]
1253:     text = text.replace("_", " ")
1254:     return text.capitalize()
1255: 
1256: 
1257: func _as_string_array(value: Variant) -> Array[String]:
1258:     var out: Array[String] = []
1259:     if value is Array:
1260:         for item: Variant in value:
1261:             var row: String = str(item).strip_edges()
1262:             if row != "":
1263:                 out.append(row)
1264:     return out
1265: 
1266: 
1267: func _refresh_fragment_review() -> void:
1268:     var unlocked_fragments: Array[String] = SaveManager.get_unlocked_fragments()
1269:     if unlocked_fragments.is_empty():
1270:         _review_fragment_button.disabled = true
1271:         _fragment_review_value.text = "Memory Archive: no fragments unlocked yet"
1272:         _fragment_cursor = 0
1273:         return
1274: 
1275:     _review_fragment_button.disabled = false
1276:     _fragment_cursor = posmod(_fragment_cursor, unlocked_fragments.size())
1277:     var fragment_id: String = unlocked_fragments[_fragment_cursor]
1278: 
1279:     var fragment_rows_var: Variant = ConfigManager.get_config("narrative_content", {}).get("memory_fragments", {})
1280:     var row: Dictionary = {}
1281:     if fragment_rows_var is Dictionary:
1282:         var row_var: Variant = (fragment_rows_var as Dictionary).get(fragment_id, {})
1283:         if row_var is Dictionary:
1284:             row = row_var
1285: 
1286:     var title: String = str(row.get("title", fragment_id))
1287:     var text: String = str(row.get("text", "No memory text."))
1288:     _fragment_review_value.text = "Memory Archive (%d/%d)\n%s\n%s" % [
1289:         _fragment_cursor + 1,
1290:         unlocked_fragments.size(),
1291:         title,
1292:         text
1293:     ]
1294: 
1295: 
1296: func _refresh_ending_review() -> void:
1297:     var unlocked_endings: Array[String] = _get_ordered_unlocked_endings()
1298:     if unlocked_endings.is_empty():
1299:         _review_ending_button.disabled = true
1300:         _review_ending_button.text = "Review Next Ending"
1301:         _ending_review_value.text = "Ending Archive: no endings unlocked yet"
1302:         _ending_cursor = 0
1303:         _apply_ending_theme("")
1304:         return
1305: 
1306:     _review_ending_button.disabled = false
1307:     _ending_cursor = posmod(_ending_cursor, unlocked_endings.size())

\"ranged\"]\n+\n+    for chapter_id: String in expected_chapters:\n+        assert_true(chapter_map.has(chapter_id), \"Missing archetype map for %s\" % chapter_id)\n+        var chapter_row_var:     continue\n+        var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapter_row_var\n+        for enemy_type: String in expected_types:\n+            assert_true(chapter_row.has(enemy_type), \"Missing %s in %s\" % [enemy_type, chapter_id])\n+            var enemy_id: String = str(chapter_row.get(enemy_type, \"\"))\n+            assert_true(enemy_id.begins_with(\"enemy_\"), \"%s.%s should start with enemy_\" % [chapter_id, enemy_type])\n*** End Patch"
}

64:     var min_room_type_per_chapter: Dictionary = _normalize_room_type_mins(constraints.get("min_room_type_per_chapter", {}))
65:     if not max_room_type_per_chapter.has(ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE):
66:         max_room_type_per_chapter[ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE] = max_treasure_per_chapter
67:     if not min_room_type_per_chapter.has(ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE):
68:         min_room_type_per_chapter[ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE] = 0
69:     var avoid_shop_near_boss: bool = bool(constraints.get("avoid_shop_near_boss", true))
70:     var avoid_event_near_boss: bool = bool(constraints.get("avoid_event_near_boss", true))
71: 
72:     var rooms: Array[Dictionary] = []
73:     var room_plan_map: Dictionary = {}
74:     var history_types: Array[String] = []
75:     var room_type_count_by_chapter: Dictionary = {}
76:     var chapter_rollable_slots: Dictionary = _build_chapter_rollable_slots(chapter_order, chapters, room_count, fixed_room_types, avoid_shop_near_boss, avoid_event_near_boss)
77:     var chapter_slot_cursor: Dictionary = {}
78: 
79:     for room_index in range(1, room_count + 1):
80:         var chapter_id: String = _resolve_chapter_id(room_index, chapter_order, chapters)
81:         var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapters.get(chapter_id, {})
82:         var chapter_index: int = int(chapter_row.get("index", _fallback_chapter_index(chapter_id)))
83:         var boss_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("boss_room", -1))
84:         var intro_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("intro_room", int(chapter_row.get("start_room", 1))))
85:         var boss_id: String = ""
86: 
87:         var room_type: String = ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT
88:         if room_index == 1:
89:             room_type = ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT
90:         elif room_index == boss_room:
91:             room_type = ROOM_TYPE_BOSS
92:             boss_id = str(chapter_row.get("boss_id", "boss_unknown"))
93:         elif fixed_room_types.has(room_index):
94:             room_type = str(fixed_room_types.get(room_index, ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT))
95:         else:
96:             var chapter_weights: Dictionary = _build_chapter_weights(chapter_id, base_weights, chapter_weight_mult)
97:             var chapter_weights_before_min: Dictionary = chapter_weights.duplicate(true)
98:             var chapter_type_counter: Dictionary = {}
99:             var chapter_type_counter_var: Variant = room_type_count_by_chapter.get(chapter_id, {})
100:             if chapter_type_counter_var is Dictionary:
101:                 chapter_type_counter = chapter_type_counter_var
102: 
103:             for room_type_key in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
104:                 var cap_value: Variant = max_room_type_per_chapter.get(room_type_key, -1)
105:                 var cap_count: int = int(cap_value)
106:                 if cap_count < 0:
107:                     continue
108:                 var current_count: int = int(chapter_type_counter.get(room_type_key, 0))
109:                 if current_count >= cap_count:
110:                     chapter_weights[room_type_key] = 0.0
111:             if avoid_shop_near_boss and boss_room > 0 and room_index >= boss_room - 1:
112:                 chapter_weights[ROOM_TYPE_SHOP] = 0.0
113:             if avoid_event_near_boss and boss_room > 0 and room_index >= boss_room - 1:
114:                 chapter_weights[ROOM_TYPE_EVENT] = 0.0
115: 
116:             var chapter_slots: Array = []
117:             var chapter_slots_var: Variant = chapter_rollable_slots.get(chapter_id, [])
118:             if chapter_slots_var is Array:
119:                 chapter_slots = chapter_slots_var
120: 
121:             var slot_cursor: int = int(chapter_slot_cursor.get(chapter_id, 0))
122:             var deficits: Dictionary = {}
123:             for room_type_key in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
124:                 var min_required: int = int(min_room_type_per_chapter.get(room_type_key, 0))
125:                 if min_required <= 0:
126:                     continue
127:                 var current_count: int = int(chapter_type_counter.get(room_type_key, 0))
128:                 if current_count < min_required:
129:                     deficits[room_type_key] = min_required - current_count
130: 
131:             if not deficits.is_empty() and not chapter_slots.is_empty():
132:                 var forced_types: Array[String] = _collect_forced_min_types(deficits, chapter_slots, slot_cursor)
133:                 var remaining_slots: int = maxi(0, chapter_slots.size() - slot_cursor)
134:                 var required_slots: int = 0
135:                 for deficit_value in deficits.values():
136:                     required_slots += int(deficit_value)
137: 
138:                 var restrict_types: Array[String] = forced_types.duplicate(true)
139:                 if restrict_types.is_empty() and required_slots >= remaining_slots:
140:                     for deficit_key in deficits.keys():
141:                         restrict_types.append(str(deficit_key))
142: 
143:                 if not restrict_types.is_empty():
144:                     var restricted_total: float = 0.0
145:                     for room_type_key in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
146:                         if not restrict_types.has(room_type_key):
147:                             chapter_weights[room_type_key] = 0.0
148:                         else:
149:                             restricted_total += float(chapter_weights.get(room_type_key, 0.0))
150: 
151:                     if restricted_total <= 0.0:
152:                         chapter_weights = chapter_weights_before_min.duplicate(true)
153: 
154:             room_type = _roll_room_type(chapter_weights, history_types, max_consecutive_same_type)
155: 
156:             chapter_slot_cursor[chapter_id] = slot_cursor + 1
157: 
158:         if ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES.has(room_type):
159:             var chapter_type_counter: Dictionary = {}
160:             var chapter_type_counter_var: Variant = room_type_count_by_chapter.get(chapter_id, {})
161:             if chapter_type_counter_var is Dictionary:
162:                 chapter_type_counter = chapter_type_counter_var.duplicate(true)
163:             chapter_type_counter[room_type] = int(chapter_type_counter.get(room_type, 0)) + 1
164:             room_type_count_by_chapter[chapter_id] = chapter_type_counter
165: 
166:         history_types.append(room_type)
167:         if history_types.size() > max_consecutive_same_type + 1:
168:             history_types.pop_front()
169: 
170:         var row: Dictionary = {
171:             "index": room_index,
172:             "room_type": room_type,
173:             "chapter_id": chapter_id,
174:             "chapter_index": chapter_index,
175:             "show_intro": room_index == intro_room,
176:             "boss_id": boss_id,
177:             "is_boss_room": room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS,
178:             "next_rooms": [],
179:             "previous_rooms": []
180:         }
181:         rooms.append(row)
182:         room_plan_map[room_index] = row
183: 
184:     var graph: Dictionary = _build_room_graph(room_plan_map, chapter_order, chapters)
185:     _apply_room_graph(room_plan_map, graph)
186:     var map_bounds: Dictionary = _assign_map_coordinates(room_plan_map, chapter_order, chapters)
187: 
188:     var computed_cols: int = int(map_bounds.get("cols", layout_cols))
189:     if computed_cols > 0:
190:         layout_cols = maxi(layout_cols, computed_cols)
191: 
192:     var rebuilt_rooms: Array[Dictionary] = []
193:     for room_index in range(1, room_count + 1):
194:         var room_row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_index, {})
195:         if room_row_var is Dictionary:
196:             rebuilt_rooms.append((room_row_var as Dictionary).duplicate(true))
197: 
198:     return {
199:         "room_count": room_count,
200:         "layout_cols": layout_cols,
201:         "map_bounds": map_bounds,
202:         "chapter_order": chapter_order,
203:         "start_room": 1,
204:         "rooms": rebuilt_rooms,
205:         "room_plan_map": room_plan_map
206:     }
207: 
208: 
209: func _build_room_graph(room_plan_map: Dictionary, chapter_order: Array[String], chapters: Dictionary) -> Dictionary:
210:     var graph: Dictionary = {}
211:     for room_id_var: Variant in room_plan_map.keys():
212:         graph[int(room_id_var)] = []
213: 
214:     var previous_boss_room: int = -1
215:     for chapter_id in chapter_order:
216:         var chapter_row_var: Variant = chapters.get(chapter_id, {})
217:         if not (chapter_row_var is Dictionary):
218:             continue
219:         var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapter_row_var
220:         var start_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("start_room", -1))
221:         var end_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("end_room", -1))
222:         var boss_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("boss_room", -1))
223:         if start_room <= 0 or end_room < start_room or boss_room <= 0:
224:             continue
225: 
226:         var chapter_rooms: Array[int] = []
227:         for room_id in range(start_room, end_room + 1):
228:             if room_plan_map.has(room_id):
229:                 chapter_rooms.append(room_id)
230: 
231:         if chapter_rooms.is_empty():
232:             continue
233: 
234:         var ordered_rooms: Array[int] = chapter_rooms.duplicate()
235:         ordered_rooms.sort()
236: 
237:         if previous_boss_room > 0 and start_room != previous_boss_room:
238:             _add_edge(graph, previous_boss_room, start_room)
239: 
240:         var middle_rooms: Array[int] = []
241:         for room_id in ordered_rooms:
242:             if room_id == start_room or room_id == boss_room:
243:                 continue
244:             middle_rooms.append(room_id)
245: 
246:         if middle_rooms.size() >= 2:
247:             var branch_a: int = middle_rooms[0]
248:             var branch_b: int = middle_rooms[1]
249:             _add_edge(graph, start_room, branch_a)
250:             _add_edge(graph, start_room, branch_b)
251:             _add_edge(graph, branch_a, boss_room)
252:             _add_edge(graph, branch_b, boss_room)
253:             _set_branch_anchor(room_plan_map, start_room)
254: 
255:             for idx in range(2, middle_rooms.size()):
256:                 var extra_room: int = middle_rooms[idx]
257:                 var target_room: int = branch_a if idx % 2 == 0 else branch_b
258:                 _add_edge(graph, start_room, extra_room)
259:                 _add_edge(graph, extra_room, target_room)
260:         elif middle_rooms.size() == 1:
261:             var mid_room: int = middle_rooms[0]
262:             _add_edge(graph, start_room, mid_room)
263:             _add_edge(graph, mid_room, boss_room)
264:         else:
265:             _add_edge(graph, start_room, boss_room)
266: 
267:         previous_boss_room = boss_room
268: 
269:     return graph
270: 
271: 
272: func _apply_room_graph(room_plan_map: Dictionary, graph: Dictionary) -> void:
273:     var previous_map: Dictionary = {}
274:     for room_id_var: Variant in graph.keys():
275:         var room_id: int = int(room_id_var)
276:         var next_rows: Array[int] = []
277:         var raw_next_var: Variant = graph.get(room_id, [])
278:         if raw_next_var is Array:
279:             for target_var: Variant in raw_next_var:
280:                 var target_id: int = int(target_var)
281:                 if target_id <= 0 or not room_plan_map.has(target_id):
282:                     continue
283:                 if not next_rows.has(target_id):
284:                     next_rows.append(target_id)
285:                     if not previous_map.has(target_id):
286:                         previous_map[target_id] = []
287:                     var previous_rows: Array = previous_map.get(target_id, [])
288:                     if not previous_rows.has(room_id):
289:                         previous_rows.append(room_id)
290:                     previous_map[target_id] = previous_rows
291: 
292:         var room_row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
293:         if room_row_var is Dictionary:
294:             var room_row: Dictionary = room_row_var
295:             room_row["next_rooms"] = next_rows
296:             room_plan_map[room_id] = room_row
297: 
298:     for room_id_var: Variant in room_plan_map.keys():
299:         var room_id: int = int(room_id_var)
300:         var room_row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
301:         if not (room_row_var is Dictionary):
302:             continue
303:         var room_row: Dictionary = room_row_var
304:         var previous_rows_out: Array[int] = []
305:         var previous_rows_var: Variant = previous_map.get(room_id, [])
306:         if previous_rows_var is Array:
307:             for source_var: Variant in previous_rows_var:
308:                 var source_id: int = int(source_var)
309:                 if source_id > 0 and not previous_rows_out.has(source_id):
310:                     previous_rows_out.append(source_id)
311:         room_row["previous_rooms"] = previous_rows_out
312:         room_plan_map[room_id] = room_row
313: 
314: 
315: func _assign_map_coordinates(room_plan_map: Dictionary, chapter_order: Array[String], chapters: Dictionary) -> Dictionary:
316:     var chapter_offset_x: int = 0
317: 
318:     for chapter_id in chapter_order:
319:         var chapter_row_var: Variant = chapters.get(chapter_id, {})
320:         if not (chapter_row_var is Dictionary):
321:             continue
322:         var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapter_row_var
323:         var start_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("start_room", -1))
324:         var end_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("end_room", -1))
325:         var boss_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("boss_room", -1))
326:         if start_room <= 0 or end_room < start_room:
327:             continue
328: 
329:         var chapter_rooms: Array[int] = []
330:         for room_id in range(start_room, end_room + 1):
331:             if room_plan_map.has(room_id):
332:                 chapter_rooms.append(room_id)
333:         if chapter_rooms.is_empty():
334:             continue
335: 
336:         var middle_rooms: Array[int] = []
337:         for room_id in chapter_rooms:
338:             if room_id == start_room or room_id == boss_room:
339:                 continue
340:             middle_rooms.append(room_id)
341:         middle_rooms.sort()
342: 
343:         _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, start_room, chapter_offset_x, 0)
344:         if boss_room > 0 and room_plan_map.has(boss_room):
345:             _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, boss_room, chapter_offset_x + 2, 0)
346: 
347:         if middle_rooms.size() == 1:
348:             _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, middle_rooms[0], chapter_offset_x + 1, 0)
349:         elif middle_rooms.size() >= 2:
350:             _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, middle_rooms[0], chapter_offset_x + 1, -1)
351:             _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, middle_rooms[1], chapter_offset_x + 1, 1)
352: 
353:             var extra_offsets: Array[int] = _build_extra_lane_offsets(middle_rooms.size() - 2)
354:             for idx in range(2, middle_rooms.size()):
355:                 _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, middle_rooms[idx], chapter_offset_x + 1, extra_offsets[idx - 2])
356: 
357:         chapter_offset_x += 3
358: 
359:     for room_id_var: Variant in room_plan_map.keys():
360:         var room_id: int = int(room_id_var)
361:         var row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
362:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
363:             continue
364:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
365:         if row.has("map_x") and row.has("map_y"):
366:             continue
367: 
368:         var chapter_index: int = maxi(1, int(row.get("chapter_index", 1)))
369:         _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map, room_id, (chapter_index - 1) * 3 + 1, 0)
370: 
371:     var min_x: int = 0
372:     var max_x: int = 0
373:     var min_y: int = 0
374:     var max_y: int = 0
375:     var first: bool = true
376: 
377:     for row_var: Variant in room_plan_map.values():
378:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
379:             continue
380:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
381:         var map_x: int = int(row.get("map_x", 0))
382:         var map_y: int = int(row.get("map_y", 0))
383:         if first:
384:             min_x = map_x
385:             max_x = map_x
386:             min_y = map_y
387:             max_y = map_y
388:             first = false
389:         else:
390:             min_x = mini(min_x, map_x)
391:             max_x = maxi(max_x, map_x)
392:             min_y = mini(min_y, map_y)
393:             max_y = maxi(max_y, map_y)
394: 
395:     return {
396:         "min_x": min_x,
397:         "max_x": max_x,
398:         "min_y": min_y,
399:         "max_y": max_y,
400:         "cols": max_x - min_x + 1,
401:         "rows": max_y - min_y + 1
402:     }
403: 
404: 
405: func _set_room_map_coord(room_plan_map: Dictionary, room_id: int, map_x: int, map_y: int) -> void:
406:     var row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
407:     if not (row_var is Dictionary):
408:         return
409:     var row: Dictionary = row_var
410:     row["map_x"] = map_x
411:     row["map_y"] = map_y
412:     room_plan_map[room_id] = row
413: 
414: 
415: func _build_extra_lane_offsets(count: int) -> Array[int]:
416:     var output: Array[int] = []
417:     var depth: int = 2
418:     while output.size() < count:
419:         output.append(-depth)
420:         if output.size() >= count:
421:             break
422:         output.append(depth)
423:         depth += 1
424:     return output
425: 
426: 
427: func _set_branch_anchor(room_plan_map: Dictionary, room_id: int) -> void:
428:     var row_var: Variant = room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
429:     if row_var is Dictionary:
430:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
431:         row["is_branch_anchor"] = true
432:         room_plan_map[room_id] = row
433: 
434: 
435: func _add_edge(graph: Dictionary, from_room: int, to_room: int) -> void:
436:     if from_room <= 0 or to_room <= 0 or from_room == to_room:
437:         return
438:     if not graph.has(from_room):
439:         graph[from_room] = []
440:     var next_rows: Array = graph.get(from_room, [])
441:     if not next_rows.has(to_room):
442:         next_rows.append(to_room)
443:     graph[from_room] = next_rows
444: 
445: 
446: func _extract_fixed_rooms(rows_var: Variant) -> Dictionary:
447:     var output: Dictionary = {}
448:     if not (rows_var is Array):
449:         return output
450: 
451:     for item: Variant in rows_var:
452:         if not (item is Dictionary):
453:             continue
454:         var row: Dictionary = item
455:         var index: int = int(row.get("index", -1))
456:         var room_type: String = str(row.get("type", "")).strip_edges()
457:         if index <= 0:
458:             continue
459:         if not _is_valid_room_type(room_type):
460:             continue
461:         output[index] = room_type
462:     return output
463: 
464: 
465: func _normalize_weights(raw_weights: Dictionary, fallback: Dictionary) -> Dictionary:
466:     var normalized: Dictionary = fallback.duplicate(true)
467:     for room_type in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
468:         normalized[room_type] = maxf(0.0, float(raw_weights.get(room_type, fallback.get(room_type, 0.0))))
469:     return normalized
470: 
471: 
472: func _normalize_room_type_caps(raw_caps_var: Variant) -> Dictionary:
473:     var output: Dictionary = {}
474:     if not (raw_caps_var is Dictionary):
475:         return output
476: 
477:     var raw_caps: Dictionary = raw_caps_var
478:     for room_type in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
479:         if not raw_caps.has(room_type):
480:             continue
481:         output[room_type] = maxi(-1, int(raw_caps.get(room_type, -1)))
482:     return output
483: 
484: 
485: func _normalize_room_type_mins(raw_mins_var: Variant) -> Dictionary:
486:     var output: Dictionary = {}
487:     if not (raw_mins_var is Dictionary):
488:         return output
489: 
490:     var raw_mins: Dictionary = raw_mins_var
491:     for room_type in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
492:         if not raw_mins.has(room_type):
493:             continue
494:         output[room_type] = maxi(0, int(raw_mins.get(room_type, 0)))
495:     return output
496: 
497: 
498: func _build_chapter_rollable_slots(chapter_order: Array[String], chapters: Dictionary, room_count: int, fixed_room_types: Dictionary, avoid_shop_near_boss: bool, avoid_event_near_boss: bool) -> Dictionary:
499:     var output: Dictionary = {}
500: 
501:     for chapter_id in chapter_order:
502:         var chapter_row_var: Variant = chapters.get(chapter_id, {})
503:         if not (chapter_row_var is Dictionary):
504:             continue
505:         var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapter_row_var
506:         var start_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("start_room", -1))
507:         var end_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("end_room", -1))
508:         var boss_room: int = int(chapter_row.get("boss_room", -1))
509:         if start_room <= 0 or end_room < start_room:
510:             continue
511: 
512:         var slots: Array[Dictionary] = []
513:         for room_index in range(start_room, mini(end_room, room_count) + 1):
514:             if room_index == 1:
515:                 continue
516:             if room_index == boss_room:
517:                 continue
518:             if fixed_room_types.has(room_index):
519:                 continue
520: 
521:             var eligible_types: Array[String] = ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES.duplicate(true)
522:             if avoid_shop_near_boss and boss_room > 0 and room_index >= boss_room - 1:
523:                 eligible_types.erase(ROOM_TYPE_SHOP)
524:             if avoid_event_near_boss and boss_room > 0 and room_index >= boss_room - 1:
525:                 eligible_types.erase(ROOM_TYPE_EVENT)
526: 
527:             slots.append({
528:                 "index": room_index,
529:                 "eligible_types": eligible_types
530:             })
531: 
532:         output[chapter_id] = slots
533: 
534:     return output
535: 
536: 
537: func _collect_forced_min_types(deficits: Dictionary, chapter_slots: Array, slot_cursor: int) -> Array[String]:
538:     var forced_types: Array[String] = []
539:     if slot_cursor < 0 or slot_cursor >= chapter_slots.size():
540:         return forced_types
541: 
542:     var current_slot_var: Variant = chapter_slots[slot_cursor]
543:     if not (current_slot_var is Dictionary):
544:         return forced_types
545:     var current_slot: Dictionary = current_slot_var
546:     var current_eligible_var: Variant = current_slot.get("eligible_types", [])
547:     var current_eligible: Array = current_eligible_var if current_eligible_var is Array else []
548: 
549:     for deficit_key in deficits.keys():
550:         var room_type_key: String = str(deficit_key)
551:         var deficit: int = int(deficits.get(room_type_key, 0))
552:         if deficit <= 0:
553:             continue
554: 
555:         var eligible_remaining: int = 0
556:         for idx in range(slot_cursor, chapter_slots.size()):
557:             var slot_row_var: Variant = chapter_slots[idx]
558:             if not (slot_row_var is Dictionary):
559:                 continue
560:             var eligible_var: Variant = (slot_row_var as Dictionary).get("eligible_types", [])
561:             if eligible_var is Array and (eligible_var as Array).has(room_type_key):
562:                 eligible_remaining += 1
563: 
564:         if eligible_remaining > 0 and eligible_remaining <= deficit and current_eligible.has(room_type_key):
565:             forced_types.append(room_type_key)
566: 
567:     return forced_types
568: 
569: 
570: func _resolve_chapter_id(room_index: int, chapter_order: Array[String], chapters: Dictionary) -> String:
571:     for chapter_id in chapter_order:
572:         var row_var: Variant = chapters.get(chapter_id, {})
573:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
574:             continue
575:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
576:         var start_room: int = int(row.get("start_room", 1))
577:         var end_room: int = int(row.get("end_room", 1))
578:         if room_index >= start_room and room_index <= end_room:
579:             return chapter_id
580: 
581:     var chapter_size: int = maxi(1, int(ceil(float(room_index) / 4.0)))
582:     return "chapter_%d" % chapter_size
583: 
584: 
585: func _fallback_chapter_index(chapter_id: String) -> int:
586:     var suffix: String = chapter_id.trim_prefix("chapter_")
587:     if suffix.is_valid_int():
588:         return maxi(1, int(suffix))
589:     return 1
590: 
591: 
592: func _build_chapter_weights(chapter_id: String, base_weights: Dictionary, chapter_weight_mult: Dictionary) -> Dictionary:
593:     var output: Dictionary = base_weights.duplicate(true)
594:     var chapter_mult_var: Variant = chapter_weight_mult.get(chapter_id, {})
595:     if chapter_mult_var is Dictionary:
596:         var chapter_mult: Dictionary = chapter_mult_var
597:         for room_type in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
598:             var base_weight: float = maxf(0.0, float(output.get(room_type, 0.0)))
599:             var mult: float = clampf(float(chapter_mult.get(room_type, 1.0)), 0.0, 3.0)
600:             output[room_type] = base_weight * mult
601:     return output
602: 
603: 
604: func _roll_room_type(weights: Dictionary, history_types: Array[String], max_consecutive_same_type: int) -> String:
605:     var blocked_type: String = ""
606:     if history_types.size() >= max_consecutive_same_type:
607:         var tail_type: String = history_types[history_types.size() - 1]
608:         var same_count: int = 1
609:         for idx in range(history_types.size() - 2, -1, -1):
610:             if history_types[idx] == tail_type:
611:                 same_count += 1
612:             else:
613:                 break
614:         if same_count >= max_consecutive_same_type:
615:             blocked_type = tail_type
616: 
617:     var total: float = 0.0
618:     var weighted_rows: Array[Dictionary] = []
619:     for room_type in ROLLABLE_ROOM_TYPES:
620:         var weight: float = maxf(0.0, float(weights.get(room_type, 0.0)))
621:         if room_type == blocked_type:
622:             weight = 0.0
623:         if weight <= 0.0:
624:             continue
625:         weighted_rows.append({"type": room_type, "weight": weight})
626:         total += weight
627: 
628:     if total <= 0.0 or weighted_rows.is_empty():
629:         if blocked_type != ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT:
630:             return ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT
631:         return ROOM_TYPE_EVENT
632: 
633:     var roll: float = randf() * total
634:     var cursor: float = 0.0
635:     for row in weighted_rows:
636:         cursor += float(row.get("weight", 0.0))
637:         if roll <= cursor:
638:             return str(row.get("type", ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT))
639: 
640:     return str(weighted_rows[weighted_rows.size() - 1].get("type", ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT))
641: 
642: 
643: func _is_valid_room_type(room_type: String) -> bool:
644:     return room_type == ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT \
645:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS \
646:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_EVENT \
647:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SHOP \
648:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE \
649:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SAFE_CAMP \
650:         or room_type == ROOM_TYPE_ELITE

(End of file - total 650 lines)
</content>
```

47: - 武器自动攻击，无需玩家手动操作
48: - 每个武器有独立的攻击间隔、伤害、攻击范围、弹道模式
49: - 武器可升级（最高 Lv.8），每级提升属性或解锁新效果
50: - 同时最多装备 6 个武器
51:

53: | 武器 | 弹道类型 | 说明 |
54: |------|----------|------|

56: | 圣光环 | 环绕 | 围绕玩家旋转的光环 |
57: | 火焰喷射 | 锥形AOE | 朝玩家面朝方向喷射 |
58: | 闪电链 | 链式 | 命中后弹射至附近敌人 |
59: | 冰霜新星 | 圆形AOE | 以玩家为中心的冰冻爆发 |
60: | 飞刀 | 直线弹幕 | 高速直线投射物 |
61: 
62: #### FR-W03: 被动技能
63: - 被动技能提供永久属性加成或特殊效果
64: - 初始最多装备 6 个被动技能，通过章节进度逐步解锁至 12 槽位
65:   - 第1章通关：解锁第 7-8 槽位
66:   - 第2章通关：解锁第 9-10 槽位
67:   - 第3章通关：解锁第 11-12 槽位
68: - 被动技能可升级（最高 Lv.5）
69: - 被动技能分为三类路线标签：`holy`（神圣系）、`void`（虚空系）、`neutral`（中立）
70: 
71: #### FR-W04: 武器进化
72: - 特定武器 + 特定被动技能满级后可进化为高级武器
73: - 进化武器拥有全新的攻击模式和大幅增强的属性
74: 
75: #### FR-W05: 饰品系统
76: - 饰品为独立装备类型，与武器和被动技能分开管理
77: - 最多同时装备 2 件饰品
78: - 饰品仅通过 Boss 击杀、宝藏房间、特殊事件获取（不可通过升级选择获得）
79: - 饰品提供独特机制效果（非数值加成），无法升级

83: ### 1.3 敌人系统
84: 
85: #### FR-E01: 敌人生成
86: - 敌人从房间预设刷新点或边缘生成，朝玩家方向移动
87: - 生成频率和敌人强度由双因子驱动：**楼层编号**（基础难度）+ **房间内战斗时间**（递增压力）
88:   - 进入战斗房间开始计时，清除所有敌人或离开房间时停止
89:   - 安全营地、商店房间、事件房间不计时

93: | 类型 | 行为 | 说明 |
94: |------|------|------|

97: | 坦克 | 缓慢追踪 | 高血量高伤害 |
98: | 远程 | 保持距离+射击 | 远程攻击型 |
99: | 精英 | 追踪+特殊技能 | 带有特殊能力的强化敌人 |
100: | Boss | 复杂AI | 阶段性Boss，多种攻击模式 |
101: 
102: #### FR-E03: 敌人掉落
103: - 所有敌人死亡后掉落经验宝石

105: - 精英/Boss 掉落高品质物品和更多经验
106:

109: ### 1.4 升级与进度系统
110: 
111: #### FR-L01: 经验与升级
112: - 拾取经验宝石获得经验值
113: - 升级所需经验随等级递增（公式：`base_xp * level ^ 1.3`）
114: - 升级时暂停游戏，弹出技能选择界面
115: 
116: #### FR-L02: 升级选择
117: - 每次升级随机提供 3 个选项（受幸运值影响品质）
118: - 选项包括：新武器、武器升级、新被动、被动升级
119: - 已满级的武器/被动不再出现
120: - 支持重新随机（消耗金币，每局限定次数）
121: 
122: #### FR-L03: Meta 进度（永久升级）
123: - 每局游戏结束获得 Meta 货币（基于表现）
124: - Meta 升级树提供永久属性加成
125: - 解锁新角色、新武器、新被动技能
126: - Meta 进度存储在本地存档中
127: 
128: #### FR-L04: 矿石收集与锻造
129: - 特定楼层（如第2章锻炉层）可获取矿石材料
130: - 矿石用于在安全营地的锻造站强化当前武器
131: - 锻造消耗：3 矿石 → 武器伤害 +10%，5 矿石 → 武器附加元素效果
132: - 矿石为当局资源，不跨局保留
133: 
134: ---
135: 
136: ### 1.5 Roguelike 地图系统
137: 
138: #### FR-R01: 程序化地图生成
139: - 使用 BSP / Wave Function Collapse 算法生成随机地图
140: - 地图由多个房间（Room）和走廊（Corridor）组成
141: - 每个房间有不同的地形和敌人配置
142: 
143: #### FR-R02: 地图结构
144: - 每局游戏包含多个楼层（Floor），难度递增
145: - 每个楼层包含：
146:   - 起始房间（安全区）
147:   - 普通战斗房间（3-5个）
148:   - 精英房间（1-2个）
149:   - 商店房间（1个）
150:   - 宝藏房间（0-1个，随机出现）
151:   - Boss 房间（1个，通往下一层的入口）
152: 
153: #### FR-R03: 房间事件
154: - 进入房间触发战斗，清除所有敌人后解锁出口
155: - 商店房间：使用金币购买武器/被动/回复道具
156: - 宝藏房间：解谜或挑战后获得稀有奖励
157: - 随机事件房间：触发随机事件（祝福/诅咒/NPC交互）
158: 
159: #### FR-R04: 小地图
160: - HUD 显示当前楼层的小地图
161: - 已探索房间显示图标（战斗/商店/Boss等）
162: - 未探索房间显示为灰色问号
163: 
164: #### FR-R05: 环境危害系统
165: - 每个楼层拥有独特的环境主题和对应的环境危害
166: - 环境危害类型包括：水流推移、孢子毒云、熔岩地形、冰面滑行、虚空腐蚀等
167: - 环境危害同时影响玩家和敌人（部分敌人可免疫对应楼层的环境效果）
168: - 环境交互支持组合效果（如：冰面 + 火焰 = 融化产生水面）
169: 
170: #### FR-R06: 楼层主题
171: - 每章楼层拥有统一视觉主题（地形瓦片、配色、光照、粒子效果）
172: - 第1章（堕落起始）：灰绿色调、苔藓石墙、昏暗火把
173: - 第2章（炼狱试炼）：红橙色调、熔岩、工业金属
174: - 第3章（寒霜深渊）：冰蓝色调、冰晶、极光
175: - 终章（虚空圣殿）：紫黑色调、虚空裂隙、几何结构
176: 
177: #### FR-R07: 安全营地
178: - 每章通关后进入安全营地（非战斗区域）
179: - 营地功能：NPC 对话、商店购物、记忆碎片阅读、锻造站（特定章节）
180: - 营地不计入游戏计时，玩家可自由探索后选择进入下一章
181: 
182: #### FR-R08: 可破坏物与交互物
183: - 房间内包含可破坏物体（木桶、水晶、蘑菇等），破坏后掉落金币/回复物
184: - 特定房间包含交互物体（机关、传送门、NPC）
185: - 可破坏物与环境主题匹配
186: 
187: ---
188: 
189: ### 1.7 叙事系统
190: 
191: #### FR-N01: 章节转场叙事
192: - 每章开始和结束时播放叙事转场画面
193: - 叙事包含：旁白文字、角色对话、场景描写
194: - 玩家可通过按键加速或跳过叙事
195: 
196: #### FR-N02: 分支选择
197: - 章节转场中提供关键选择点（2-3 个选项）
198: - 选择影响后续剧情走向和可获取的奖励
199: - 选择记录存入 RunData，影响路线亲和度计算
200: 
201: #### FR-N03: 双路线系统（救赎 / 堕落）
202: - 玩家行为和选择积累路线亲和度（`alignment` 值，范围 -100 ~ +100）
203:   - 正值倾向救赎路线，负值倾向堕落路线
204: - 影响亲和度的因素：
205:   - 升级时选择神圣系被动（+亲和度）或虚空系被动（-亲和度）
206:   - 叙事分支选择
207:   - 特定事件房间的决策
208: - 亲和度影响：最终结局、部分 NPC 对话、隐藏层解锁条件
209: 
210: #### FR-N04: 记忆碎片
211: - 记忆碎片散布在宝藏房间、隐藏区域和 Boss 掉落中
212: - 收集的碎片可在安全营地阅读，揭示世界观和角色背景
213: - 碎片分为 4 类：世界史、角色记忆、堕落真相、救赎之路
214: - 总计 33 个碎片，收集进度记录在 RunData 中
215: 
216: #### FR-N05: 三结局系统
217: - 根据路线亲和度和关键选择，游戏提供三种结局：
218:   - **救赎结局**：亲和度 ≥ 50 且完成救赎路线关键选择
219:   - **堕落结局**：亲和度 ≤ -50 且完成堕落路线关键选择
220:   - **平衡结局**：亲和度在 -49 ~ +49 之间，或未满足上述条件
221: 
222: #### FR-N06: 事件分支权重与门禁
223: - 事件房叙事选择采用加权路由，不仅基于随机
224: - 加权因子至少包含：当前 alignment 区间、已解锁结局、近期事件历史（避免重复）
225: - 支持事件门禁字段：`requires_endings_any` 与 `forbid_endings_any`
226: 
227: #### FR-N07: 章节持续效果
228: - 事件选择可附加 `chapter_effect`，持续 2~3 个房间
229: - 章节效果可影响：刷怪速率、敌人 HP、敌人伤害、环境危害强度、玩家移速、伤害加成、临时护甲
230: - HUD 与房间状态必须显示效果名称、正负向、剩余房间数
231: 
232: #### FR-N08: 结局后记与叙事回顾
233: - 结算界面需显示结局后记文本（首次解锁版与重复轮回版）
234: - 结算界面需展示本局叙事选择时间线摘要（上限与溢出提示）
235: - 主菜单支持记忆碎片回看轮播（标题 + 正文）
236: 
237: ---
238: 
239: ### 1.6 UI 系统
240: 
241: #### FR-U01: 主菜单
242: - 开始游戏（角色选择 → 进入游戏）
243: - Meta 升级（永久升级树）
244: - 图鉴（已解锁的武器/被动/敌人/角色）
245: - 设置（音量、画面、按键绑定）
246: - 退出
247: 
248: #### FR-U02: 游戏内 HUD
249: - 生命值条、耐力条
250: - 经验值条 + 当前等级
251: - 已装备武器图标（显示等级）
252: - 已装备被动图标（显示等级）
253: - 已装备饰品图标
254: - 游戏计时器（当前房间战斗时间）
255: - 击杀计数
256: - 金币数量
257: - 矿石数量（仅在含矿石的楼层显示）
258: - 环境仪表（冻伤/虚空腐蚀，仅在对应楼层显示）
259: - 路线亲和度指示器（简化图标，不显示数值）
260: - 小地图
261: 
262: #### FR-U03: 升级选择界面
263: - 暂停游戏
264: - 展示 3 个选项卡片（图标 + 名称 + 描述 + 等级）
265: - 支持键盘/鼠标选择
266: - 重新随机按钮（显示剩余次数）
267: 
268: #### FR-U04: 暂停菜单
269: - ESC 暂停游戏
270: - 显示当前属性面板
271: - 继续 / 设置 / 放弃本局
272: - 暂停菜单需支持“回主菜单（不结算）”操作
273: - 暂停菜单设置子页支持运行时调节并即时生效：
274:   - Master / BGM / SFX / Ambience 音量
275:   - 屏幕震动强度
276:   - UI 缩放（80%~150%）
277: - 设置变更需持久化到存档，并在下一次启动自动恢复
278: 
279: #### FR-U05: 结算界面
280: - 存活时间、击杀数、获得经验、获得金币
281: - 获得的 Meta 货币
282: - 解锁成就提示
283: - 返回主菜单
284: 
285: #### FR-U06: 局内反馈增强
286: - HUD 需支持事件吐司通知（成就/结局/记忆碎片/饰品）
287: - HUD 需提供 3x5 迷你地图（15 房），显示：房间编号、房型、当前房间高亮、已完成状态
288: - HUD 章节效果条需显示图标化正负向（`[+]` / `[-]` / `[~]`）与剩余房间计数
289: 
290: ---
291: 
292: ## 2. 非功能需求
293: 
294: ### 2.1 性能要求
295: 
296: | 指标 | 目标值 |
297: |------|--------|
298: | 帧率 | ≥ 55 FPS（500 敌人同屏场景下） |
299: | 同屏敌人数 | ≥ 500 |
300: | 同屏弹幕数 | ≥ 200 |
301: | 内存占用 | ≤ 512 MB |
302: | 启动时间 | ≤ 3 秒 |
303: | 存档加载 | ≤ 1 秒 |
304: | 场景切换 | ≤ 0.5 秒（含过渡动画） |
305: 
306: ### 2.2 可维护性
307: - 武器/敌人/被动技能通过 Resource 配置文件定义，支持热加载
308: - 数值平衡通过外部 JSON/CSV 配置表驱动
309: - 模块间低耦合，使用信号（Signal）通信
310: 
311: ### 2.3 可扩展性
312: - 支持通过 Mod 系统添加新武器/敌人/角色
313: - 地图生成算法可插拔替换
314: - 预留多人联机接口（未来版本）
315: 
316: ### 2.4 存档系统
317: - 自动保存 Meta 进度
318: - 单局游戏不支持中途存档（Roguelike 设计）
319: - 存档数据加密防篡改
320: - 存档包含运行时设置（音量/震动/UI缩放）并支持实时落盘
321: 
322: ### 2.5 本地化
323: - 支持中文（简体）和英文
324: - 所有文本通过 i18n 键值对管理
325: - UI 布局适配不同语言文本长度
326: 
327: ### 2.6 无障碍
328: - 支持完全键盘操作
329: - 支持手柄输入（Xbox / PlayStation 布局）
330: - 支持输入重映射（键盘和手柄均可自定义按键）
331: - 色盲模式（三种类型：红绿色盲 / 蓝黄色盲 / 全色盲，通过替换配色方案实现）
332: - UI 字体大小可调（小 / 中 / 大，默认中）
333: - UI 缩放支持（80% ~ 150%）
334: - 叙事文本支持字幕样式显示（底部半透明背景条 + 白色文字）
335: - 屏幕震动强度可调（关闭 / 低 / 中 / 高）

(End of file - total 335 lines)
</content>
```

310: ## 风险与应对
311: 
312: | 风险 | 概率 | 影响 | 应对策略 |
313: |------|------|------|----------|
314: | 500敌人性能不达标 | 中 | 高 | Phase 1 提前做性能原型验证；备选：降至300 + MultiMesh视觉欺骗 |
315: | BSP地图生成质量差 | 中 | 中 | 准备WFC备选算法；可退化为预制房间随机组合 |
316: | 数值平衡失控 | 高 | 中 | 自动化模拟测试；配置表外置便于快速调整；CDR/护甲已设上限 |
317: | AI素材质量不达标 | 高 | 中 | 多方案并行 (SD + MJ + 手绘修正)；像素风容错率高；预留手动优化时间 |
318: | AI素材风格不一致 | 中 | 中 | 固定种子/LoRA/提示词模板；Aseprite统一像素化后处理 |
319: | 单人开发进度延迟 | 高 | 中 | MVP只做2章；P2任务可砍；后续版本渐进发布 |
320: | 叙事系统复杂度超预期 | 中 | 低 | MVP只实现线性叙事；分支选择简化为2选1 |
