```
389:         chapter_rows.append("CH%d:%s" % [idx, _get_route_style_label(style_id)])
390:     rows.append(" | ".join(PackedStringArray(chapter_rows)))
391: 
392:     if not _route_style_timeline.is_empty():
393:         var latest: Dictionary = _route_style_timeline[_route_style_timeline.size() - 1]
394:         rows.append("Latest lock: R%d %s -> %s" % [
395:             int(latest.get("room_index", _room_index)),
396:             str(latest.get("chapter_id", "chapter")),
397:             _get_route_style_label(str(latest.get("style_id", "neutral")))
398:         ])
399: 
400:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
401: 
402: 
403: func get_minimap_text() -> String:
404:     var coordinate_lookup: Dictionary = _build_minimap_coordinate_lookup()
405:     if not coordinate_lookup.is_empty():
406:         var bounds: Dictionary = _get_minimap_bounds()
407:         var min_x: int = int(bounds.get("min_x", 0))
408:         var max_x: int = int(bounds.get("max_x", 0))
409:         var min_y: int = int(bounds.get("min_y", 0))
410:         var max_y: int = int(bounds.get("max_y", 0))
411: 
412:         var coord_rows: Array[String] = []
413:         for map_y in range(min_y, max_y + 1):
414:             var parts: Array[String] = []
415:             for map_x in range(min_x, max_x + 1):
416:                 var coord_key: String = "%d:%d" % [map_x, map_y]
417:                 if not coordinate_lookup.has(coord_key):
418:                     parts.append("----")
419:                     continue
420: 
421:                 var room_id: int = int(coordinate_lookup.get(coord_key, 0))
422:                 parts.append(_build_minimap_room_token(room_id))
423:             coord_rows.append(" ".join(PackedStringArray(parts)))
424:         return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(coord_rows))
425: 
426:     return _build_minimap_index_grid()
427: 
428: 
429: func _build_minimap_index_grid() -> String:
430:     var room_count: int = _get_run_room_count()
431:     var cols: int = _get_run_layout_cols()
432:     var rows_count: int = int(ceil(float(room_count) / float(cols)))
433:     var rows: Array[String] = []
434:     for row_index in range(rows_count):
435:         var parts: Array[String] = []
436:         for col_index in range(cols):
437:             var room_id: int = row_index * cols + col_index + 1
438:             if room_id > room_count:
439:                 parts.append("----")
440:             else:
441:                 parts.append(_build_minimap_room_token(room_id))
442:         rows.append(" ".join(PackedStringArray(parts)))
443:     return "\n".join(PackedStringArray(rows))
444: 
445: 
446: func _build_minimap_coordinate_lookup() -> Dictionary:
447:     var lookup: Dictionary = {}
448:     for room_id_var: Variant in _room_plan_map.keys():
449:         var room_id: int = int(room_id_var)
450:         var row_var: Variant = _room_plan_map.get(room_id, {})
451:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
452:             continue
453:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
454:         if not row.has("map_x") or not row.has("map_y"):
455:             continue
456:         var key: String = "%d:%d" % [int(row.get("map_x", 0)), int(row.get("map_y", 0))]
457:         lookup[key] = room_id
458:     return lookup
459: 
460: 
461: func _get_minimap_bounds() -> Dictionary:
462:     if not _run_map_bounds.is_empty():
463:         return _run_map_bounds
464: 
465:     var has_any: bool = false
466:     var min_x: int = 0
467:     var max_x: int = 0
468:     var min_y: int = 0
469:     var max_y: int = 0
470:     for row_var: Variant in _room_plan_map.values():
471:         if not (row_var is Dictionary):
472:             continue
473:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
474:         if not row.has("map_x") or not row.has("map_y"):
475:             continue
476:         var map_x: int = int(row.get("map_x", 0))
477:         var map_y: int = int(row.get("map_y", 0))
478:         if not has_any:
479:             min_x = map_x
480:             max_x = map_x
481:             min_y = map_y
482:             max_y = map_y
483:             has_any = true
484:         else:
485:             min_x = mini(min_x, map_x)
486:             max_x = maxi(max_x, map_x)
487:             min_y = mini(min_y, map_y)
488:             max_y = maxi(max_y, map_y)
489: 
490:     if has_any:
491:         return {
492:             "min_x": min_x,
493:             "max_x": max_x,
494:             "min_y": min_y,
495:             "max_y": max_y,
496:             "cols": max_x - min_x + 1,
497:             "rows": max_y - min_y + 1
498:         }
499: 
500:     var cols: int = _get_run_layout_cols()
501:     var rows_count: int = int(ceil(float(_get_run_room_count()) / float(cols)))
502:     return {
503:         "min_x": 0,
504:         "max_x": cols - 1,
505:         "min_y": 0,
506:         "max_y": maxi(0, rows_count - 1),
507:         "cols": cols,
508:         "rows": rows_count
509:     }
510: 
511: 
512: func _build_minimap_room_token(room_id: int) -> String:
513:     if not _room_history.has(room_id):
514:         return "??"
515: 
516:     var row_var: Variant = _room_history.get(room_id, {})
517:     if not (row_var is Dictionary):
518:         return "??"
519: 
520:     var row: Dictionary = row_var
521:     var room_type: String = str(row.get("type", ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT))
522:     var completed: bool = bool(row.get("completed", false))
523:     var marker: String = _room_type_to_minimap_marker(room_type)
524:     if completed:
525:         marker = marker.to_lower()
526: 
527:     var token: String = "%02d%s" % [room_id, marker]
528:     if room_id == _room_index and not _run_finished:
529:         return ">%s<" % token
530:     return token
531: 
532: 
533: func _room_type_to_minimap_marker(room_type: String) -> String:
534:     match room_type:
535:         ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
536:             return "B"
537:         ROOM_TYPE_EVENT:
538:             return "E"
539:         ROOM_TYPE_SHOP:
540:             return "S"
541:         ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE:
542:             return "T"
543:         ROOM_TYPE_SAFE_CAMP:
544:             return "H"
545:         ROOM_TYPE_ELITE:
546:             return "L"
547:         _:
548:             return "C"
549: 
550: 
551: func _ensure_room_history(index: int, room_type: String) -> void:
552:     _room_history[index] = {
553:         "type": room_type,
554:         "completed": bool((_room_history.get(index, {}) as Dictionary).get("completed", false))
555:     }
556: 
557: 
558: func _mark_room_completed(index: int) -> void:
559:     if not _room_history.has(index):
560:         return
561:     var row_var: Variant = _room_history.get(index, {})
562:     if row_var is Dictionary:
563:         var row: Dictionary = row_var
564:         row["completed"] = true
565:         _room_history[index] = row
566: 
567: 
568: func _start_room() -> void:
569:     if _room_index > _get_run_room_count():
570:         _finish_run("victory")
571:         return
572: 
573:     _clear_active_enemies()
574:     _clear_active_pickups()
575:     _chapter_intro_pending = false
576:     _narrative_event_pending = false
577:     _chapter_transition_pending = false
578:     _memory_altar_pending = false
579:     _pause_menu_pending = false
580:     _pending_next_rooms.clear()
581:     _selected_next_room_slot = 0
582:     _current_room_type = _resolve_room_type(_room_index)
583:     _sync_route_style_for_room(_room_index)
584:     if GameManager != null and GameManager.has_method("set_run_context"):
585:         GameManager.set_run_context(_room_index, _current_room_type, _get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index))
586:     _ensure_room_history(_room_index, _current_room_type)
587:     _active_hazards = _get_hazards_for_room(_room_index)
588:     _advance_chapter_effects_for_room()
589:     _apply_room_theme(_room_index)
590: 
591:     _kills_in_room = 0
592:     _required_kills = 0
593:     _hazard_tick_timer = 0.0
594:     EventBus.room_entered.emit("room_%d" % _room_index, _current_room_type)
595: 
596:     if _should_show_chapter_intro(_room_index):
597:         _show_chapter_intro(_room_index)
598:         return
599: 
600:     _enter_current_room_type()
601: 
602: 
603: func _enter_current_room_type() -> void:
604:     if _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_COMBAT:
605:         _enter_combat_room()
606:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_ELITE:
607:         _enter_elite_room()
608:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_BOSS:
609:         _enter_boss_room()
610:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_EVENT:
611:         _enter_event_room()
612:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_SHOP:
613:         _enter_shop_room()
614:     elif _current_room_type == ROOM_TYPE_TREASURE:
615:         _enter_treasure_room()
616:     else:
617:         _enter_safe_camp_room()
618: 
619: 
620: func _should_show_chapter_intro(index: int) -> bool:
621:     var room_plan: Dictionary = _get_room_plan(index)
622:     if room_plan.is_empty():
623:         return false
624:     if not bool(room_plan.get("show_intro", false)):
625:         return false
626:     var chapter_key: String = str(room_plan.get("chapter_id", _get_chapter_id_for_room(index)))
627:     return not bool(_shown_chapter_intro.get(chapter_key, false))
628: 
629: 
630: func _show_chapter_intro(index: int) -> void:
631:     _room_active = false
632:     _chapter_intro_pending = true
633:     _set_doors_locked(false)
634:     if _spawner != null and _spawner.has_method("stop_room_combat"):
635:         _spawner.stop_room_combat()
636: 
637:     _room_timer_label.text = "-"
638:     _room_status_label.text = "Chapter briefing..."

640:     var chapter_index: int = _get_chapter_index_for_room(index)
641:     if _chapter_intro_panel != null and _chapter_intro_panel.has_method("show_intro"):
642:         _chapter_intro_panel.show_intro(chapter_index, get_active_hazards_text(), _get_active_blessing_text())
643: 
644: 
645: func _on_intro_closed() -> void:
646:     _chapter_intro_pending = false
647:     _shown_chapter_intro[_get_chapter_id_for_room(_room_index)] = true
648:     _enter_current_room_type()
649: 
650: 
651: func _enter_combat_room() -> void:
652:     _required_kills = 10 + _room_index * 3
653:     _room_active = true
```

```
165: - `test/unit/test_map_generation_config.gd` also validates treasure-room schema keys and generated treasure room types
166: - `test/unit/test_evolutions_config.gd` validates evolution recipe schema and evolution_profile bounds
167: - `test/unit/test_enemy_pooling.gd` validates enemy pool lifecycle reset and death-release behavior

(End of file - total 167 lines)
</content>
```

**Tool: read**

```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\Desktop\\Project\\Game\\angel-fallen\\spec-design\\requirements.md"
}
```

**Output:**
```
<path>D:\Desktop\Project\Game\angel-fallen\spec-design\requirements.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # 需求规格说明书
2: 
3: ## 1. 功能需求
4: 
5: ### 1.1 玩家系统
6: 
7: #### FR-P01: 玩家移动
8: - 玩家通过 WASD / 方向键控制角色八方向移动
9: - 移动速度受属性和Buff影响
10: - 支持冲刺（Shift），消耗耐力值，冷却恢复
11:   - 耐力消耗速率：30/秒（冲刺期间持续扣除）
12:   - 耐力恢复速率：20/秒（停止冲刺后 0.5 秒延迟恢复）
13:   - 冲刺速度倍率：1.6x 基础移动速度
14:   - 耐力为 0 时无法冲刺，需恢复至 ≥20 后才可再次冲刺
15: 
16: #### FR-P02: 玩家属性
17: | 属性 | 说明 | 基础值 |
18: |------|------|--------|
19: | HP | 生命值 | 100 |
20: | MaxHP | 最大生命值 | 100 |
21: | MoveSpeed | 移动速度 | 200 px/s |
22: | Armor | 护甲（减伤百分比） | 0% |
23: | PickupRange | 拾取范围 | 64 px |
24: | Luck | 幸运值（影响掉落品质） | 0 |
25: | CritRate | 暴击率 | 5% |
26: | CritDamage | 暴击伤害倍率 | 150% |
27: | CooldownReduction | 冷却缩减 | 0% |
28: | XPMultiplier | 经验倍率 | 1.0 |
29: | Stamina | 耐力值（冲刺消耗） | 100 |
30: 
31: #### FR-P03: 玩家角色选择
32: - 至少提供 6 个可选角色
33: - 每个角色拥有独特的初始武器和被动技能
34: - 角色通过 Meta 进度解锁
35: 
36: #### FR-P04: 玩家死亡与复活
37: - HP 归零时角色死亡，本局结束（永久死亡）
38:   - 例外：Meta 升级"复活"可在每局恢复 1 次（HP 恢复至 30%，原地复活，3 秒无敌）
39: - 死亡后展示本局统计数据（存活时间、击杀数、获得金币等）
40: - 获得的 Meta 货币保留，用于永久升级
41: 
42: ---
43: 
44: ### 1.2 武器与技能系统
45: 
46: #### FR-W01: 武器机制
47: - 武器自动攻击，无需玩家手动操作
48: - 每个武器有独立的攻击间隔、伤害、攻击范围、弹道模式
49: - 武器可升级（最高 Lv.8），每级提升属性或解锁新效果
50: - 同时最多装备 6 个武器
51: 
52: #### FR-W02: 武器类型（初始至少实现以下类型）
53: | 武器 | 弹道类型 | 说明 |
54: |------|----------|------|
55: | 魔法飞弹 | 追踪弹 | 自动追踪最近敌人 |
56: | 圣光环 | 环绕 | 围绕玩家旋转的光环 |
57: | 火焰喷射 | 锥形AOE | 朝玩家面朝方向喷射 |
58: | 闪电链 | 链式 | 命中后弹射至附近敌人 |
59: | 冰霜新星 | 圆形AOE | 以玩家为中心的冰冻爆发 |
60: | 飞刀 | 直线弹幕 | 高速直线投射物 |
61: 
62: #### FR-W03: 被动技能
63: - 被动技能提供永久属性加成或特殊效果
64: - 初始最多装备 6 个被动技能，通过章节进度逐步解锁至 12 槽位
65:   - 第1章通关：解锁第 7-8 槽位
66:   - 第2章通关：解锁第 9-10 槽位
67:   - 第3章通关：解锁第 11-12 槽位
68: - 被动技能可升级（最高 Lv.5）
69: - 被动技能分为三类路线标签：`holy`（神圣系）、`void`（虚空系）、`neutral`（中立）
70: 
71: #### FR-W04: 武器进化
72: - 特定武器 + 特定被动技能满级后可进化为高级武器
73: - 进化武器拥有全新的攻击模式和大幅增强的属性
74: 
75: #### FR-W05: 饰品系统
76: - 饰品为独立装备类型，与武器和被动技能分开管理
77: - 最多同时装备 2 件饰品
78: - 饰品仅通过 Boss 击杀、宝藏房间、特殊事件获取（不可通过升级选择获得）
79: - 饰品提供独特机制效果（非数值加成），无法升级
80: 
81: ---
82: 
83: ### 1.3 敌人系统
84: 
85: #### FR-E01: 敌人生成
86: - 敌人从房间预设刷新点或边缘生成，朝玩家方向移动
87: - 生成频率和敌人强度由双因子驱动：**楼层编号**（基础难度）+ **房间内战斗时间**（递增压力）
88:   - 进入战斗房间开始计时，清除所有敌人或离开房间时停止
89:   - 安全营地、商店房间、事件房间不计时
90: - 支持波次系统：每隔固定时间触发精英波次
91: 
92: #### FR-E02: 敌人类型
93: | 类型 | 行为 | 说明 |
94: |------|------|------|
95: | 普通 | 直线追踪 | 基础敌人，缓慢移动 |
96: | 快速 | 快速追踪 | 高速低血量 |
97: | 坦克 | 缓慢追踪 | 高血量高伤害 |
98: | 远程 | 保持距离+射击 | 远程攻击型 |
99: | 精英 | 追踪+特殊技能 | 带有特殊能力的强化敌人 |
100: | Boss | 复杂AI | 阶段性Boss，多种攻击模式 |
101: 
102: #### FR-E03: 敌人掉落
103: - 所有敌人死亡后掉落经验宝石
104: - 按概率掉落：金币、回复道具、宝箱、磁铁（吸取所有掉落物）
105: - 精英/Boss 掉落高品质物品和更多经验
106: 
107: ---
108: 
109: ### 1.4 升级与进度系统
110: 
111: #### FR-L01: 经验与升级
112: - 拾取经验宝石获得经验值
113: - 升级所需经验随等级递增（公式：`base_xp * level ^ 1.3`）
114: - 升级时暂停游戏，弹出技能选择界面
115: 
116: #### FR-L02: 升级选择
117: - 每次升级随机提供 3 个选项（受幸运值影响品质）
118: - 选项包括：新武器、武器升级、新被动、被动升级
119: - 已满级的武器/被动不再出现
120: - 支持重新随机（消耗金币，每局限定次数）
121: 
122: #### FR-L03: Meta 进度（永久升级）
123: - 每局游戏结束获得 Meta 货币（基于表现）
124: - Meta 升级树提供永久属性加成
125: - 解锁新角色、新武器、新被动技能
126: - Meta 进度存储在本地存档中
127: 
128: #### FR-L04: 矿石收集与锻造
129: - 特定楼层（如第2章锻炉层）可获取矿石材料
130: - 矿石用于在安全营地的锻造站强化当前武器
131: - 锻造消耗：3 矿石 → 武器伤害 +10%，5 矿石 → 武器附加元素效果
132: - 矿石为当局资源，不跨局保留
133: 
134: ---
135: 
136: ### 1.5 Roguelike 地图系统
137: 
138: #### FR-R01: 程序化地图生成
139: - 使用 BSP / Wave Function Collapse 算法生成随机地图
140: - 地图由多个房间（Room）和走廊（Corridor）组成
141: - 每个房间有不同的地形和敌人配置
142: 
143: #### FR-R02: 地图结构
144: - 每局游戏包含多个楼层（Floor），难度递增
145: - 每个楼层包含：
146:   - 起始房间（安全区）
147:   - 普通战斗房间（3-5个）
148:   - 精英房间（1-2个）
149:   - 商店房间（1个）
150:   - 宝藏房间（0-1个，随机出现）
151:   - Boss 房间（1个，通往下一层的入口）
152: 
153: #### FR-R03: 房间事件
154: - 进入房间触发战斗，清除所有敌人后解锁出口
155: - 商店房间：使用金币购买武器/被动/回复道具
156: - 宝藏房间：解谜或挑战后获得稀有奖励
157: - 随机事件房间：触发随机事件（祝福/诅咒/NPC交互）
158: 
159: #### FR-R04: 小地图
160: - HUD 显示当前楼层的小地图
161: - 已探索房间显示图标（战斗/商店/Boss等）
162: - 未探索房间显示为灰色问号
163: 
164: #### FR-R05: 环境危害系统
165: - 每个楼层拥有独特的环境主题和对应的环境危害
166: - 环境危害类型包括：水流推移、孢子毒云、熔岩地形、冰面滑行、虚空腐蚀等
167: - 环境危害同时影响玩家和敌人（部分敌人可免疫对应楼层的环境效果）
168: - 环境交互支持组合效果（如：冰面 + 火焰 = 融化产生水面）
169: 
170: #### FR-R06: 楼层主题
171: - 每章楼层拥有统一视觉主题（地形瓦片、配色、光照、粒子效果）
172: - 第1章（堕落起始）：灰绿色调、苔藓石墙、昏暗火把
173: - 第2章（炼狱试炼）：红橙色调、熔岩、工业金属
174: - 第3章（寒霜深渊）：冰蓝色调、冰晶、极光
175: - 终章（虚空圣殿）：紫黑色调、虚空裂隙、几何结构
176: 
177: #### FR-R07: 安全营地
178: - 每章通关后进入安全营地（非战斗区域）
179: - 营地功能：NPC 对话、商店购物、记忆碎片阅读、锻造站（特定章节）
180: - 营地不计入游戏计时，玩家可自由探索后选择进入下一章
181: 
182: #### FR-R08: 可破坏物与交互物
183: - 房间内包含可破坏物体（木桶、水晶、蘑菇等），破坏后掉落金币/回复物
184: - 特定房间包含交互物体（机关、传送门、NPC）
185: - 可破坏物与环境主题匹配
186: 
187: ---
188: 
189: ### 1.7 叙事系统
190: 
191: #### FR-N01: 章节转场叙事
192: - 每章开始和结束时播放叙事转场画面
193: - 叙事包含：旁白文字、角色对话、场景描写
194: - 玩家可通过按键加速或跳过叙事
195: 
196: #### FR-N02: 分支选择
197: - 章节转场中提供关键选择点（2-3 个选项）
198: - 选择影响后续剧情走向和可获取的奖励
199: - 选择记录存入 RunData，影响路线亲和度计算
200: 
201: #### FR-N03: 双路线系统（救赎 / 堕落）
202: - 玩家行为和选择积累路线亲和度（`alignment` 值，范围 -100 ~ +100）
203:   - 正值倾向救赎路线，负值倾向堕落路线
204: - 影响亲和度的因素：
205:   - 升级时选择神圣系被动（+亲和度）或虚空系被动（-亲和度）
206:   - 叙事分支选择
207:   - 特定事件房间的决策
208: - 亲和度影响：最终结局、部分 NPC 对话、隐藏层解锁条件
209: 
210: #### FR-N04: 记忆碎片
211: - 记忆碎片散布在宝藏房间、隐藏区域和 Boss 掉落中
212: - 收集的碎片可在安全营地阅读，揭示世界观和角色背景
213: - 碎片分为 4 类：世界史、角色记忆、堕落真相、救赎之路
214: - 总计 33 个碎片，收集进度记录在 RunData 中
215: 
216: #### FR-N05: 三结局系统
217: - 根据路线亲和度和关键选择，游戏提供三种结局：
218:   - **救赎结局**：亲和度 ≥ 50 且完成救赎路线关键选择
219:   - **堕落结局**：亲和度 ≤ -50 且完成堕落路线关键选择
220:   - **平衡结局**：亲和度在 -49 ~ +49 之间，或未满足上述条件
221: 
222: #### FR-N06: 事件分支权重与门禁
223: - 事件房叙事选择采用加权路由，不仅基于随机
224: - 加权因子至少包含：当前 alignment 区间、已解锁结局、近期事件历史（避免重复）
225: - 支持事件门禁字段：`requires_endings_any` 与 `forbid_endings_any`
226: 
227: #### FR-N07: 章节持续效果
228: - 事件选择可附加 `chapter_effect`，持续 2~3 个房间
229: - 章节效果可影响：刷怪速率、敌人 HP、敌人伤害、环境危害强度、玩家移速、伤害加成、临时护甲
230: - HUD 与房间状态必须显示效果名称、正负向、剩余房间数
231: 
232: #### FR-N08: 结局后记与叙事回顾
233: - 结算界面需显示结局后记文本（首次解锁版与重复轮回版）
234: - 结算界面需展示本局叙事选择时间线摘要（上限与溢出提示）
235: - 主菜单支持记忆碎片回看轮播（标题 + 正文）
236: 
237: ---
238: 
239: ### 1.6 UI 系统
240: 
241: #### FR-U01: 主菜单
242: - 开始游戏（角色选择 → 进入游戏）
243: - Meta 升级（永久升级树）
244: - 图鉴（已解锁的武器/被动/敌人/角色）
245: - 设置（音量、画面、按键绑定）
246: - 退出
247: 
248: #### FR-U02: 游戏内 HUD
249: - 生命值条、耐力条
250: - 经验值条 + 当前等级
251: - 已装备武器图标（显示等级）
252: - 已装备被动图标（显示等级）
253: - 已装备饰品图标
254: - 游戏计时器（当前房间战斗时间）
255: - 击杀计数
256: - 金币数量
257: - 矿石数量（仅在含矿石的楼层显示）
258: - 环境仪表（冻伤/虚空腐蚀，仅在对应楼层显示）
259: - 路线亲和度指示器（简化图标，不显示数值）
260: - 小地图
261: 
262: #### FR-U03: 升级选择界面
263: - 暂停游戏
264: - 展示 3 个选项卡片（图标 + 名称 + 描述 + 等级）
265: - 支持键盘/鼠标选择
266: - 重新随机按钮（显示剩余次数）
267: 
268: #### FR-U04: 暂停菜单
269: - ESC 暂停游戏
270: - 显示当前属性面板
271: - 继续 / 设置 / 放弃本局
272: - 暂停菜单需支持“回主菜单（不结算）”操作
273: - 暂停菜单设置子页支持运行时调节并即时生效：
274:   - Master / BGM / SFX / Ambience 音量
275:   - 屏幕震动强度
276:   - UI 缩放（80%~150%）
277: - 设置变更需持久化到存档，并在下一次启动自动恢复
278: 
279: #### FR-U05: 结算界面
280: - 存活时间、击杀数、获得经验、获得金币
281: - 获得的 Meta 货币
282: - 解锁成就提示
283: - 返回主菜单
284: 
285: #### FR-U06: 局内反馈增强
286: - HUD 需支持事件吐司通知（成就/结局/记忆碎片/饰品）
287: - HUD 需提供 3x5 迷你地图（15 房），显示：房间编号、房型、当前房间高亮、已完成状态
288: - HUD 章节效果条需显示图标化正负向（`[+]` / `[-]` / `[~]`）与剩余房间计数
289: 
290: ---
291: 
292: ## 2. 非功能需求
293: 
294: ### 2.1 性能要求
295: 
296: | 指标 | 目标值 |
297: |------|--------|
298: | 帧率 | ≥ 55 FPS（500 敌人同屏场景下） |
299: | 同屏敌人数 | ≥ 500 |
300: | 同屏弹幕数 | ≥ 200 |
301: | 内存占用 | ≤ 512 MB |
302: | 启动时间 | ≤ 3 秒 |
303: | 存档加载 | ≤ 1 秒 |
304: | 场景切换 | ≤ 0.5 秒（含过渡动画） |
305: 
306: ### 2.2 可维护性
307: - 武器/敌人/被动技能通过 Resource 配置文件定义，支持热加载
308: - 数值平衡通过外部 JSON/CSV 配置表驱动
309: - 模块间低耦合，使用信号（Signal）通信
310: 
311: ### 2.3 可扩展性
312: - 支持通过 Mod 系统添加新武器/敌人/角色
313: - 地图生成算法可插拔替换
314: - 预留多人联机接口（未来版本）
315: 
316: ### 2.4 存档系统
317: - 自动保存 Meta 进度
318: - 单局游戏不支持中途存档（Roguelike 设计）
319: - 存档数据加密防篡改
320: - 存档包含运行时设置（音量/震动/UI缩放）并支持实时落盘
321: 
322: ### 2.5 本地化
323: - 支持中文（简体）和英文
324: - 所有文本通过 i18n 键值对管理
325: - UI 布局适配不同语言文本长度
326: 
327: ### 2.6 无障碍
328: - 支持完全键盘操作
329: - 支持手柄输入（Xbox / PlayStation 布局）
330: - 支持输入重映射（键盘和手柄均可自定义按键）
331: - 色盲模式（三种类型：红绿色盲 / 蓝黄色盲 / 全色盲，通过替换配色方案实现）
332: - UI 字体大小可调（小 / 中 / 大，默认中）
333: - UI 缩放支持（80% ~ 150%）
334: - 叙事文本支持字幕样式显示（底部半透明背景条 + 白色文字）
```

```
2746:     for row_variant: Variant in weighted_rows:

2757:             continue

2801:         if not pickup.picked.is_connected(callback):
2802:             pickup.picked.connect(callback)
2803: 
2804:     if pickup.get_parent() == null:
2805:         _pickups_root.add_child(pickup)
2806: 
2807:

2811:             return {"type": "xp", "amount": 5}
2812:         "xp_gem_medium":
2813:             return {"type": "xp", "amount": 12}
```

```
91:     _combat_mode = "normal"
92:     _boss_spawned = false
93:     _boss_id = ""
94:     _boss_style_profile = {}
95: 
96: 
97: func get_room_time() -> float:
98:     return _room_time
99: 
100: 
101: func get_alive_count() -> int:
102:     var total: int = 0
103:     for node: Node in get_tree().get_nodes_in_group("enemy"):
104:         if node == null or not is_instance_valid(node):
105:             continue
106:         if ObjectPool != null and node.get_parent() == ObjectPool:
107:             continue
108:         if node.has_method("is_pool_active") and not bool(node.is_pool_active()):
109:             continue
110:         total += 1
111:     return total
112: 
113: 
114: func set_runtime_modifiers(spawn_rate_mult: float, enemy_hp_mult: float, enemy_damage_mult: float) -> void:
115:     _runtime_spawn_rate_mult = clampf(spawn_rate_mult, 0.55, 1.8)
116:     _runtime_enemy_hp_mult = clampf(enemy_hp_mult, 0.55, 1.8)
117:     _runtime_enemy_damage_mult = clampf(enemy_damage_mult, 0.55, 1.8)
118: 
119: 
120: func _spawn_enemy() -> void:
121:     if enemy_scene == null:
122:         return
123:     var alive_limit: int = max_alive
124:     if _combat_mode == "elite":
125:         alive_limit = mini(max_alive, maxi(6, int(round(float(max_alive) * 0.55))))
126: 
127:     if get_alive_count() >= alive_limit:
128:         return
129: 
130:     var enemy: CharacterBody2D = _acquire_enemy_instance()
131:     if enemy == null:
132:         return
133: 
134:     var archetype: String = _pick_enemy_archetype()
135:     var is_elite_wave: bool = _combat_mode == "elite" or (_elite_wave_interval > 0 and _spawn_count > 0 and _spawn_count % _elite_wave_interval == 0)
136:     var chapter_id: String = _get_chapter_id_for_floor(floor_index)
137:     var enemy_id: String = _build_enemy_id(archetype, is_elite_wave, chapter_id)
138:     var profile: Dictionary = _build_archetype_profile(archetype, is_elite_wave)
139:     var tier: String = str(profile.get("tier", "normal"))
140:     enemy.enemy_id = enemy_id
141: 
142:     var player: Node2D = get_tree().get_first_node_in_group("player") as Node2D
143:     var center: Vector2 = global_position
144:     if player != null:
145:         center = player.global_position
146: 
147:     var angle: float = randf() * TAU
148:     var distance: float = randf_range(320.0, 460.0)
149:     enemy.global_position = center + Vector2.RIGHT.rotated(angle) * distance
150: 
151:     var pressure: Dictionary = _get_room_pressure_values()
152:     var floor_mult: float = _get_floor_multiplier()
153:     var hp_mult: float = floor_mult * float(pressure.get("hp_mult", 1.0)) * _runtime_enemy_hp_mult * float(profile.get("hp_mult", 1.0))
154:     var damage_mult: float = floor_mult * float(pressure.get("damage_mult", 1.0)) * _runtime_enemy_damage_mult * float(profile.get("damage_mult", 1.0))
155:     var speed_mult: float = float(profile.get("speed_mult", 1.0))
156:     var attack_interval_mult: float = float(profile.get("attack_interval_mult", 1.0))
157: 
158:     var health_component: Node = enemy.get_node_or_null("HealthComponent")
159:     if health_component != null and health_component.get("max_hp") != null:
160:         health_component.max_hp *= hp_mult
161:         health_component.current_hp = health_component.max_hp
162: 
163:     if enemy.get("touch_damage") != null:
164:         enemy.touch_damage *= damage_mult
165:     if enemy.get("move_speed") != null:
166:         enemy.move_speed *= speed_mult
167:     if enemy.get("attack_interval") != null:
168:         enemy.attack_interval = maxf(0.2, float(enemy.attack_interval) * attack_interval_mult)
169: 
170:     if enemy.has_method("apply_spawn_profile"):
171:         enemy.apply_spawn_profile({
172:             "tier": tier,
173:             "archetype": archetype,
174:             "enemy_id": enemy_id,
175:             "base_color": profile.get("base_color", Color(0.83, 0.37, 0.37, 1.0)),
176:             "scale": profile.get("scale", Vector2.ONE),
177:             "ranged": bool(profile.get("ranged", false)),
178:             "preferred_range": float(profile.get("preferred_range", 170.0)),
179:             "ranged_attack_range": float(profile.get("ranged_attack_range", 255.0)),
180:             "ranged_attack_interval": float(profile.get("ranged_attack_interval", 1.25)),
181:             "ranged_damage_mult": float(profile.get("ranged_damage_mult", 0.8))
182:         })
183: 
184:     _spawn_count += 1
185: 
186: 
187: func _spawn_boss() -> bool:
188:     if enemy_scene == null:
189:         return false
190:     if get_alive_count() > 0:
191:         return true
192: 
193:     var boss: CharacterBody2D = _acquire_enemy_instance()
194:     if boss == null:
195:         return false
196: 
197:     var boss_name: String = _boss_id
198:     if boss_name == "":
199:         boss_name = "boss_unknown"
200:     if boss.get("enemy_id") != null:
201:         boss.enemy_id = boss_name
202: 
203:     var player: Node2D = get_tree().get_first_node_in_group("player") as Node2D
204:     if player != null:
205:         boss.global_position = player.global_position + Vector2(randf_range(-220.0, 220.0), -260.0)
206:     else:
207:         boss.global_position = global_position
208: 
209:     var health_mult: float = (10.0 + float(floor_index) * 1.7) * _runtime_enemy_hp_mult
210:     var damage_mult: float = (1.8 + float(floor_index) * 0.08) * _runtime_enemy_damage_mult
211:     var speed_mult: float = 1.0
212:     var scale_mult: float = 1.0
213:     var boss_color: Color = Color(0.95, 0.45, 0.2, 1.0)
214: 
215:     if not _boss_style_profile.is_empty():
216:         health_mult *= clampf(float(_boss_style_profile.get("hp_mult", 1.0)), 0.7, 1.4)
217:         damage_mult *= clampf(float(_boss_style_profile.get("damage_mult", 1.0)), 0.7, 1.5)
218:         speed_mult = clampf(float(_boss_style_profile.get("speed_mult", 1.0)), 0.7, 1.5)
219:         scale_mult = clampf(float(_boss_style_profile.get("scale_mult", 1.0)), 0.85, 1.25)
220:         boss_color = Color.from_string(str(_boss_style_profile.get("color", "#f2733a")), boss_color)
221: 
222:     var health_component: Node = boss.get_node_or_null("HealthComponent")
223:     if health_component != null and health_component.get("max_hp") != null:
224:         health_component.max_hp *= health_mult
225:         health_component.current_hp = health_component.max_hp
226: 
227:     if boss.get("touch_damage") != null:
228:         boss.touch_damage *= damage_mult
229:     if boss.get("move_speed") != null:
230:         boss.move_speed *= 0.76 * speed_mult
231: 
232:     var visual: Polygon2D = boss.get_node_or_null("Polygon2D") as Polygon2D
233:     if visual != null:
234:         visual.color = boss_color
235:     boss.scale = Vector2(1.9, 1.9) * scale_mult
236:     if boss.has_method("set_visual_scale_base"):
237:         boss.set_visual_scale_base(boss.scale)
238:     if boss.has_method("apply_spawn_profile"):
239:         boss.apply_spawn_profile({
240:             "tier": "boss",
241:             "archetype": "boss",
242:             "enemy_id": boss_name,
243:             "base_color": boss_color,
244:             "scale": boss.scale
245:         })
246:     return true
247: 
248: 
249: func _pick_enemy_archetype() -> String:
250:     var total: float = 0.0
251:     for value: Variant in _enemy_type_weights.values():
252:         total += maxf(0.0, float(value))
253:     if total <= 0.0:
254:         return "normal"
255: 
256:     var roll: float = randf() * total
257:     var cumulative: float = 0.0
258:     for key: Variant in _enemy_type_weights.keys():
259:         var weight: float = maxf(0.0, float(_enemy_type_weights.get(key, 0.0)))
260:         cumulative += weight
261:         if roll <= cumulative:
262:             return str(key)
263:     return "normal"
264: 
265: 
266: func _build_enemy_id(archetype: String, is_elite: bool, chapter_id: String) -> String:
267:     var chapter_row_var: Variant = _chapter_archetype_map.get(chapter_id, _chapter_archetype_map.get("chapter_1", {}))
268:     var chapter_row: Dictionary = {}
269:     if chapter_row_var is Dictionary:
270:         chapter_row = chapter_row_var
271:     var base_name: String = str(chapter_row.get(archetype, chapter_row.get("normal", "enemy_shadowling")))
272:     if base_name == "":
273:         base_name = "enemy_shadowling"
274:     if is_elite:
275:         return "elite_%s" % base_name.trim_prefix("enemy_")
276:     return base_name
277: 
278:

328:         var base_scale: Vector2 = profile.get("scale", Vector2.ONE)
329:         profile["scale"] = base_scale * 1.25
330:

333: 
334: func _load_spawn_profile_config() -> void:
335:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
336: 
337:     var interval: int = int(scaling.get("elite_wave_interval", 8))
338:     _elite_wave_interval = maxi(3, interval)
339: 
340:     var config_weights_var: Variant = scaling.get("enemy_type_weights", {})
341:     var config_weights: Dictionary = {}
342:     if config_weights_var is Dictionary:
343:         config_weights = config_weights_var
344: 
345:     var required_types: Array[String] = ["normal", "fast", "tank", "ranged"]
346:     for enemy_type: String in required_types:
347:         var raw_weight: float = float(config_weights.get(enemy_type, _enemy_type_weights.get(enemy_type, 0.0)))
348:         _enemy_type_weights[enemy_type] = maxf(0.0, raw_weight)
349: 
350:     var chapter_map_var: Variant = scaling.get("chapter_archetype_map", {})
351:     if chapter_map_var is Dictionary:
352:         for chapter_id: String in ["chapter_1", "chapter_2", "chapter_3", "chapter_4"]:
353:             var chapter_row_var: Variant = (chapter_map_var as Dictionary).get(chapter_id, {})
354:             if not (chapter_row_var is Dictionary):
355:                 continue
356:             var chapter_row: Dictionary = chapter_row_var
357:             if not _chapter_archetype_map.has(chapter_id):
358:                 _chapter_archetype_map[chapter_id] = {}
359:             var target_row: Dictionary = _chapter_archetype_map[chapter_id]
360:             for enemy_type: String in required_types:
361:                 var enemy_id: String = str(chapter_row.get(enemy_type, target_row.get(enemy_type, "enemy_shadowling"))).strip_edges()
362:                 if enemy_id != "":
363:                     target_row[enemy_type] = enemy_id
364: 
365: 
366: func _get_chapter_id_for_floor(target_floor: int) -> String:
367:     var safe_floor: int = maxi(1, target_floor)
368:     if safe_floor <= 4:
369:         return "chapter_1"
370:     if safe_floor <= 8:
371:         return "chapter_2"
372:     if safe_floor <= 12:
373:         return "chapter_3"
374:     return "chapter_4"
375: 
376: 
377: func _acquire_enemy_instance() -> CharacterBody2D:
378:     var enemy: CharacterBody2D
379:     if ObjectPool != null:
380:         enemy = ObjectPool.acquire("enemy_basic", self) as CharacterBody2D
381:     if enemy == null and enemy_scene != null:
382:         enemy = enemy_scene.instantiate() as CharacterBody2D
383:         if enemy != null:
384:             add_child(enemy)
385:     return enemy
386: 
387: 
388: func _get_spawn_interval() -> float:
389:     var floor_ratio: float = 1.0 + float(floor_index - 1) * 0.09
390:     var time_ratio: float = 1.0
391:     if _room_time > 120.0:
392:         time_ratio = 1.8
393:     elif _room_time > 60.0:
394:         time_ratio = 1.5
395:     elif _room_time > 30.0:
396:         time_ratio = 1.25
397: 
398:     var interval: float = 1.3 / (floor_ratio * time_ratio * _runtime_spawn_rate_mult)
399:     if _combat_mode == "elite":
400:         interval *= 1.18
401:     return clampf(interval, 0.2, 1.3)
402: 
403: 
404: func _get_floor_multiplier() -> float:
405:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
406:     var multipliers: Dictionary = scaling.get("floor_multipliers", {})
407:     return float(multipliers.get(str(floor_index), 1.0))
408: 
409: 
410: func _get_room_pressure_values() -> Dictionary:
411:     var scaling: Dictionary = ConfigManager.get_config("enemy_scaling", {})
412:     var brackets: Array = scaling.get("room_time_brackets", [])
413:     for item: Variant in brackets:
414:         if not (item is Dictionary):
415:             continue
416:         var row: Dictionary = item
417:         if _room_time <= float(row.get("max_seconds", 9999.0)):
418:             return row
419:     return {"hp_mult": 1.0, "damage_mult": 1.0}
```

```
304:         _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json base_room_weights must be non-empty object")
305:     else:
306:         total = 0.0
307:         for key in required_weight_keys:
308:             weight = _to_float(base_weights.get(key))
309:             if weight is None or weight < 0:
310:                 _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json base_room_weights.{key} must be >= 0")
311:             else:
312:                 total += weight
313:         if total <= 0:
314:             _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json base_room_weights total must be > 0")
315: 
316:     if not isinstance(chapter_mult, dict):
317:         _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json chapter_room_weight_mult must be object")
318:     else:
319:         for chapter_id in chapter_order:
320:             row = chapter_mult.get(chapter_id)
321:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
322:                 _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json chapter_room_weight_mult missing '{chapter_id}'")
323:                 continue
324:             for key in required_weight_keys:
325:                 value = _to_float(row.get(key))
326:                 if value is None or value < 0.0 or value > 3.0:
327:                     _add_error(errors, f"map_generation.json chapter_room_weight_mult.{chapter_id}.{key} must be within [0, 3]")
328: 
329:     if constraints is not None:
330:         if not isinstance(constraints, dict):
331:             _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints must be object")
332:         else:
333:             max_consecutive = constraints.get("max_consecutive_same_type")
334:             max_treasure_per_chapter = constraints.get("max_treasure_per_chapter")
335:             max_room_type_per_chapter = constraints.get("max_room_type_per_chapter")
336:             min_room_type_per_chapter = constraints.get("min_room_type_per_chapter")
337:             if not isinstance(max_consecutive, int) or max_consecutive < 1 or max_consecutive > 5:
338:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_consecutive_same_type must be int within [1, 5]")
339:             if not isinstance(max_treasure_per_chapter, int) or max_treasure_per_chapter < 0 or max_treasure_per_chapter > 5:
340:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_treasure_per_chapter must be int within [0, 5]")
341: 
342:             required_cap_keys = ("event", "shop", "elite", "treasure")
343:             if not isinstance(max_room_type_per_chapter, dict) or not max_room_type_per_chapter:
344:                 _add_error(errors, "map_generation.json constraints.max_room_type_per_chapter must be non-empty object")
345:             else:
346:                 for key in required_cap_keys:
347:                     value = max_room_type_per_chapter.get(key)

352:                     treasure_cap = max_room_type_per_chapter.get("treasure")
353:                     if isinstance(treasure_cap, int) and treasure_cap != max_treasure_per_chapter:

367:                         if isinstance(value, int) and isinstance(max_value, int) and value > max_value:

380: def _validate_enemy_scaling(data: dict[str, Any], errors: list[str]) -> None:
381:     brackets = data.get("room_time_brackets")
382:     multipliers = data.get("floor_multipliers")
383:     elite_wave_interval = data.get("elite_wave_interval")
384:     type_weights = data.get("enemy_type_weights")
385:     chapter_map = data.get("chapter_archetype_map")
386:     if not isinstance(brackets, list) or not brackets:
387:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be a non-empty array")
388:     else:
389:         last_max = -1.0
390:         for i, row in enumerate(brackets):
391:             if not isinstance(row, dict):
392:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}] must be object")
393:                 continue
394:             max_seconds = row.get("max_seconds")
395:             hp_mult = row.get("hp_mult")
396:             dmg_mult = row.get("damage_mult")
397:             max_seconds_f = _to_float(max_seconds)
398:             if max_seconds_f is None:
399:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
400:             elif max_seconds_f <= 0:
401:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].max_seconds must be > 0")
402:             elif max_seconds_f <= last_max:
403:                 _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json room_time_brackets must be strictly increasing")
404:             else:
405:                 last_max = max_seconds_f
406: 
407:             hp_mult_f = _to_float(hp_mult)
408:             if hp_mult_f is None:
409:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
410:             elif hp_mult_f <= 0:
411:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].hp_mult must be > 0")
412: 
413:             dmg_mult_f = _to_float(dmg_mult)
414:             if dmg_mult_f is None:
415:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
416:             elif dmg_mult_f <= 0:
417:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json bracket[{i}].damage_mult must be > 0")
418: 
419:     if not isinstance(multipliers, dict):
420:         _add_error(errors, "enemy_scaling.json floor_multipliers must be an object")
421:     else:
422:         for floor in range(1, 16):
423:             key = str(floor)

426:                 continue
427:             value = multipliers[key]

431:             elif value_f <= 0:
432:                 _add_error(errors, f"enemy_scaling.json floor {floor} multiplier must be > 0")
```
